Hadien ba nga la ngam la kyrthom ha ki lynter ki pynkiang jong ka laiphew snem kynthih, nga sa lap 1 a u ksai nangno ba nga dei ban sdang. Lehse ka long ka bok, ka rwiang , ka nusib jong ka jaitbynriew ba nga 1 a kynduh ia U Rangbah B. Wollington, uba la ih bha ki jingmut jingpyrkhat bad uba la lum la lang la biang la ki jingtip jong baroh kane ka thaih ha ka por kaba biang. Une u rangbah, hadien ba ula pule ia ki katto katne ki jingthoh jong nga, ula pynpaw ia ka dohnud kaba kmen ban Varap 1 a nga ha kaba lum ia ki jingtip baroh jong kane ka thaih. Ha ki kyntien jong u ia kine ki jingshisha u pynpaw- "Masan, kaba lum ia kiei kiei kiba don hapoh kane ka ksing jingtip, nga kitram shirynieng ha kito ki Meidot-Padot jong kane ka thaih - kum U Shloin Duwakdar, U Jogidhon Roy Chyne, Duwakdar (Ki Duwakdar Saw-Seng na Shala); U Ksaniang na Mustoh uba la im tymmen sa ban kot 200 snem ka rta, U Along Sing, Headman U Sande Mustoh bad U President ba nyngkong ka Lai-seng, U Bising na Nongwar: Kiba ha khmat jong ki nga dang dei tang ban Yasong kwai bad thep duma. Nga la ju shong bad pynshah shkor dngong mynba ki tei ki radbah ki iathuhkhana shaphang kito ki por kiba la phet sha ri jingklet, bad lada kila shu shong syam mynthi khlem lathuh; lehse ka pateng kaba mynta bad kaba dang wan kin nym tip ei ei shuh shaphang k. sngi ba la leit; bad ngin shu shah padai ha ki leh batip jong ka juk mynta." "Kaba nga im jmgmut kliaw ban lum ban lang da kaba thoh ka long naduh ka snem 1923; namar dei naduh kane ka snem ba ka thain Ri War kala sdang ban ia lum-seng lum-dang kham khah-khah, khamtam eh ha kine ki saw shnong-Nongwar, Mustoh, Shala bad Lyngkien (Nongbah). Lyngba kine ki seng nga loh peit loh pule 1 a ki jingthoh U Rev. Ksan (Ksan Mastar) na u khun jong u U Snarai Natep kumno u ruid dak ia ka jinghiar pateng jong ki briew ha kane ka thain. Dei kane kaba la ktik jingmut ia nga ban buh jingthoh bad lum jingtip shaphang kiei kiei baroh kiba donkam jong kane ka thain khnang ba kan long ka jingkyrkhu 1 a ki longdien ki ban dang wan." "Hynrei la katta ruh ngam ong ba baroh kaba nga la lum ka long kaba janai; bad ngan da sngewnguh ia uno uno na ki rangbah uba dang lah shuh ban ai ka jingVatei ia kynpham halor kine ki jingtip kiba nga la lum khnang ba ka ri bad ka jaitbynriew kan Yoh ia kaei kaei kaba nylla tarn." "Masan," u ong, "Nga la jan kot sha ka 79 snem bad nga tip ba ki sngi jong nga kila jan; bad nga la Yai wad lyngba ki snem ia u briew u ban pyndonkam ia kine ki thup jingtip, hynrei ngam lap: bad ngam kwah ba ka jingtrei shitom jongnga kan hap ha ka kti jong ka khniang bad ka sarang. Haba nga Yohi ia phi ba phi wad sngur da ka dohnud ban tip shaphang kiei kiei kiba dei la ki jong; ka dohnud jong nga ka um bad ka shad kmen Ill ba lehse ba tang ha u khulom ba nep jong phi, ka lawei kan dang tip shaphang la ka thymmei; lym kumta ka thain jong ngi kan belerong." Kine ki kyntien ksiar kyntien rupa kila ngam jylliew ha ka sohpdung ka dohnud jong nga. Hato ngan long ma u Nongthoh ? Ka wan ka jingkylli. La katta ruh nga durut bad dem diap kum u masi lur ha ka lyngkha. Ha ka snem 1964 nga la ai kawei ka kot sha ka Reviewing Committee bad shi copy de ha uwei u Rangbah. Ka Reviewing Committee kala ai jingkynthoh ba ka kot jongnga kam don dor ha ka Literature (It has no literary value) bad ynda nga kylli pat ha utei u Rangbah la u la leh kumno bad ka kot jongnga, ka jubab ka long ba u la pynjah Va ka. Dei tad haduh ka snem 1980, ynda nga la Voh ia ka State Literary Award kaba nyngkong, ba ka bneng ka sa phngaih. Triang nga kut jingmut ban pyndep ia ka thong bad ban thoh lut la ki jingtip baroh kiba nga la lum shaphang la ka jong ka thain. Nga tip ba ka lynti ba nga dei ban laid ka long kaba eh bad ba jwat; hynrei ki symboh ksiar symboh rupa kiba u Rangbah Wollington ula pashat ha nga kin tyngshain kum ka sharak bad pynshai kdar ia ka ri bad ka jaitbynriew baroh kawei: ban tip kumno ki longshuwa ki seng riti ki sainhima. U Nongthoh Ka history kam ju klet i'alade. Ka syntuid kum ka Wahduid kaba dap ba shlei bad bym ju rngad da ki jingjia bad ki Khanatang lyngba ki thwei hamsaia ki por. Lyngba ki khriang jong ka, ka pathai la ki khubor tympang na kawei ka pateng sha kawei pat bad ka kdew lynti ia ki nonglum jingtip ban jam shaduh ka tyrpa jong ka jingshisha hi. Ba kumta, wat ki kpep jong ka mynnor kim lah shuh ban shu shong kynjah bad buhrieh ia lade ha ki kynthem jong ki lngaid ki lwait. Ka pateng kaba dang wan kan khynra kan tihthai haduh ba kan da shem ia ka jingshisha kaba ka dohnud ka thrang. Napdeng ki Hima Khasi, ka Hima Sheila ka long kawei kaba la pawkhmat eh; wat la ka long ka Hima kaba dang mih ha ki khyndiat spah snem. Ka daw ka long ba na pneh jong ka kala pynmih ia ki rangkynih rangphawar bad ki khun dap tyrpeng kiba la pynphyrnai ia ka ri bad ka jaitbynriew. Ka daw ka long namar ba ka Hima Shelia kala long kaba nyngkong eh napdeng ki Hima Khasi ban ioh kjit la ka jingshai jong ka thoh ka pule. Ka por, namarkata, kala ih ba ka hima Sheila bad ki briew jong ka ki dei ban tip ia la ka mynnor. Ka jaitbynriew kaba khlem ka history ka long kaba lymbuit lymbiang, kaba khlem dur khlem dar bad kaba kopia ha asa. Ki riewpyrkhat ki orig ba ka jaitbynriew khlem ka thymmei ka history ka long ka jaitbynriew kaba khlem rijied. Ki thied ki thning jong ka kim ioh kjit jor tynrai bad ki khun jong ka ki tei paki dulan ha ka V asa. Thik kum ki ’tiew lyngksiar ba san halor ki maw, kiba tang shu shoh khyndiat ka sngi ki kohnguh khlieh bad samthiah lyngngeh namar ba ym don dewtrai ban kyrshan ia ki. Lyngba kane ka kot ngin pyrshang ban khura na kpep ka mynnor ia ki dak ksiar dak rupa ba la ruid ha ki mawlyngkniap jong ka: kumno ngi sdang bad nangno ngi wan. La ki khanatang khatar snem kynthih ki sabut bad mynjur ne cm bad ka jingsdang jong ka, ne, ngin shu bynshet lyngngeit bad mynjur lang bad ki Khanatang U Diengiei bad U Sohpetbneng. Ka jingwad ba sani kam ailad ia ngi ban shu shong lyngngeit hangne. Ka sei la ki nia ki jutang ban pynsabut jai pa jai; ba ngi kum ka jaitbynreiw ngi wan sha kane ka pyrthei kum kiwei pat ki para bynriew: bad kane ka ri ha kaba ngi im, ka long ka ri kaba u Ni u kong u la thied kyntang da ka dorbah ka snam. Naduh Rondi haduh Kupli bad naduh Lum Meikha haduh Rupatylli: kane ka dei ka n jingngi. La ngi pher ka ktien ka thylliej, ka nam ka beit, ka shnong ne ka Ilaka; ka jaitbynriew dei kawei. La tip pateng ha ka history kum ka ri ki Laiphew Syiem bad Khatar Daloi - “Ki ju ialeh thma ban sngap ruh sngewtriem” kiba ki dustur ki riti, ki sainpyrkhat synshar khadar, ki rukom ki phukom-fla, ha ka mane shine ne ka imlang ka sahlang), Ki aih ki kanun, ka pyrkhat ka pyrdain, ka sain hima sima ne ka trei ka ktah ki iapher bak lbak kawei ka Hima na kawei pat. Kaba la pynlong kumne ka long ym tang namar ki daw jong ka history hynrei namar ka jirtglor\g ka jaka bad ka mariang kiba la pynkylla dur ia ki: wat la ka jaitbynriew ka mih na ujuh u tnum u thyndai. VI Ka Hima Shela ka kynthup ia ki 9 shnong kiba don ym palat ia ki 1 5000 ngut ki nongshong shnong; kynthup lang ia kito baroh kiba don habar jong ka hima kiba dang bat ia lade ki trai shnong jong ka Sheila Confedaracy kat kum ki dustur ki riti tynrai jong ka hima, kiba dang i'oh hok i'oh bynta ha ki kam shnong kam thaw. Ka Hima Shelia wat la ka don la ki dustur ki riti kiba pher na baroh ki hima Khasi ryngkat ka rukom synshar khadar kaba ym don jingia parpain bad kiwei pat ki hima; pynban kam shym pyniapher ia lade na kiwei pat ki para khun Khasi Khara bad kim pdiang pat ba ki dei tang ki khun ki ksiew u 7 trep. Ki ngeit ba ia ka jaitbynriew Khasi Khara la pynlong da ki 16 trep 1 6 skum kiba U Blei Trai Kynrad u la mon sngewbha ban ai ha ki la kine ki lum ksiar lum paila ban long ka hok ka bynta bad ka jaka shong neh shong tynrai jong ki. Ki ngeit ruh ba ka jingseng jong ki la ka it ka hima ka long da ka hukum blei ba kin iar kin roi, kin koit kin khiah krad ryngkat ka khan ka kamai ban paw bynriew ha pyrthei. Ki don la ki khanatang bad ki puriskam nangno ki wan bad kumno ki sdang kiba ia pher na kiwei pat ki it ki hima. Ki ngeit ba ki wan sha kane ka pyrthei kumba long lem kiwei pat ki para bynriew kiba hap ban shah ia u slap ia ka Iyer, ia ka shit ia ka khriat bad ban iaidwir laid sakma kumba long lem ki para bynriew da kaba ngam ia ki khlaw ki btap bad ryngkang ia ki lum ki wah haduh ba kin da shem ka jaka kaba lait phar na ki jingma baroh. Dei kine ki jingiashem bad jingiatakhuh kiba la khun wandur ia ka pyrkhat pyrdaifl bad ka histoiyjong ki ban iohi pongshai sha lyndet ka bor jong kiwei pat ki hima Khasi ha kaba ki saihdur ia la ka imlang sahlang, ka synshar ka Vll khadar ban pynpaw ha ka pyrthei ba ki long kiba iohi jngai bad ba dap jingmut jingpyrkhat: kiba kiwei pat ki hima khasi ki dang ia sdang kynjoh khaskaifi sha katei ka pyrkhat. Ia ka Hima Sheila la bynshet halor ka sain pyrkhat synshar Duwakdar jong u Jin ha ka durbar wad nongsynshar bishar jong ki 23 shnong ha Shyrten ha ka snem 1662; hadien ka Sawthyndaw U Lum Baniang bad ka Phetmungor U Mir Jumla. Ki 23 shnong ki kynthup ia ka Shala , Mustoh, Nongwar, Nongbah, Nongtrai, Dewsaw, Tynger, Lyngkhom, Umtlang, Nonglyngkien, Mawrap, Rymnong, Tyma, Nongkroh, Mynteng, Ramdait, Nongriat, Synnei, Nongshluid, Sinai Mawshynrut, Nongsteng Umeit, Mawphu bad ka Thieddieng: kaba kylla long ka Hima ba khlaifi bor tarn ha ka phang shathie jong ka Ri Khasi. Hynrei ha ka snem 1724, ki 1 1 shnong hadien ba kim iahap jingmut ha ka jingthung dewanji ha ka jaka jong ki laingut ki Duwakdar bala iap - U Kynshe, U Stein bad u Bor, da kaba ki 12 shnong ki aidaw ba ym dei ban thung Duwakdar katba U Jerkha u dang don: kala pynpait phiaw ia ka Hima Sheila. Kine ki 1 1 shnong ki long - Ka Tyrna, Nongkroh, Ramdait, Mynteng, Nongriat, Synnei, Sinai Mawshynrut, Nongshluit (kiba sah kyrpang khlem i'asnoh bad kano kano ka hima tad haduh ka snem 1860; bad hadien nangta ki rung noh kum ki shnong sorkar hapoh jong ka Sorkar Bilat ba la pyniaid da ki Sirdar. Hynrei ki laishnong-Ka Nongsteng-Umeit, Mawphu bad Thieddieng, ki ia syllok noh bad U Basan Swer ryngkat U Buh Sing naduh ka snem 1727-28. Hadien ka jingiap jong U Laitlyngka Syiem Nongkhlaw ha ka snem 1731; uba la thmu ban klun ia ka Raij 1 2 shnong 1 2 blang: ki 3 shnong kila kyrshan tyngeh ia (J Basan Swer bad U Buh Sing ban pynieng ia ka Vlll Nongbah jong ki ha Weiser ha ka snem 1735. Dei tad hadien jong kaiVima Siat-U Dei bad ka Pom-Sohmen pyrshah a ki Ryngut, Laitiam bad Sohbar ba kitei ki 3 shnong ki pynbor ia U Basan Swer bad U Buh Sing ban kynriah jaka noh sha Sohra ha ka snem 1 785 da kaba ki ruh ki pyni'asnoh noh ia lade bad kane ka Hima. Hynrei namar ba kim don ka lew ka Hat khaii pateng kaba biang kim banse ban long ki buhai hat jong ka Hat Phali ki 1 2 shnong ka Hima Shelia. Hadien ba ki 1 1 shnong kila kynriah noh ia lade na ka Hima Sheila, Ka Hima Sheila ka sah tang 12 shnong- Ka Nongwar, Mustoh, Shala, Nongtrai, Nongbah, Tynger, Dewsaw, Lyngkhom, Umtlang, Mawrap, Nonglyngkien bad Rymnong. Sa shisien pat ka jmgor ka wan ha ka Hima Shelia ha ka snem 1870. Ki Nongbah, ki Mawrap bad ki Rymnong naduh ka por jong U Syiem Ganga Singh kila ju long kiba ia dei jingmut bha bad kiba la wanrah bun ki jingeh ia ka Hima Sheila, hynrei ki 9 shnong kim ailad satia. Ki Nongbah ynda ki la iohi ia ka jingmyntoi jong ka Hat Phali kila pyrshang ban dawa bynta na ka jingioh jong ka naduh ka snem 1 850 hynrei ka durbar Hima kam ailad satia. Ba kumta ha ka snem 1865 kitei baroh 3 shnong ki mih noh na ka Hima Shelia bad ki pyrshang ban ai Mokotduma ia ka Hima Sheila da kaba ki dawa ba namar ba ka Hat Phali ka don hapoh ka Hima Nongbah; ki ruh ki dei ban ioh bynta lem na ka khrong ka dan. Hynrei ki bor synshar ba halor jong ka Sorkar Bilat kim ailad satia bad ki da sneng pyrshah ia ki Nongbah ba kim bit ban thaw kulmar ne pynmih kano kano ka jihgja kajia ha Hat Phali. Hadien ka jingkhlad noh jong kitei ki lai shnong, ka Hima Sheila ka sah sa tang 9 shnong* Nongwar, Mustoh, Shala, IX Nongtrai, Tynger, Dewsaw, Lyngkhom, Umtlang bad Nonglynkien: ba la tip ia ka kum ka Sheila Confederacy. Kane ka Hima ka don hapdeng ka lhuh bah jong ka Ri War ha baroh arliang jong ka Bakra Shelia, kaba long naduh mynhyndai u budlum jong ka khaii pateng hapdeng ka Ri Khasi ba shathie bad ka Ri Thor Sylhet. Ki pud sawdong jong ka ki long: shatei la ker da ka Hima Nongkroh, Tyrna, Mynleng bad Mawrap; Mihngi da ka Hima Laitkynsew, Mawlong, bad Laiseng; Shathie da ka Ri thor Sylhet bad Sepngi da ka Hima Mawdon, Sinai Mawshynrut, Fhlang Synnei, Synnei bad Rymnong. Ka long ka jaka kaba seisoh bad ba tap da ki khlaw ki btap barben ha kaba ki ngap ki lwai , ki sim ki doh bad ki khriiang ki ksiah ba har rukom ki rwai bad kynud sngewtynnad ha ki sharing bad ranab lum jong ka . Ki syntiew ki skud ki phuh baroh saw samoi bad ki dieng ki siej, ki phlang ki kymbat ki jyrngam 12 bnai. Ka long ka ri jong u Knup-Mawiang. U Diengngai, U Tiewpathai khubor, U Tiewdohmaw bad ki spah hajar jait ki tiewdieng kiba niar eh ban shem haka pyrthei. Ka long ka Hima kaba pynmih bun eh u Mawshun ha ka por hyndai bad ka don ki par kiba kynrei kiba ym lah niewtang. Lehse ka lah ban pyndap mawshun ne dewbilat ia ka India baroh kawei lada la pyntrei ia ki. Ka long ka jaka ba jur slap bad ba sboh- ka ling jong u soh u pai, u kwai u tympew, ki har rukom ki jait soh bad ki musli musla kum u Sohmrit, ka sla tyrpat, u sying, u shynrai bad ki har rukom ki kynja kynbat dawai kiba niar ban shem ha kiwei pat ki bynta jong ka pyrthei. Ka ioh ka ai’om slap ba jrong eh naduh u May haduh u October, ka Synrai kaba lyngkot; ka Tlang kaba pyngngad (November, December bad January) bad ka Pyrem kaba syaid (February, March bad April). Ka Tlang ka long ka X aiom kaba sngewtynnad tam namar ka dei ka aiom ha kaba ki soh ki pai bad ki rep ki riang ki ih. Ka dei ka aiom kaba ki briew ki rusha kam ban lum ban lang ban kheit ban kit. Ki lyngkha ki risai ki dap da ki sur babang ba kynud na ka dohnud ba kmen ba phuhmat namar mynta ki loh ban kheit na ka umsyep bad na ka jingshoh jong u slap ka Iyer baroh shilyiur. Ka Sheila Confederary ka ioh slap na ki Iyer South East Monsoon kiba beh na ka Bay of Bengal naduh u April haduh u October. Namar ba ka shah ha ka lynti slap, kijaka kiba hapdeng 2000 bad 3500 ft ki ioh haduh 500 inches palat u slap; katba kito pat ki jaka kiba don hapdeng 400 bad 1500 ft ki ioh hapdeng 300 bad 400 inches u slap shisnem shisnem. Wat la u slap u jur ki briew ki long kiba koit ba khiah krad bad basmat basting. U slap u long ka jingkyrkhu ba ki lah ban trei ban ktah bad ban thung ban tep namar ki ioh la u slap khiah krad. Ki rashing ki ranab ki dap da ki kshaid ba rymphum bad ki wah ba kmen kiba mareh sted ban ia snoh bad ka Wah Bakra ban pyndap miar la ka baroh shilynter haduh ban da poi ha Wah Rupatylh. Kane ka dei ka aiom ha kaba ka Surma ka kop ia ka Brahma. Ka lymbub naphang lin bad nguid katba don bad pyndap ia ka ri thor Sylhet da ki um jong ka. Kane ruli ka dei ka por ha kaba ki nongjngi ba snah ki pynher la ki dieng tokta ban shalan sha ri thor. Namar ba ki wah ki dap ki shlei ha ka por Lyiur bad ba ki hat ki iew ki rit ki tyrkliong: ka ju long ka rukom ba ki briew ka Shelia Confederacy ba kin kynshew lypa ia u khaw u kba, ka dohkha ka dohpnat ban bam lyiur. Ka long ka por ban thaw kwar bad wad dohjei ia ki rangbah bad ka aiom thaw khoh thaw trap, thain shylliah thaih iarong ia ki kynthei. Namar kata, XI ka Hat Fhali ka long ka hat jingpyndap ia ki jmgdonkam baroh jong ka lyiur. Ka aiom ban sei ia ki khadki kha tyrkliong bala buh kynnai ha ki khra ban shoh kha-shyieng bad kylla jyntah ne ban kyllan muslah ia ki ksa-ksup na tynipan bad u jajew ban bam pura bam shngiam. Tang shu poi ka por Synrai ki leng ban (hiew ban mait bad ban khreh ka kheit ka et. Ki pynkhreh lypa la ki iarong ladep: ki khoh ki star, ki skong ki jingkieng , ki bnoh hami bad ki tint riam sim ba ka por tlang kumne kala poi. Te, ka Ri War ka shongshit ba ki lieng ki kiew bad ba ki nongbylla na satlak ki hiar ban mad lem ia ki jingkyrkhu ka n War bad ba km leit phai pat sha la ki shnong ki thaw, ki skum ki trep ynda ka puhktieh bad ka kylia stong kala poi. Ki nongkhaii na Maws yn ram- ‘Katba nangsait nangrbian 1 na Sohra bad na Laitkynsew, ki sieh la ki dukan ha tliana Hat Fhali ban lapeih la ka nusib bad ki leit phai sha la shnong da ka klimat kaba kmen bad ka dohnud kaba kyndeh ynda ka aiom Fhali kala wai ban nangpyniar ia la ka khan ka kamai bad ban ap kmang lano ka Lyiur kan wai bad ka Hat Fhali kan sdang. Ka Pyrem ka dei ka por shongthait: ka por nohjar bad ka por tyor: ka por jingsngewbha bad jmgdap kyrhai. Ki khlaw ki btap ki sawa da ki sur babang bad ki lynti hat lynti icw ki khapngiah da ki nongkit nongbah ban pynbiang ia ka lyiur. Ki miet ki shongshit da ki jingialeh theatre bad sawanka bad ki shnong ki thaw ki kingkyndeh da ki phur ki siang, ki bam khana bad ki jingiathoh shongkurim: namar ka dei ka atom ban pynpaw ia la ka jingkmen bad ban ainguh la la U Trai Nongthaw ba ula pynphong pynkup, pyndap pynbiang ia ki jingdonkam baroh jong ka met bad ka mynsiem. Baroh ki phuhmut phuhmat, ki kmen ki sngewbha bad ki ai la ka jingiaroh ia U Trai Nongthaw. Don jingdap dohnud nalor kane: Ki Rangsamla bad ki bohkhaila artdong ryngkat ki banat ba tabah ha tyrpeng, ki thei samla ryngkat ki pien thoh khyrwang bad ki jain-it dilein ryngkat ki ksiar shirynieng ba ki kit ia ki khoh rit syngkai bad ki bat la ki pla kyrsit ha kti ban kyntiap na kawei ka dukan sha kawei pat ban wad la ki jingdonkam: ki pyndap shorn ia ka dohnud. Hato kato ka aiom kan sdang wanphai? Ka jingphiah ia ka India bad ka Pakistan ha ka snem 1947 kala pynlip phiaw ia u sharak sharyngkuid ka ri War bad ki sngi jong ka jingsuk baroh ki her pustai sha lyndet jong ka ngen. Ka Hat Phali ka kynjah jar bad ka Nongbah ka kylla long ka jaka shong jong ki khhiang ki puit bad ki niangkynjah. Mano ban kyllie biang ia ka Hat Phali ? Ngi buh ka jingkylli. Ka mynsiem trei lang ryngkat ka romsnge kila duh kila prem bad ki lyngkha ki risai ki tap da ki riphuji bad ki shiah maileh. Ka bneng kaba stem da u soh u pai la synshar da ki lawbah lawsan. Ka ri kaba pynmih na trai diengsoh diengkwai ia ki radbah bad ki prohjabieng kum ki paia jong ka ri: mynta na ei pat yn pynmih - na trai mawrymsong bad narud ki pajwa I To ai ba ka main u longshuwa kan phngain kan phyrnai sa shisien pat, ba sa shisien kin win ki khlaw bad kin khih ki maw. Lynnong I Ki Sheila kumba paw ha ki Khanatang Shuwa ban ngam sha ki lynter ki pyngkiang jong ka history ka Hima Sheila, nyngkong eh ngi dei ban tip nangno ki wan bad ki dei kiei ? Ka khanatang ka parom ba ngi dei ki khun ki ksiew jong ki 16 trep ki 16 skum. Hynrei kim mynjur pat ba ki wan hiar na bneng (yngba ka Jingkieng Ksiar U Sohpetbneng ne lyngba ki tnad Diengiei na kliar u Lum Diengi'ei: ban pynlong ki persoh persyntiew ha kane ka ri jong ka dud bad ka ngap. Ki ngeit ba ki wan poi wier na ka ri kaba jngai kaba shim por ia ki haduh 12 snem kynthih ban poi shaduh kane ka ri ba seisoh, ba pyngngad bad ba itynnad. Ka Khanatang ka iathuh ba ka jaka shong tynrai jong ki ka dei ha Hunan, ka bynta kaba shathie lam mihngi jong ka China, ha ki pyntha ba seisoh jong ka Yangtzikiang shuwa ban tyllep ia ka da ki Moghal na Central Asia. Te, ynda ki la ia roi bad bun paid ki shem ba ym don jaka rep jaka riang shuh. Ba kumta shikynhun na ki kila mih noh ha ki 16 lieng ban wad jaka rep thymmai hapoh ka bneng. Ki king arsut ka Wah Yangzikiang sha ka Duriaw China ba shathie. La ong ba hadien bun bun sngi kila Tohi na jngai ia ka ri kaba itynnad kaba tap da ki lawbah lawsan. Da ka jingkmen ki 16 lieng ki pynphai ia la ki phar sha ki rud duriaw jong ka ba ki thmu ban hiar ryngkew hangta. Hapdeng jong ka jingkmen bad jingphuh mynsiem kynsan kynsan la khie ka ’eriong ’erngit kaba jur bad ia ki lieng jong ki la fiiad jubor bad lynshop ha duriaw. Ki nongking lieng ki Taleh dohi'ap dohim ban Tada na ka jingngam jyllop bad baroh kila duh jngkyrmen ban dang Yohi 2 ryngkew biang. Ha kane ka jingi'aleh la pyn'iakhlad ia ki 7 lieng bad ki 9 lieng. Ynda ka ’eri'ong kala thanda bad ka duriaw ka la jai jai ki 9 lieng kim i'ohi syrngiew synget shuh ia ki 7 lieng. Ynda kila hiar ryngkew ki pyrshang ban wad ia ki 7 lieng lyngba ki lawbah lawsan, ki lum bad ki madan bun bun sngi khlem da ia shem shuh ia ki. Ki Taid na kawei ka jaka sha kawei ka jaka ryngkat ka jingi'am jingsngewsih bad ki pyrta ia ki lum ki pyntha hynrei jlang jlang ki en kynjah. Hadien ka jingwad kaba sohsat ki pynsuk jingmut noh ia lade bad ki sher dara ha trai jong ki jri ki kya (i'ei) bad ki ai kyrteng ia kata ka jaka “La ang ka wad” lehse na kane ka kyntien sa mih suki suki ka kyrteng Ankorvat, bad ia kata ka ri kaba ki wad ia ki hynfiiew da ki ummat ki khot ia ka ka ‘Sah-i'am’ bad lehse na kane ka kyntien sa mih ka ri kaba ki khot Siam. Ki 9 lieng ki ngeit ba ki 7 lieng ki don ha bneng, ha ka jingsuk bad U Blei Trai Nongthaw bad ki ngeit ruh ba kin sa i'ashem pat bad ki ynda ka jingim ha kane ka pyrthei ruhshong bynda kala wai. Khlem artatien ki 7 lieng ruh ki hiar ryngkew bad ki wad i'a ki 9 lieng bad namar ba kim lap syrngiew syrnget shuh ia ki; ki ngeit ba ki 9 lieng ki don ha bneng bad U Blei ha ka jingsuk jingsaifi, Hynrei lyngba ki pateng bad ki rta ki 7 kim klet ban duwai ia ki 9 bad ki khyndai ruh kim klet ban duwai na ka bynta ki 7. Hadien bun snem jong ka jingsaphriang bad ka jingiaid wir, ka paw ba ki Khyndai bad ki Hynfiiew ki shong ki sah stem slem ha Combodia. Katkum ka jingshem jong U Gurdon, ki Khasi ki long tang ma ki kiba kren ia ka ktien Austric katba ki marjan jong ki baroh ki kren ia ka ktien Bodo. Ki stad wad 3 jingtip ki ngeit ba ki Khasi ki wan sha kine ki lum na shaphang mihngi, kata na ka thaifi jong ka wah Mekong bad ki don ka jingi'adei kaba jan bad ki Kmer ne Mon-kmer ne Mon-Anam. Ki Khasi kim shym wan shisien wan lymbung sha kine ki lum lyngba ki Lum Padkoi, hynrei kynhun kynhun lyngba ki snem. U Hutton u ong ba ki Khasi ki don ka jingi'adei kaba jan eh bad ki Mon-Khmer, U iathuh ruh ba ki mawbynna bad mawniam kiba ngi shem ha North-Cachar Hills ki don ka jingi'a syriem kaba jur bad ki mawniam mawbyna ha Tonkin. Kane ka pynjan shibun bad ka Khanatang ki Sheila ba ki wan na Hunan. Ki Khanatang bad ka jingshem ki riewstad mynta ki ia mynjur ba ki Khasi ki wan na shaphang mihngi bad ki shong ki sah nyngkong ha ri Jaintia. Katno slem ki 9 bad 7 ki phriang ki saphret ia lade ha Combodia khlem ia kynduh, ngim tip; hynrei ki dak ki shin ki pynpaw ba kila sah slem slem. Ki Sheila, kum kawei na ki kynhun jong ki 9 ki ngeit ba ki dei ma ki ki nongtei jong kata ka nongbah Ankorvat ba donnam: bad ban pynsah jingkynmaw ia ka ki shna ka kynja jingdeng ne jingwoh shkor kaba ki khot “Engkor" haman la kawei pa kawei ka kynthei. Balei pat ki phet bad iehnoh Ting jah ia kane ka nongbah; ki stad wad jingtip ki pynsabut ba ki iehnoh ia ka namar ka khlam ka Yap them kaba la sarTa ka Nongbah jong ki. Ba kumta kim banse ban iehnoh bad turn bad tarn bad phet Yap sha ki khlaw ki btap jong ki lum Patkoi lyngba jong ka North Cachar Hills ban poi sha ka Ri Jaifitia: bad ban pynsah jingkynmaw ia kata ka jingshem lanot jong ki; man ka snem ki pynlong ka Beh-deifi khlam: ka jingleh niam ryngkat ka phur ka shat ban kyrpad Ta U Blei Trai Kynrad ban da ban ri ia ki na ka khlam ka ngoh. 4 Napdeng jong ki Khasi tang ki Synteng/Pnar bad ki Sheila kiba rakhe bad lehniam kyrpang ia ka Beh-dein khlam; kaba pynpaw ba ki Sheila bad ki Synteng/Pnar ki dei ka kynhun jong kito ki 9 lieng. Lada ka history ka pynsabut ba ki Mon- khmer mynba ki wan sha kine ki lum; ki shong ki sah nyngkong ha ri Jaifitia bad nangta ki sa saphret kylleng ka ri Lum Khasi: ka phalang jingmut ha ngi ba ki 7 kila poi sha kine ki lum shuwa jong ki 9. Namarkata, lada ki riewstad mynta ki pynshisha ba ki Khasi ki dei tang ma ki, kiba kren ia ka ktien Austric ha kine ki phang jong ka ri India: khlem artatien ngi ngeit skhem ba ki 7 bad ki khyndai ki pynlong ia ka jaitbynriew Khasi. Ka history ka Tathuh ba ki Shelia ki wan na Jaihtiapur. Kumjuh ruh ki Malngiang na Madur- Maskut, ki Syiemlieh ka Hima Nongkhlaw na Sutnga bad ki Jirang na Umwi. Namarkata, ngi pynkut nia ba ka ri Laiphhew Syiem Khatar Daloi kam dei ka ri tang jong ki 7 trep talawiar u Sohpetbneng, hynrei ka ri kyntang jong u 16 trep khathynriew skum kiba wan na khatar snem lynti ban thong i'a la ka jingim katkum ka tang Blei hangne. i. Na Shylla Sha Laitkor: Katkum ka khanatang, ki Sheila ki shong shnong nyngkong eh ha Shylla bad hadien ba kila bun paid bad khlaifi bor ki hiar ban dakhol ia ka ri thor bad tei ia ka nongbah ba donnam, ka Jaifitiapur, ha ka khyndai spah snem. Kane ka nongbah ka neh haduh kaba sdang jong ka Khatlai spah snem (1210-12). U Altamush, u syiem mraw bakhraw tarn; hadien ba ula pyndem ia ka Bengal baroh kawei, u hiar thma ia ka Jaihtiapur bad u thang sain ia ka. Kane ka long ka sien kaba nyngkong ba ki Syiem Masulman ki hiarthma ia ka ri Khasi 5 bad ka Jaifttiapur ka long kaba nyngkong ban hap ha ka kti jongki. Hynrei ki Sheila ki lait na ka jingshah ring mraw bad ki pheti'ap sha ki lum bad ki khlaw jong ka Hima Jaifitia. Ka khana pateng ka Yathuh ba ki shipai u Altamush kila kerkut ia ka Nongbah Jaifitiapur lai sngi lai miet: hynrei kim shym lah satia ban jop. Ki Shelia, hapoh ka jingYalam jong ki Kuhaifi (khaifi): ynda kim sngew don pyrthei shuh ban Yada ia ka: ha ka miet kaba lai kila mih jar jar na ka Nongbah lyngba kawei ka lynti rieh bad kila phetYap bad turn bad tarn sha ki khlaw barben jong ki lum Jaifitia. Ha kane ka jingYaidwir kila leit poi sha ki pud jong ka North Cachar Hills bad ki shong ki sah ha Batua. Ha ka step kaba bud jong ka sngi kaba lai; ki Masulman ki lyngngoh ban Yohi ba ka Nongbah ka sah khlem nongYada. Ki ryngkang ia ki Kharai urn bad ki kiew ia ki kynroh ka nongbah. Ha ka jinglyngngoh ki lap ba ka shnong baroh kawei kala thylli khlem da don shuh tang ka ksew ka miaw ruh. Ha ka jingbitar ki la thang saift ia ka bad leit phai noh sha Bengal. Ki Khana pateng ki Yathuh ba ki Sheila kila sah bun bun snem ha Batua. la kane lah ban pynshisha na ki Kharai, ki Mawbynna, ki pepbah ki peprit bad bun kiwei kiwei ki jingtei maw kiba ngi dang lah ban Yohi haduh kine ki sngi. Hangne ki la riewspah bad kila man roi bad ki la pyrshang ban pynfar la ki pud ki sam. Ki la tei ki kynroh bad ki kharai kiba khlaifi sawdong ka shnong: hynrei ka jingpyndik jong ki Dimasa bad ki Kachari kiba pyrshang ban kyntur jaka man ka por, ka la pynlong ia ki ban kynriah jaka noh hadien bun ki thma bad ki jingYaleh. Kawei ka khana pateng ka Yathuh ba hadien jong ki thma bad ki jingYaleh pyrshah ia ki Dimasa bad ki Cachari ka khlam kala 6 sar la ka shnong jong ki bad kim banse shuh ban kynriah jaka. Sa shisienltii Sheila ki i'eng ka phetwir. Ki shem ba kim lah ban jam sha Mihngi ne shatei namar ba ki don ki kynhun bakhlairi jong ki Cachari, ki Mikir, ki Demasa bad ki Bodo; ba kumta kim banse ban phai sha ka liang sepngi sha ki lum Jaifitia. Nyngkong eh ki poi ha Shangpung bad ki panjaka na u Doloi Shangpung ban shong ban sah hapoh ka llaka jong u. Ha kaba nyngkong U Doloi bad ki paitbah ki shah sngewbha ia ki ban shong ban sah hapoh ka llaka jong ki. Hynrei ynda ki shem ba ki Shelia ki long khamsian, kham riewspah bad kham don buit ban trei ban ktah bad pyni'adei i'ajan bad kiba bun ki shnong ki thaw ki tieng bishm kylla bad ki pyrshang da bun ki lad ki lynti bad wad la kajia bad pynkhih thma. Ki Sheila ki sngewsih eh ia kane ka jingleh shukor shetkylla: bad namar ba kim sngew kot bor ban i'aleh da ka thma ka ktien: shisyndon ki kut jingmut ban mih noh na Shangpung bad ban wad da kawei pat ka jaka ha kaba ki lah ban im ha ka jingshngaifi bad jingsuk jingsaih. Ki phai la ki khmat sha ki lum Khasi bad ki wanpoi ha Puriang bad Mawryngkneng. Ki pynrieh ia ki jaitsyiem ha kawei ka krem kaba ngi tip pateng haduh mynta kum ka ‘Krem Syiem’, kaba don harudjong kawei ka wahduid kaba la sin pateng haduh mynta ka “Umsyiem” namar ba ki syiem ki leit sum tang hangta. Lehse dei na kane ka khana pateng ba ki syiem Malngiang hadien ka jingthang ia ka Madur- Maskut da ki synteng , bun spah snem hadien jong ka jingphetwir ki Sheila ki wan rieh ha kane kajuh hi ka jaka ban lait na ki synteng. Ki mawbynna bad ka Kut Sheila ha Mawryngkneng ki sakhi ba ki Sheila kila sah hangne kham katto katne por. Ki tymmen ki dang iathuh khana ba harud ka Umsyiem ki i'eng lai tylli ki Ting Syiem ha kaba ki jaitsyiem ki 7 shong ki sah, bad sa sin pateng ia kane ka jaka haduh mynta ka Um-lai-syiem. Na kano ka daw ba ki Shelia ki kynriah jaka noh nangne ngim tip. Ka lah ban long ka daw jong ka jingbymseisoh ka jaka ne ka jingpyndik jong kiwei pat ki kynhun kiba shong sawdong jong ka: ka khanatang kam kren ei ei halor kane. La ong ba na Puriang- Mawryngkneng ki wanpoi bad sah shipor ha Sohryngkham. Da ka jingi'a sngewthuh jingmut bad ki Nongkrem, kiba shong shnong ha kata ka por ha Umlung, ha ki ranab lum lyndiang u Lum Rapleng- ki wan thaw shnong ha Laitkor (hajan ka Raaar bad Television Station mynta); ka jaka kaba sawang na kaba ki lah ban i'ohi kyndiang i'a ki pyntha ka Ri Bhoi bad ki Lum pylloit ka ri Khasi. Katkum ki kor, ki maw shongthait, ki mawniam, ki mawbynna, ki maw shyieng bad ki oepbah peprit, ka pynpaw ba ki Sheila kila sah slem hangne. Ha kaba nyngkong ki Sheila bad ki Nongkrem ki don <a jingi'adei i'ajan kaba sngewtynnad bad ki im ha ka jingsuk ingsaifi bad jingi'aburom markylliang. Dei kane ka jingiadei iajan kaba la pynlong ia ki Shelia ban pdiang ia U ’Lei Shyllong kum u Ryngkew u Basan jong ki bad ki ainguh ha u da ar langtlem sop ksiar ki reng shisien shisnem, katba ki Nongkrem ki ai da ar langtlem sop reng rupa. Ki Nongkrem ki i kumba u ’Lei Shyllong u kham thiah sha ki Shelia namar ba ki Shelia ki kham khraw ha ka spah bad ka burom. Suki suki ka jingbishni ka rung bad ka jingi'a kynad ka sdang. Nyngkong eh ka sdang ka jingi'akajia pud kajia sam ha ka liang ka rep ka riang bad nangta suki suki ka mih ka jingi'a kyntur jaka phuka bad ka jingi'awad daw haneng harum. Hynrei ka mat kaba kongsan ka long ka jingsngew bishni ba ki Shelia ki ai da ki ’langsopreng 8 ksiar ha u 'lei Shyllong. Man ka khep ki Nongkrem ki wad daw sha ka jingialeh hynrei ki Sheila ki kiar namar ba kim sngew lah kotbor ban ia khun. Ki Nongkrem pat ki nangpyni bor namar ba ki shrai ba ki Shelia ki manbha. Ynda ki lad jingiasuk baroh kila kut, ki Shelia jar jar ki thmu ban mihnoh bad phet sha ki thain ri Bhoi. Ki Nongkrem ki ipher ia ka rukom laid rukom i'eng ki Sheila bad ki phah syntiat na man la ki dong. Ha kawei ka step ki mih jar jar bad turn bad tarn bad hiar ia ki rashing u Lum Shyllong. Ki Nongkrem kiba la apthap ki buddien sia bad ki lap ngung ha padun u Lum Shyllong. Ka jingialeh ka long kaba jur bad ki Nongkrem ki i'oh ban siat ia u Thu Noi na ka siang tyrpeng, katba ki paitbah bad ki rang kiengstieh kiengwait ki lait war sha shiliang. Ka jaka ha kaba la siat ia u la tip pateng la pateng kum ka ‘Law-pom-im-im’ harum jong ka Don Bosco Technical School, Shillong. Ki Nongkrem ki kem ia u bad im- im peit-peit ki khlong ia ki shyieng tyngam bad sah ia ki ha u dieng kseh uba ngat hapdeng lynti. Haduh mynta mynne, ki khun ki ksiew jong ki Sheila kim ju jam ia kane ka khlaw kaba ki khot mynta ka ‘Lawpomdngiem’ (Lawpom-im-im) lymda ki biah ki bynthiew laisien laiwat kum ka dak jong ka jingsngewsih ia ka jinglehsang jong ki Nongkrem ia u Kpa-rad jong ki. ii. Na Laitkor sha Mawtyngang (Pom Sheila) Ki Nongkrem kim nud shuh ban tur namar ki Rangkiengstieh kiengwait ki pahara bad ki siat klep kat ia uba nud ban buddien. Ynda la janmiet bad ba ka kynhun ka la thait Tan; ki poi ha Mawtyngang ha kaba i'eng ka North Eastern Hills University mynta bad ki rai ban shong shnong hangne. Ki tei saw tylli ki shnong- kawei ha Mawi'ong hajan ka Lawbyrwa, ba 9 shong ki Marwet ne ki Nongwar, ka Mustoh, ha ki thaifi Mawsiatkhnam, ka Shala, ha Mawtyngang bad ki Nongbah, ha ki thain Mawtawar. la kine ki saw shnong saw kynhun la tip pateng ha ki khanatang kum ki Sawkher Sawkuro, namar ba ki mih na kajuh ka tynrai Ka thymmei. Sa shisien ka Iyer jong ka jingkmen bad jingmanbha ka beh ha ki Shelia namar ba ki i'oh ia ki khlaw kiba rben bad lyngkha ktieh ba seisoh. Ki im pahuh pahai bad ki tei ki ling bha ilng miat ryngkat ki kut, ki khyrdop bad ki kharai sawdong ki shnong jong ki. Ka kut kaba khlain bad ba pawnam ka dei ka kut U Byrwa ha Ryndangbriew, Mawi'ong: namar hangne ki shong ki Nongwar kiba long ki riewthma. Ha neng jong kane ka kut ka don kawei ka pyndem shad ha kaba ki shadrong shadniam shisien shisnem bad uwei u Mawrong ha uba ki kfiia ki khriam bad ki puja pukat. Harum jong u Mawrong don u Mawlympat khlieh ha uba la ki khlieh jong ki nongshun kiba i'oh khrai ki lympat ki lynthaw hadien ka shadniam shadrukom ne ka shadthma. Kham harum shuh shuh pat ka don ka thwei ha kaba ki bret ia ki sla-kliar hadien ba la dep pyndonkam ha ka niam ka rukom, ka kfiia ka khriam bad ki khot ia ka ‘Ka Wei- sla’ ha ka Wah Nongksih. Ki Shala ki long ki riewnia bad ba sian buit. Namar hapdeng jong ki, ki don ki jait syiem bad ki riewsaifi hima sima. Ki Mustoh bad ki Nongbah ki long ki riew bun paid kiba pynmih ia kimyntri ki Korbari. Katba ki Nongwar (Marwet) pat ki long ki riewthma bad ki nongiada. Kane ka jinglong jong ki ka hiarpateng haduh U Bosan U Snakon kiba ki khana tympang shaphang ka jingshlur jong ki, ki dang sah ha Mawrynfiiaw ha U Thlong bad haduh u Borthan, u Rangbah nongi'alam thma 10 ka Hima Shelia; uba la i'akhun marwei bad la ka kynhun pyrshah ia ki phareng naduh ka snem 1829-30 haduh u December, 1939' wat hadien ba ki Duwakdar ka hima Shelia kila pyndem wait pyndem stieh ha ki Phareng ha ka snem 1834 U Borthan bad ki Nongwar ki leng triang na ka Kut Wahkhain pyrshah ia ka borbah ki Phareng, hadien ba kila shah beh krad na Mawmluh. Ki Phareng ki la pyrshang ban tur na kiba bun ki dong hynrei ki hap kynran dien. Dei ka jingshet kylla jong ki Ramdait bad U Duwan Syiem Sohra da kaba ki pyni lynti la ki shipai phareng ban tur sha Wahkhain na ki thain Tynrong, ba sa i'oh siat i'a U Borthan bad sa jem jai-ljai ka jingi'aleh. La ki nongthoh history ki la leh bym dei ia u Borthan, pynban ka history kam klet ban pynkynmaw ba u long uwei na ki riewshlur jongka ri Khasi ha ka thma pyrshah ia ki Phareng. Ki khanatang ki i'athuh ba ki Sawkher sawkuro kila shong bun pateng ha Mawtyngang, Mui'ong, Mawsiatkhnam bad Mawtawar. Da ka jingstad ki pyni'ar la ka khail pateng ryngkat ka jingi'adei i'ajan bad ka Ri Bhoi shaduh ki pud ki sam jong ka ri thor Assam. Ki khanapateng ki i'athuh ba ki Shelia kila don ka jingi'adei kabajan haduh katta katta bad ki Sohbar, Nongjri bad Thai'ang. La ong ba ha kata ka juk, ka Thaiang ka long ka kadbah jong ka khaii ka pateng hapdeng ka ri Khasi ba shatei bad ka thor Assam; bad ki Shelia ki i'oh ia ka kabu ban pyntuid la ka khaii ka pateng lyngba kane ka kad. Haduh mynta, ki don bun ki sakhi ban pynshisha ba ka Thai'ang ka long kawei na ki Nongbah ba pawnam tarn ha ka ri Khasi ba shaphang shatei. Ka jingstad jong ki Sheila ha ka liang ka saifi hima sima ka pynlong ia kiba bun ki shnong ha ri Bhoi ban i'asnoh noh bad ki. 11 Dei kane ka dawbah kaba la pynsat sia ia kiba khraw ka Hima U Basan Nongkseh; khamtam eh ki Mawproh Mawpri: kiba shong basah ha kata ka por ha Laitkor. La ki pyrshang da ka buit kim lah Ban i'aleh pat da ka thma ha bapaw bashai ki tieng namar ba ki Sheila kila bun paid bad ba ki long ki nongsiat khnam kiba tbit. Nalor nangta shuh shuh ki Shelia ki Voh ia ka jingieit jingsngewbha jong kiba bun ki shnong ha ri Bhoi bad kumjuh ruh jong ki Bodo bad ki Mikir. Nalor kata, ki Sheila ki don ki kut ki kharai bad ki rangkieng stieh kiengwait kiba pawnam ha kata ka por. Ka kyntien Sawkher Sawkuro ka pynkhynhiuh ia kiba bun: hynrei kim long pat ki riew pathar ba pyni'ar hima da ka thma. Ka jingthmu jong ki ka long ban pyniar 1 a u pud u sam ka hima da ka jingsuk ym da kaba ia umsnam. Namar kata, ki pynpaw ha ka pyrthei ba ki long khamsian khamlah ban ia kiwei pat: bad kata hi ka khring ia kiba bun ki shnong ki thaw ban wan ia snoh bad ki. Kane ka juh ka buit ki pyndonkam ha kaba ki seng ia ka Hima 23 shnong. Ki Mawproh Mawpri ki shu peit siar da ka dohnud kaba ingkhong bad ki ap ia ka por. Hadien ba ki Shelia kila shong la sah bun snem ha Mawtyngang la wanpoi shikynhun ki nongsyntiat kiba leh mynleh wan behmrad sha ki thaifl ba ki shong. Ki RangTapom kila kynshu da ki Ksew bad kila behthong Ta ki. Ki nongsyntiat kim don lad shuh ban leh kumno kumno ruh namar ba ki ksew ki kahait ia ki baroh swdong. Shisyndon ki rieh ia lade hapoh jong ki skum kba. Ki Shelia ki tang shu Tohi ia kane ki tur roit roit bad ki sum ia ki da ki sum. Hynrei ynda kila sabut na ka riam ka beit ba ki dei na ka jait syiem; kila rai ban leit pynphai ia ki metl'ap jong ki katkum ka aifi jong ka juk; khnang ba ki trai 12 kur ki lah ban thang Siarkait thang lyngkha-son ia ki. Kane ka jingleh kala pynjynsur la u khu ki Nongkrem bad pynjem ia ka jingi'akynat jingbuh ingtyrkhong kaba kila ju don baroh shikatta Ka khanatang ka lathuh ba ki Nongkrem bad ki Sheila ki pynlong ka jingiakren Vasuk da kaba ki kular ban pynlong ia ka jingiateh lok bad ka jingiadei iajan kaba palei pasiang. Ban pynskhem la kane, baroh arliang ki kular ban pynlong ka jingkhawai iasuk ryngkat ka shad ka kmen hakhmat jong u lok u jor bad ki marjan marpa ki ban i'eng kum ka sakhi la kane ka soskular. Ka sngi jong ka jingkhawai Vasuk kala poi. Ka riew ka ksiang ka dhah, ka besli ka tangmuri ryngkat ka shad ka kmen ka kynkui ka risa bad ka khawai ka dawai kaba ym don thylliet ban batai. Hynrei ynda la dei ka pali ba ki Sheila kin bam kin dih, ha ka jinglehraih ki Nongkrem ki lap ba ym don doh shuh. Ynda la swar la tohkit ki lap ba ki Mylliem na Bisi kila rah tuh noh ia ki doh baroh. Kane ka jingleh dusmon kala pynkthang ia ki Nongkrem: hynrei kim lah leh ei ei shuh namar ka sngi kala jan sep bad kila dei ban leit phai noh sha la ki jong ki jong ki shnong. Dei naduh kata ka por sa sin biria pateng la pateng “Mylliem tuhdoh”. Ka shad ka kmen bad ka kynhui ka risa ka dkut syndet bad ka jingjahburom ka par kum ka jingtyrsaih. Ki paitbah ki pra phiaw bad ki Sheila ki wan syndet sha la shnong khlem da pynlong satia ia ka jingiasuitiashor Vasuk. Lehse kane ka long kawei na ki daw ba ki Mawproh Mawpri ki ingtyrkhong bad buhnud ia ki Sheila. Ki Shelia ki nangroi ha ka spah bad ka burom hapdeng ki para khun syiem khun long bad ki nangpynVar ia la ka jingiadei iajan ym tang hapoh ka ri Khasi hynrei wat shabar ri 13 Khasi ruh. Kane, kata nang pynbitar bad pynshrai shuh shuh ia ki Mawproh Mawpri. Ba kumta, ha kawei ka miet badum bnai; katba ki Sheila ki dang pynlong ka puja pukat bad ka leh kmen leh sngewbha ha ka blei kali, katkum ka niarn ka rukom jong ki: khlem da phohsmew eiei ba kaba smew kan hap ha ki: ki riewthma Mawproh Mawpri kila partuh shapoh ka shnong bad kila pyniap khatlai (13) kynthei Ha ko jmglamwir ki paitbah kila phet kulmar bad ki Mawproh Mawpri kila thangsain ia ka shnong jong ki. Ki Mustoh bad ki Nongbah ynda kila lohi ia ka jingklang ka ding kila boh wot wot hynrei kim lap shuh ia ki Mawproh Mawpri Ki lum la ki met lap bad ki rah la ki sha MawTong. Ka Riah ka fa phet ruma shimiet ,-himiet bad rieh ha ka jaka ha Mawlai kaba la tip pateng haduh mynta ‘Ka Syllai Ka Riah’. Ha ka step kaba bud ki Rangiapom ki wad la ki paidbah ba saphret bad ki lum lang ia ki ha kut U Byrwa ha Ryndangbriew. Ki rangbah Sawkher Sawkuro ki pynlong ka durbar bad ki rai ban khot la u Lei Shyllong. Harud jong u Mawrong, ha Pyndem Shad ki tei ka duwan bad ki kylli ia u Lei Shyllong- balei ba u buh ka bijar ka lanot haduh katne, bad kaei ba kila pynthut pynsngewsih ia u ba um lah satia ban da ban ker ia ki. La ong ba u Lei Shyllong ryngkat ki khun jong u, ki la wanpaw ha duwan ryngkat u diengduh ksiar ha kti bad ula kyntu ia ki Shelia ban mih noh na Mawtyngang bad i'aid shaphang shathie: da kaba u kular skhem ban da ban sumar ia ki lynter lynti ba ki laid. Ha khmat ka duwan u tim ia ki Mawproh-Mawpri namar ba ki leh 1a ka kam saitmet ki riewkhawpud ban hiarthma mynmiet mynTong khlem da pynbna thma. Ka khanatang ka Tathuh ba dei kane ka jingtim kaba la 14 pynduh jait pynduh kur khoit ia ki Mawproh Mawpri. Ki ar jait bakhraw jong ka hima U Basan Nongkseh. Hynrei ki khun jong U Lei Shyllong - U Kil, U Pdah, U Thaw, Ka Snge, U Kyrban, U Saw Syiem, Ka Shati ki pan jingbit na u Kpa ban bud ryngkat bad ki Shelia kat sha ba ki leit. U Lei Shyllong um banse ban shah ia ki, bad haduh mynta ki kylla long ki dken jong ki Sheila: kiba da ba ker ia ki lyngba ki snem bad ki rta. ia ka Mawtyngang la tip pateng pakit haduh mynta kum “Ka Pom Shala”, bad mynta ka i'eng ka North Eastern Hills University hangne. iii. Na Pom Sheila (Mawtyngang) sha Pynter Hadien ka Durbar blei ha Pyndem shad Mawi'ong, ki Sawkher Sawkuro: kumba la bthah u ‘Lei Shyllong’; ki jam ia ka pyntha Umsaw ban kiar na ka Hima U Basan Nongkseh bad hadien katto katne sngi ki poi ha Manai. Nangta ki i'aid shaphang shathie lam sepngi ki wanpoi ha Bynther, kaba hapoh ka Hima Nongkhlaw. Ki Sheila kila itynnad eh ban shong ban sah hangne bad ki pan jingbit na U Syiem bad ki Bakhraw ka Hima Nongkhlaw. Ki Nongkhlaw, ba ki tieng ia ka jingbun paid; ki kyntaid ia ka jingkyrpad jong ki: wat la ki Shelia ki kloi ban pynlong ka soskular jingi'ateh lok. Ka daw kaba kongsan ba ki Nongkhlaw kirn mon ba ki Sheila kin shong kin sah ha Bynther namar ki tip ba ki long ki briew kiba kham shai bad kham don buit. Kumta ki Shelia kirn banse ban kynriah noh na Bynther bad wad da kawei pat ka jaka kaba shngaift bad ba lait na ki jingi’a kajia majia baroh. Ha kane ka jingiaidwir ki wanpoi ha Nonglwai: ka shnong jong ki Jyrwa. Ki Jyrwa ki pdiang sngewbha bad ki kyrpad ba kin shong kin sah lang noh bad ki. Hynrei ki Shelia kiba la ju im 15 haki jaka kiba seisoh kim mon satia ban shong ban sah ha Nonglwai namar ba ka long ka jaka dewksang bym seisoh. Shisyndon ki pynlong ka khat ka shat ban kylli pyrthew na ki blei la ka Nonglwai ka dei ne em ka jaka ba kin shong kin sah: ka jubab ka long ba ka lynti laid jong ki ka dang jngai. Shisyndon ki pynpaw ia ka jingsngewsih ba kim lah ban shong ban sah hangta namar ba ki blei kim mon 1a ki ba kin leh kumta. Hynrei ki kular skhem ban pynlong ka soskular lateh lok hapdeng jong ki. Ki Jyrwa kim nud pynbor shuh la ki bad pdiang ia ka soskular i'ateh lok. Sa shisien ki Sheila' ynda kila kylli pyrthew na ki Jyrwa shaphang ka jmglong jong kata ka ri ryngkat ki hima syiem hima muluk: ki kut jingmut ban jam sha ka hima U Basan Synrem. Bad hadien bun sngi ki wanpoi ha kyrdem khla ha kaba i'eng ka All India Radio, Transmission Centre, mynta. U Basan Synrem u pdiang sngewbha bad u kyrpad ia ki ban shong ban sah noh ha ka hima jong u. Ka la don ka jingi'adei i'ajan kaba jur khamtam hapdeng ki Synrem bad ki kynhun u Khang U Saei haduh ba la poi sha ka ia shongkha shongman khleh: hynrei kiwei pat ki kynhun kim mon ban shong ban sah ha Kyrdemkhla. Nangne ki thew beit phiak arsut bad ki shong shnong shipor ka Laitsohpdiah. Haduh mynta dang don u Mawshohdoh ki Shelia ha uba ki kfiia ki khriam ha U Lei Shyllong. Ha kata ka por ka Sohra bad Mawmluh ki dang long tang ki ri khali ba tap da u phlang bad ki Lawlynnong. La ong ba mynba ki Sheila ki dang don ha Laitsohpdiah ki ju leit hat leit Tew barabor ha Dubikhal bad Amsarjang ban khan pateng bad Tadie Tathied bad ki dkhar. Lehse dei kane ka jingleit jingwan jong ki kaba la pynlong ia ki ban jurip bad peit shin ia ki it ki 16 jaka ban ioh ka ri kaba shngain bad ba seisoh ha kaba ki lah ban im suk im sain Ha kawei ka sngi U Ben U Khrang, U Khang U Saei, U Skot, U Anai U Syrna bad U Kait kila i'akut ban leit beh mrad bad ban jurip jaka artad La ong ba ha kane ka jingleit behmrad kila poi ba Lum Lawbah. ka jaka kaba btiap bad ba kynrei hi skei ki khial U Syrna ula siat la u Khiat tang ba u dei salif Ynda kila buddien ki lap ba u phet sha ki thain Mawshamok bad ki i'oh pynkyllon fa u hangta. Hynrei kane ka jingleit beh mrad ka plie la ki khmat jong ki ban lotn la ka ri kaba seisoh bad ba khali Bran ki wan sha Laitsohpdiah rynqkaf u khiat ba kila Voh pynkyllon ban I'athuh ia ka khubor ba kmen kaba kila shem ha ka jingleit beh mrad jong ki Shisyridon ki khot 1a ka durbar bad ki rai ban hiar sha kata ka ri kaba thymmai. Katkum ka khana pateng baroh kiba mih na Laitsohpdiah ki long 13 kynhun: kata, baroh 13 kynhun ki wan na Pomshella. Hynrei ynda ki poi hajan Sohra (mynta) harud jong kawei ka wahduid, Ka Riah, namar ba kala thait eh ka i'apler jlang bad kam lah jam shuh. Hynniew kynhun ki ap ia ka haduh ba kan da peitmat katba ki hynriew ki nangi'aid sha khmat. Ynda ki poi ha Sohra ki phai sha ka liang mihngi phang shathie bad ki ngam sha ki ranab lum ban pynlong ia ki shnong Laiti'am, Ryngud, Sohbar, Nongjri bad Wahlong. Hadien ba ka Riah kala peitmat ki 7 kynhun ki hiar bad sher dara ha Lumkhluit (Mawmluh ba ki khot mynta), ha ki thaifi ba i'eng ka Cherra-Mawmluh Cement Factory, marpyrshah U Lum Lawbah. Ka lyiur kala wai bad ka Synrai kala sdang. Sa shisien ki Saw kynhun ki sdang ban leit jurip biang ia ka jaka ba ki thmu ban shong ban sah bad ki shem ba 17 ki khlaw ki btap ki dap da ki soh ki pai ryngkat ki phan khlaw har rukom Ki shem ruh ba ki wahduid wahrit ki dap da ki dohthli dohtham bad ki shersyngkai. Da ka jmgkmen ki wan ban i'athuh ha ki paralok kiba ap ha Lum Khluit. Ki pynlong durbar bad ki rai ban mih noh ha ka sngi kaba bud; hynrei smew bok ha kata hi ka miet, ka Pyrdei, ka tnga U Khrang ka Tap noh. Namar ba ka dei na ka jait bakhraw, donkam ban da leh mam leh rukom bad ban da phur da sieng laisngi laimiet. U Jasow, ryngkat ki para kynthei shynrang jong u ki kyrpad sngewsynei ia ki saw kynhun ban ap lang haduh ban da lait-ia- lait-miat bad ban da dep leh mam leh rukom baroh. Hynrei ki lai kynhun kim lah shuh ban ap namar ba ym don bam shun. Ynda kila pot ha Mawshamok, ki phai sha ka liang sepngi ban pynlong ia ka shnong Nongkroh, Tyrna bad Mynteng. Ki Saw kynhun, hapoh ka jingialam U Ben U Khrang, U Khang U Saei, U Skot, U Anai U Syrna bad U Kait ynda ki la poi ha Mawshamok ki kiew shalor lum bad poi ha ka jaka pyntha phlang kaba pyngngad bad itynnad kaba syriem kum ka Byrther bad ki ai kyrteng ia ka Pynter. Ka kyrteng Laitkynsew ka dang mih dang tang ha ka snem 1812 ha ka por jong ka ’Mamawkhyrdop ha Mawmluh hapdeng U Konrai Syiem Nongkhlaw bad u pyrsa jong u, U Hainsing Syiem. U Haiftsing u thorn ia ka kut Mawshamok katba U Konrai bad ki briew jong u ki khyllep la u nadien U Hainsing ynda u sngew ba um lah kyrda shuh ba la poi ha ka khim khak u panmap bad u pyrta ia suk. "Pha shu tait thaw kumba lait ka ksew”, kren dom U Konrai, ryngkat ka map artad. Naduh kata ka por ia ka kynhun U Hainsing la tip kum ki Laitkynsew: bad ki ioh de kumta ia ka kyrteng jong kane ka shnong. Hynrei baroh ki War Shelia ki tip 18 ia kane ka shnong kum ka Pynter: namar, shisien kala long ka jaka jong ki. Harud jong U Mawhat ki sher dara ban jurip ia kata ka jaka bathymmai. Ynda kila pynlong ka shat ka kheifi ka kylli ka pyrthew na ki blei ki dken: ki ruh ki mynjur ba kata ka jaka ban long ka jong ki. U Ben U Khrang, haba u peit ia ka Wah Rupatylli ryngkat ki jaka ba madan ba seisoh bad itynnad: ka ktik ia ka dohnud jong u bad u kwah ban shong ban sah hangta. Da ka jingmynjur lang jong kiwei pat ki kynhun.u kiew nalor U Mawhat bad lai tylli ki khnam u ong, “Ngan siat ia kine ki lai tylli ki khnam bad ha kano kano ka jaka ba ki hap, kata kan long ka jaka jong nga bad ki khun ki ksiew jong nga pateng la pateng." Ha ka sngi kaba bud jraifi ki hiar ban leit wad ia kita ki khnam bad ki lap ba uwei na kita ki khnam u sahkut halor ka tnad sohpijer. Jraifi ki shad ki risa ‘Kalatek Kalatek’ kaba mut, ‘Kala dei, Kala dei Haduh mynta mynne ia kane ka jaka la tip pateng kum ka Kalatek. Ki artylli kiwei pat ki khnam ki hap ha Sarang bad Umkhabaw, sha shiliang jong ka wah Umiam (Sheila). Katkum kane ka tang, ka pud jong ka jaka U Ben U Khrang ka long na ka wah Umiam (Shelia) . Ka kynhun jong U Ben U Khrang ka hiar ban dokhol ia kine ki jaka bad ki buhai shnong ha Sarang, Kalatek bad Umkhabaw, bad suki suki ki phiah 9 kyntoit, ba sa tip pateng kum ‘Ki khyndai Umtong Khyndai Umdih’ ne ‘Khyndai kher’. Ka don kawei ka khana pateng kaba i'athuh ba ynda ki Sheila kila buhai ha Kalatek bad Sarang; ki lap ba don katto katne ki ring rep hangta. Ynda kila kylli kila tohkit ki lap pynban ba dei u briew jong ki uba la jah na Pomshala. Ka khana pateng ka Vathuh ba ia une u briew la rahtuh da ki Hudkor, ki briew jong 19 U Syiem Jaintiapur; kiba wad kylleng ban kftia ha ka blei Kali. Hynrei ynda kila pynsum pynsleh, tab shandon (syndur kumba leh ki Hindu) bad pynphong jaifilieh sala; U Brahmon ula sdang ia ka myntro tantro; shuwa ban ai ha u Kholad ban mait ia ka khlieh jong u da ka waitlam Khorgo: une u khynnah ula dem arti hakhmat ka durblei Kali kum uba mon sngewbha ban shah na ka bynta ka jingbha jong u Syiem bad ka Hima; la ong ba hamar kata ka por kata ka durblei kali kala kren, “Ko Syiem, kaei kane ba me leh I Balei me wanrah la une u briew kum ka jingkfiia ha nga uba long hi u bhokto jong nga ! Khie shisyndon bad leit pynphai noh ia u sha la ka jaka ba u shong.” U Syiem bad kiba khraw batri baroh ki kyndit thret. “Kaei kane ! Da ki spah snem ka blei kali kam ju kren, hynrei tang mynta ka kren kyllah sngi bad ka kyntait ia ka jingai jong ngi ! Shisyndon ngi dei ban pyllait noh ia une u briew. Kumta kumta hi la hukum i'a ki Jorlad ban leit pynphai noh ia une u khynnah ryngkat ki jingai sngewbha - ka ksiar bad ka rupa. Ki Jorlad, ba ki tieng ban Yaid na kajuh ka lynti : kila raid narud narud jong ki lum Khasi bad kila wan pyllait ia u ha Shiliang ka Wah Rupatylli ne ka Wah Umiam (Shelia). Une u samla u ainguh eh ia U Blei ba ula pyllait im ia u: bad u raikut ban shong ban sah duh hangta. Namar ba ka jaka ka long kaba seisoh bad ba u don shibun ka spah ka hajar ba ai sngewbha U Syiem Jairitiapur: u i'oh ka burom bad ka jingshaniah na kiba bun ki dkhar ki lyngkien kiba shong ha Barakhia (Pudkhia). Suki suki u tei ka shnong kaba rit ryngkat bun ki shakri ki shakor bad u shongkurim ia ka khun jong uwei u Jamindar jong ka Burakhia. Kane ka jingi'akynduh bad une u samla ym tang ka wanrah ia ka jingkmen jingsngewbha jong kiba ha Ting ha sem 20 bad ki hymmen ki para jong u: hynrei ka plie ia kawei pat ka syrtap jong ka trei ka ktah bad ka jingi'adei I'ajan bad ki dkhar ki lyngkien kiba im ha ki khappud Hapdeng katto katne snem ki Sheila ki kylla long ki briew kiba pahuh pahai bad ba riewspalr kiba ki dkhar ki lyngkien jan bad jngai ki tieng bad burom la ki. Hadien ba ka kynhun U Ben U Khrang kala kam ia ka bynta kaba sha shilliang ka Wah Umiam (Sheila); ki lai kynhun ha Mawhat ki rai ban bynta ia ka bynta kaba dang sah da kaba shu ia wiangding i a ka khlaw. bad ki kular ba kat ia ka bynta kaba ka ding jong ki ka bam kan long ka bynta jong ki U Khang U Saei u tbeh na shken ka Lha bad ka ding ka bur naduh Umrem-Umbloi Lum Pukri bad Khahmalai, shaduh ka Jaka ba kam ki Syiemi'ong; lait noh ka Laiseng. Ka ding jong U Ei U Noi ka bam naduh Umbloi shaduh Nur U Thlong bad nangta shaduh Mawwaniew. Katba ka ding U Kait ka bam naduh Nur Uthlong haduh Umdat bad shaduh Synram bad shken ka Lha Une u long u pud u sam jong ki bad ki sdang ban tei la ki shnong ki thaw. Hynrei hamar kata ka por U Syiemi'ong u dawa ia kane ka khyndew. Ki Saw kynhun ki shong durbar bad ki soskular ban la tylli kawei bad i'eng da ka thma. Ha ka jingi'aleh ki Syiemi'ong kila shah jop bad kila shah beh krad sha shilliang Ka Wah Umi'am. Lehse dei na kane ka daw ba ki Nongspung ki i'oh ka hima kaba rit eh sawdong ka nongbah jong ki. Ki Saw kynhun ki wanphai da ka jingkynhoi bad jingrisa bad ki pynlong ka jingkfiia ainguh ha Uthlong ha U Mawrynfiiaw ne u maw jingduwai bad ki wanphai sha Mawhat. Sa shisien ki pynlong ka Soskular ryngkat ka suit ka shor ha Mawhat ba kin i'arap Tabeh markylliang ha ka bipot ka supot, ka khim ka shipa bad kane kan i'ai neh pateng ia pateng. 21 Ka kynhun jong U Ei U Noi ka hiar ban thawshnong ha Sohbar, harud jong ka wah Bakra bad ki khot kyrteng ia ka Lyngkien. Hynrei namar ba ki roi bad bun paid la tip ia ka pateng kum ka Nongbah. Ka khanapateng ka Vathuh ba dei ha kata ka por jong ka jingi'eng rasong jong ka , U Syiemi'ong ka Nongspung ula ia suhbuit bad U Syiem Rambrai ban hiarthma pyrshah ia ki Shelia. Ha kane ka jinghiar thma ki la tur kynsan ia ka Nongbah, bad ia kane ka thma la tip pateng kum ka Thma Lyngngam. Ki Nongbah kila kulmar jingmut wit bad kim lah kyrda shuh. Kim banse ban phet na shnong bad rieh ha ki khlaw ki btap Mar kumta ki phah ktien sha ki Shala, ki Mustoh bad ki Nongwar. Ki Mustoh bad ki Shala ki tur na shaphang Kuther bad ki Nongwar ki tur na shaphang Nilang bad Sohsong. Ka jingialeh ka la long kaba jur bad ha kaba khatduh ki lai kynhun ki jop thiaw bad ki beh krad 1a ki Syiemiong bad Rambrai sha shiliang ka Wah Umi'am (Bakra) ryngkat ka jingpynjulor kaba jur; namar ki lai kynhun ki long kiba syor bha ban siat khnam bad ’tihpatur. Ki Nongbah da ka jingkmen ki wanphai sha la ka shnong ha Sohbar hynrei ki lap ba ia ki Ting ki sem jong ki la lute bad pynjulor, bad sa shisien ki hap ban tei thymmai ia ki. Ki Nong- war, ki Mustoh bad ki Shelia ki i'arap katba don la ka bor: bad sa shisien pat ka jingim kaba kmen ka wanphai ha Nongbah. Hynrei shen hadien kane ka jingpang khlam ka sar ia ka shnong kat haduh ba ki briew kim lah shuh ban thang ban ring. Shisyndon ki kynriah shnong noh bad ki wan shong ha Kuther. Hangne ki sah haduh ki sngi jong ka jingsynshar U Ganga Singh. Ynda la pynlong la ka Pahari Bazar ne Phali, hapoh ka hima Nongbah; harud ka madan tharia Bakra: ki Nongbah ki 22 kynriah jaka noh na Kuther sha Phali. Kane ka shnong ka sah haduh ka Partition jong ka India bad ka Pakistan. Te, namar ba ka hat Phali kala khang khyrdep noh; ki nongshong shnong na Phali ki kynriah shnong noh sha Shala, Mustoh bad Nong- war. Mynta ka long tang ka ri khlaw ba kynjah: ba ka pdeng jong ka Ri War bad ka kpait jong ka Kha'ii pateng, ryngkat ki ilng paki ling dulan; ka kylla long ka shnong jong ki ftiangkynjah. Ka kynhun jong U Khang U Saei ki hiar ban thaw shnong ha Dirang, ia kaba la tip pateng kum ka Mustoh; katba U Kait Ka Riah ki hiar kham ha padum phang sepngi ban pynlong ia ka shnong Nongwar. Hynrei ki Nongwar hadien jong U Jumai Bah 1 897 ki kynriah noh sha jrong lum mar pyrshah ka Pynter bad ki i'ai sah haduh mynta. IV. Ka Ri War Ha Ki Sngi Ka Jingphetwir Lada kheifi katkum ki pateng naduh U Ben U Khrang, U Kait Ka Riah, U Khang U Saei, U Ei U Noi, U Skot U Anai U Syrna: Ki Shelia ki wanpoi sha kine ki thain la kumno kumno ha kaba sdang ka Khathynriew spah snem. Katkum ki khana pateng kala shim por ia ki haduh saw sngi ban Taid na Lumkhluit (Mawmluh) sha Pynter ryngkat bad ki turn ki tarn, ki khun ki kti bad ki tymmen ki kro. Kane ka pynsngewthuh ia ngi haduh katno ka jingrai eh, ka jingbtiap jong ki khlaw ki btap khamtam haba ki Taid ryngkat ryngkat ka thwet lynti. La Tathuh pateng ba U Ben bad U Skot ki long kiba snah bha ha ka kaikhlaw bad prong lynti khlaw bad ki Sheila ki donbok ban Toh ki rangbah kiba kum kine. Wat la ka lynti ka long kaba eh bad ba rashing pynban ki lap ba ki khlaw ki long ka jingkyrkhu ia ki namar ki Toh bun bah ki jaitphan khlaw, ki pashor kait, ki wang khlaw, ki soh 23 khlaw bad ki mrad ki mreng laiphew jait. Ki laid ryngkat ka wad bam thop shi thop haduh ban da poi ha Pynter. Dei ki ksew kiba la pyllait ia ki na ka jingi'ap bad jingi'ap thngan namar uno uno u jait phan uba ki bam haba la shet ki shem ba u long uba bit ia ki ban bam. Kumne shi kumne ki tynjuh ia ki jait phan baroh tad haduh ba kin da lah ban rep ban riang. Ka Ri War ha kito ki sngi ka long ka jaka shong jong ki khla ki hati, ki dngiem ki khiat, ki sier ki mynthna, ki skei ki bthong, ki shrieh ki tngaw, ki brai ki dyngkhiet, ki bshat ki huleng, ki niangbri ki masi khlaw, ki shynreh khlaw bad ki sim ba bun jait. Dang ha ki por jong U Ganga Singh ka Jatap Saikarap bad Lum Pukri ki long ki ktem hati kaba ym ju don ba shlan ban tur ruma. Ki Labasa bad ki lakyrwang ki synshar ia ki khlaw bad ki bsein ki thlen ba la soppailen ryngkat ki lenpula lenkhah ki iaid suwari ia ki khlaw ki btap. Ki don bun ki jingiathuh khana kiba sngewngiew ban sngap kiba ki tymmen jong ngi ki ia kynduh ha kito ki sngi. La ong shisien uwei u tymmen, mynba ki ia leit tyor ha kawei ka lyiur ba slap; ula sngewkhriat bad kwah rieh slap. Kumno re kumno u iohi ia uwei u maw ba long shakup bad u rung ban rieh slap hangta. Phewse urn tip ba uta urn dei u maw shakup hynrei ka shyntur ba ang u lenpula. Bha bok ba katba u dang rieh slap u sher ia ki khnam ha khyndew katba ia ka ryntieh u pynieng hapoh shakup uta u maw. Hadien shipor ula lyngngoh eh ban Vohi ba ka ryntieh jong u shiphang shiphang ka synkjop shiphang shiphang pat ka pyrdung. Shisyndon u mih bluit nangta, u shim bad khnam bad ryntieh bad mar kumta hi ka shyntur U Lenpula ka khang khop. Ba lymda dei ka ryntieh kaba pynwit ia ka shyntur jong u thlen ula shah nguid. 24 Ha kawei pat ka por uwei u briew u nang pyrkhat ba ka dei ka dieng Tap ba ngat hakhlaw. U kiew napdeng joit ban shong dih duma hangta. Mar shiphang kata ka dieng ka khih bad u nang tharai u jumai. U ryngkoh pum ha madan bad mar kumta u i'ohi ba kata ka diengi'ap ka raid- u dei u len lum ba la tymmen bha. Dang ha kine ki 50 snem ngi dang i'ohi ia ki 'Sein lyngkani, ki 'sein star, ki seini'ong kiba heh kat tynrai kaitsan bad kiba jrong haduh 16 ft ne. Kine ki pynshisha ia ki jingiathuh ki tymmen ba haduh katno ba ki hap ban Valeh thma pyrshah bad kine ki mrad kynsha: teng teng ki jop bad teng teng ki shah jop bad duh ei la ka jingim. Ki wahrit bad ki wahduid ki dap da ki ser bad ki hiangjule dap tda kiba tang shu i'oh ban dait ki tan lut ia ka snam baroh. Namar ba jur than ki mrad ki mreng, ki khlaw ki dap da ki thliem bad teng teng ki hap nalor ki sla kum ba hap lapraw tang shu sma briew. Ki ktiar, ki nianglartham, ki tyrpud bad ki kyrbei ki par ki shang kylleng khlem jingkhuslai bad u briew u hap ban sumar ban phikir man ba u jam. Thop shi thop ki hap ban i'aleh thma pyrshah ia kine ki jingthaw haduh ba kin da lah hi thiaw ban long ki kynrad jong ka ri War. Dang tang ha ki sngi jong u Shloifi Duwakdar, la Vathuh khana ba ha kawei na ki tyor; la khie artylli ki Mynthna na sai. Ki nongbeh kila ia pyrta- ‘'husiar... husiar”. Hamar kata ka por u Shloifi u i'ohsngew ba ka jingsawa ka wan sha ka phang ba u don, bad u sngewthuh ba u dei u Mynthna. Mar kumta u kiew ha jrong siej. Hynrei hamar ba u dang poi ha shiteng, u Mynthna u la lymbub trait ia u siej uba u kiew. U Shloifi u hap jraifi na jrong siej hamar pyrshah ki reng U Mynthna bad sbak u bat. U Mynthna u her kulmar ia ka khlaw ka btap bad u tur u lymbub 25 naphang hynrei U Shloifi u bat skhem triang khlem pyllait ryngkat ka hala ka pyrta lynter lynti. Ha ka jingphet kulmar u Mynthna u hiar sha bondo ktieh bad mynta um lah mareh shuh ba bat ka jyrsieh ktieh. U Shloin u sei ia ka wait na syngkai bad u siah suki suki la ka ryndang u Mynthna La ong ba hadien bun bun kynta u Mynthna u kyllon kram ha bondo. Ki paitbah nongtyor baroh kila lyngngoh jlang shano U Shloin u don. Ynda kila ia kynkui kila la kynkaw ki sa i’ohsngew ia ka sur jong u jngai bah. Kumta baroh ki ia mareh sha ta ban tip aiu kala jia. Ki lap ba ka ingdong jong u kala shu saw haifi da ka snam suda ba prat ki shiah ki tdew bad une u shong khui ha syndah U Mynthna khlem jain khlem nep ba la shah tar ha lynti. Ynda ki peit la u Mynthna ki lap ia ki dak siah ha u pdot jong u bad mynta ki sngewthuh kumno u Shloin u pynkyllon ia u Mynthna. drain ki ia shad ki ia kyrdem bad ki wan bah bad Mynthna bad Shloifl sha shnong. Ki tymmen ki ju i'athuh khana shaphang kita ki dieng piamstar bad ki jri radbah kiba tang kawei ka tap bun acre ka jaka. Kine kirn don shuh mynta namar ba u briew u la pynkhyllon pynkhyllem ia ki ban pynlong ia ka ri War Shelia, ka Ri u soh u pai; ka Ri jong ka dud bad ka ngap. Wat haduh ki sngi ka jinglong Wahadadar jong U Ksan bad U Mihsnge Ka Lum Pukri, Shken, Nur Suphoi, Sai U Jon, Sai Ka Rap, Diroi haduh ichamuti ki dang long ki kad jong ki khla, ki hati, ki Mynthna, ki Sier, Ki Khiat, Ki Bthong haduh Laiseng, Sai Ka Khan phak haduh Boi-raki. Ki tymmen ki dang iathuh khana shaphang kata ka jingkem hati jong u Raja Gouripore ha ki sngi jong U Mihsnge bad U Ksan Wahadadar: bad kata ka khana ka long kumne - La don ka jingud ka ba jur 26 na ki Nongrep bad ki nongleit bri wan bri ba ki hati ym tang ba ki pynjulor ta ki lyngkha ki risai jong ki, hynrei ki long ka jingma wat ia ka jingim jong ki ruh. U Ksan Wahadadar, ba u ia dei ia jan bad U Raja Gouripore ula pynsngew ia kane ha u. U Raja Gouripore, ba u long uba riewspah; ula kular ban siew Rs. 3000/- ia ka Hima Sheila bad Rs.1000/- ia ki Saw Wahadadar lada u lah ban kem 200 tylli ki hati na ka hima jong ki. U Raja Gouripore ula phah la ki shakri shakor ban leit shna kper bad rynsan ha Lum Pukri ban sdang ia ka jingkem hati. Tang shu dep shna, U Raja Gouripore ryngkat ki hati bad ki mahut kila wan sha Lum Pukri. U Raja bad ki Wahadadar ki shong peitkai kumno ki shakri shakor jong u ki kem ia ki hati. Nyngkong eh ki mahut bad ki shakri shakor U Raja ki i'aleh ban pynrung ia ki artylli ki hati heh hapoh kper: bad tang shu ioh pynrung ia ki, ki kem da kaba suk ia baroh kiwei pat kiba dang sah. La ong ba uwei na kitei ki hati urn treh bam jingbam na ka kti jong ki mahut: katba u bam pat haba ai uwei u khynnah samla na Shala. la kane ka khubor la leit rah sha U Raja bad u Raja ula phah khot Ta uta u samla. Vnda u la tip lut ia ka jinglong duk bad jinglong khunswet jong u, ula khroh ia kiba ha Ting ha sem jong u ban ai noh ia une u khynnah ha u ban ri pooj ne ting-khun ia u namar ba urn don khun na lade. Kiba ha Ting ha sem jong une u khynnah kila soi ia ka kot thied purja bad U Raja ula ai mar 100 tyngka uwei uwei na ki baroh hynriew ngut ki kfii jong uta u khynnah uba kyrteng U Berini. U Raja Gouripore ynda ula dep kem palat 200 tylli ki hati barit bad baheh, u leit phai noh sha la ka jong ka hima ryngkat bad une u khynnah. U Shangai, u kfii jong U Berini u 27 leit jngoh ia u hadien katto katne snem bad u wanrah ka khubor kaba kmen sha la shnong ba U Berini u suk u said bad u im kum U Raja. U shnong u thaw u lyngngoh ban i'ohi ruh ba u Berini u phah jingai sngewbha sha la ki kni bad ki kmie san kmie nah ha Shala. Ka khanatang ka iathuh ba naduh ka por ba u Raja Gounpore ula kem ia kine ki hati ka Ri thor Shala ka lait war na ka jingpynjulor jong ki. Suki suki ki briew ki sdang ban dokhol ia kine ki jaka ban pynlong ia ki, ym shuh ki raieh raidam; hynrei ki brisoh brikwai kiba wanrah ka spah bad ka jingkyrkhu ia ka ri War baroh kawei. V. Ka Trei Ka Ktah Ki Sawkher Sawkuro ki dei ki nongrep. Ki shem ba ka ri War ka long ka ri kaba sboh bad ba seisoh. Ki shyrti ia ki khlaw ki btap bad ki thung ka shriew u phan; ka kait, u syieng, u shynrai, u krai, u hadem bad u ’ba lum. Namar ba ka jaka ka long kaba seisoh ki i'oh kyrhai ka bam ka dih. Tang hapdeng khyndiat snem ki kylla long kiba riewspah bad ba pahuh pahai. Nangta ki ri ki sniang ki syiar, ki blang ki masi bad kumta ter ter. Ha kata ka por ym pat don peisa tyngka ne sbai- ki shu i'a-peifi ia-kylliang. Na ka bynta kane ki thaw kawei ka hat hajan tnad Duwarat kaba ki khot Hat ‘Kaitthang’ ne ‘Ka Hat Pdia’. Ki mar kiba kongsan eh kiba ki Khasi ki shalan ki long u Syieng, Ka kait, U Shynrai bad ka sla tyrpad. Na ki dkhar pat ki i'oh U Khaw, Ka dohkha, Ki jaifi, ki khiew bad kiwei kiwei ki tiar shet tiar tiew bad ki tiar bam tiar dih. Nangta ki shalan ruh ki dieng tokta bad u mawshun. Ka hat Pdia ka kylla long kawei na ki hat 28 kiba donnam hyndai ha kaba ki dkhar ki lyngkien na kylleng ka Bengal ki wan hangne ban ia die ia thied bad ki Khasi. Wat la ka ri War ka long kaba donnam ha ka jingshalan sohniamtra; pynban haduh kata ka por ki Sheila kim pat tip ban thung soh. Ka khana pateng ka i'athuh ba ka jingthung soh ha ri War ka sdang haduh kaba sdang jong ka 18 spah snem, kumba arpateng hadien ka jinghiar thma U Mir Jumla. Ka khana pateng ka i'athuh kumne- ha kaba sdang jong ka 18 spah snem, kata hadien ba ki Shala kila shong shnong hapoh ka jaka u Khang U Saei (Ka shnong Shala kaba mynta), la wan u nongrah khubor na U Trai Kynrad, namar ba synia sngi ki briew ki duwai blei bym don urn, ba ka Bakra ruh ka jngai. Kumta, ha kawei ka janmiet la wanpoi uwei u riewphylla ha Ting ka Wanhat, kmie U Rymbot: kaba sah riewkynthei. Une u briew ula ai ha ka sawhali ki soh tyntra ne ki soh fiiamtra ba kan bam sngewbha bad u khun jong ka. U da bthah ruh ia ka ban kynshew ia ki shyieng bad sara ia ki. Na kine ki sara ka thung kawei ka brisoh ha Khatduria. La ong ba kine ki soh ki san ki plung bad tang hapdeng san snem kila i'oh kheit sohpah bad die ha hat. Katba nangwan ki snem ki nangsan ki nangsei bad ki nang pynmih soh khambun shuh shuh; bad hapdeng shiphew snem ki kylla long ki briew kiba dap kiba kot. Kane ka brisoh kala kylla long ka khana man la ka tnum ling bad baroh baroh ki leit pan symbai sara na ka Wanhat bad U Rymbot. Tang hapdeng 30 snem ne, ka ri war baroh kawei ka kylla long ka ri jong u soh u pai bad ka them jong ka spah bad ka jingkyrkhu. Ha ka step kaba bud u Rymbot ula i'alam ia une u riew- phylla sha ling ki Duwakdar ban pynpaw ha ki ia ka khubor ba phah U Trai Kynrad. “U Trai Kynrad ula Tohsngew ia ka jingud 29 jinglynfiiar jong ki khun ka shnong Shala namar bym don um bad ula phah ia nga ban pynmih um” ong une u riewphylla. "Lada ka burom jong ki Duwakdar ka shah, ngan pynmih um na utei u maw harum Ting jong ka kmie U Rymbot, ” pynkut uta u riewphylla. “la kane phi dei ban rai mynta mynta hi ka sngi namar lashai nga la hap ban leit noh nangne. ” Ki Duwakdar ryngkat ka durbar ha ka jaka ba kin sngewkmen ki bishni pynban ia ka kmie U Rymbot ba ka um kan mih narum Ting jong ka. Te, namar ba ka durbar kam hun ia ka jaka ba ka um kan mih, u nonglam khubor jong U Trai Kynrad ula leit noh. U Rymbot u bud ia u haduh tharia hynrei ha ka shikhyllipmat u shu jah mgai khlem i'ohi shuh. Shuwa ba un jah rngai ula ong kumne ha u Rymbot, “Da kito ki soh tyntra, U Trai Kynrad un kyrkhu ia phi; hynrei to tip naduh mynta ba ka shnong Shala kan ym i'oh um lano lano ruh.” Hynrei kawei kaba pynlyngngoh ia ngi ki longdien ka long kumno ki tymmen mynshuwa ki lah ban trei ban ktah, ban thung ban tep spah shah palat ban ia ka juk kaba mynta? Khlem artatien ki long shisha ki briew kiba smat ba sting bad ba khlaifi ka bor met bor phat: hynrei kaba kongsan tarn ka long ba ki nang kumno ban ia trei lang. Ha ki aVom jong ki ym ju don-nong don-ni, hynrei ki i'eng da ka rom-snge ne ka kylliang sngi. Dei kane ka bor kaba la pynlah ia ki ban pynkhyllem ia ki khlaw bad ban pynlong ki brisoh brikwai. Ki briew ruh ki long kiba dukhi bad ba trei shitom. Ki bam da ki phan ki shriew, ka jakrai jahadem bad bing bing ki trei. U khaw u kba ki ioh tad ynda kila pahuh pahai bad ba kila don ki jingmih ban ia peifl bad ki dkhar ki lyngkien. Kane ka mynsiem rom-snge kala duh noh bad ka jingim shimet ka synshar: ba sa sah khlaw ki brisoh 30 brikwai bad ki lyngkha ki risai. Wat la kane ka juk kala long kham shai bad kham riewbha ban ia ka juk ki kpa tymmen jong ngi; hynrei da lei lei ruh kin nym lah ban trei wat tang shipawa na kaba ki ki trei. III. Ka Synshar shnong Synshar thaw Mynba ki saw kynhun ki wan buhai ia ka Ri War ban pynlong ia ka shnong Nongwar, Shala, Mustoh bad Nongbah: ki rangbah nong'i'alam jong kine ki kynhun hi, ki kylla long ki nongsynshar nongbishar: kiba peit la ka jingkhuid jingsuba jong ka shnong ka thaw; ka rukom thawi'ing thaw sem, ka shong ka sah bad ki nongbthah nongbujai kumno ban shna ki lynti ki syngkieng, ban rep ban riang, ban trei ban ktah ban bha ban miat ka imlang ka sahlang. la ki jaka ki phuta la la bynta hapdeng para ma ki kumno ban rep ban riang bad ban thung ban tep. Kine ki jaka ki phuta suki suki ki kylla long ki ri seng ki ri dang. Ki Rangbah shnong ki peit ba kawei pa kawei ka ling ka rep ka riang khnang ban nym i'apthngan Tap jingit. Nalornangta, ki lynti shnong lynti thaw, ki lynti bri bad ki lynti hat lynti Tew ki dei ban long kiba khuid bad ba la shna bha ba ka iaid ka i'eng kan nym thud la ki jingkieng ki panat ha ki wahrit bad ki wahbah la shna lang da ka shnong ka thaw. Kumjuh ruh ia ki lynti bah la pynkhuid bad pynbha shisien shisnem. Man ka snem ki buh ka adong ba kawei pa kawei ka ling ka dei ban pynkhuid la ki kper ki phrah khnang ba ki bsein ki ktiar, ki mrad ki mreng kin nym wanrung hapoh shnong poh thaw ban long ka jingmynsaw ia ki briew. Ki Tymmen shnong ki bishar ia ki kajia majia baroh bad ki peit ia ka jingsuk jingsaifi jong ka shnong ka thaw. Katkum ba paw, haduh ka snem 1662 kine ki saw shnong ki ia synshar 31 bishar hi shishnong shishnong namar ba ym shym don kano kano ka bor ba halor ka ban teh song lang ia ki hapoh kawei ka jingsynshar. Ki long ki shnong kiba laitluid, kiba rai hi ia la ki kam baroh hapoh shnong. Hapdeng jong kine ki snem la mih ka jingi'akyntur pud, kaba la wanrah ia ka thma Umsanglet hapdeng ki Nongkroh, ki Laiseng bad ki Mustoh ha kawei ka liang pyrshah ia ki Mawlong: namar ba kim lah shuh ban ia pynbeit da ka ktien. Ki Saw shnong ryngkat bad ki Nongkroh ki hiar ha Umnn bad knieh la ki jaka haduh Umsanglet na ki Mawlong. Hadien jong ka jingiasuk la iatang ba ka nur Umsanglet kan long u pud u sam hapdeng ki Mawlong bad ki Nongkroh. Ki Laiseng bad ki Mustoh ruh kila i'asuk noh da kaba buh beit ia ki pud ki sam baroh shilynter. hynrei ka jingiasuk kaba thikna ka wan tad haduh ka por ki Phareng da kaba thung da ki thum bad ki mawpud kiba skhem shilynter. Dei kane ka thma kaba la wanrah ia ka sanglet shilynter ia ka shongkha shongman hapdeng ki Mawlong bad kitei ki shnong. 05 $005 32 Lynnong 2 Ka Pateng Pakit Ki Kpa Tymmen Na Ponishella Katkum ki khana pateng ia kiba la sakhi pynskhem da ki kot Seng Kot Dang ryngkat ki Jai-Pateng naduh Pomshella haduh mynta; la sabut ba ki Saw Kynhun, kata, Ki Shala, Nongwar, Mustoh bad Nongbah: ia kiba la tip pateng kum ki Sheila: ki wan phetwir na Pomshella hapoh ka jingi'alam U Ben U Khrang; U Kait Ka Riah (Shipara); U Khang U Saei bad U Skot, U Anai, U Syrna. Katkum ka tang na Mawhat Pynter, U Ben bad U Khrang ki hiar ban dakhol bad shong shnong ha ka jaka ba ki khnam U Ben ki hap, kata, ha Kalatek, Sarang bad Dilong sha shilliang ka Wah Bakra (Umiam) ban pynlong ia ka shnong Shala; U Khang U Saei ki hiar sha Dirang ban pynlong ia ka Shnong Mustoh; U Kait Ka Riah ki hiar shathie lam sepngi na Mawhat ban pynlong ia ka shnong Nongwar; bad U Skot, U Anai, U Syrna ki hiar shaphang sepngi lam shathie ha Sohbar ban pynlong ia ka Nongbah. Shuwa ban pra sha la ki jong ki jong ki jaka ki pynlong ka kular ha Mawhat ba kin nym ia iehnoh iwei ia iwei pat ha kano kano ka khim ka shipa bad kin i'amir kajuh ka jingmut ha ka imlang sahlang ka synshar ka khadar. Baroh saw kynhun ki don ka jingiadei kaba i'ajan haduh katta katta lyngba ka poikha poiman, ka shongbha ka shongmiat bad kila ia kyrda markylliang lyngba ki thma bad ki jingialeh. Khnang ban pynioh ka jaka kaba Tar bad kylluid ban rep ban riang bad lait na ka jingkhyllep khyllong jong ki nongshun: ki jied la ki jong ki jong ki jaka ban thaw shnong thaw thaw bad pynbiang ki lynti ki syngkieng ban pynTasoh hapdeng jong ki 33 ba ka leit ka wan kan suk bad ka jingVadei Vajan kan kham skhem 1. Ka Pateng U Khrang Ka Pyrdei, para U Khang: U Khrang Ka Pyrdei ki pynkha Ta U Jasow, U Jrem, U KuTa, Ka Lha, Ka Lynnong bad U Noi. Ka Pyrdei ka Tap noh ha Mawmluh (Lumkhluit) shuwa ba kin hiar sha Pynter U Khrang tang bad ki khun ki hiar ban buhai shnong ha Sarang. Ha ka jingiaid dkhar kylleng kylleng U Khrang ula wanrah Ta kawei ka Kharbrahmon bad ula shongkurim la ka Kane kajingleh kala pynsngewsih jur 1a ki khun ba ki sngewlehraih ba U Kpa jong ki u i'oh da ka dkhar. Namar ba um patiaw ia ka jingkren jong ki shisyndon ki mih noh na Sarang ban wanpan jaka na U Saei U Kni jong ki na Mustoh. U Saei um banse ban ai jaka ia la ki pyrsa ha Shiliang Umshynrang arsut haduh Umbyrseh shaduh Tyrsang. U Jasow u jied ia lade ban shong ha Mawlieh bad ka tnga jong u Ka Khylloid. U Not ka Nariang ki jied ia ka pud Mawlong, katba Ka Lha, Ka Lynnong, U Jrem bad U KuVa ki mon ban shong hajan Mustoh. Katei ka dkhar tnga U Khrang ynda ka Vohi ba ki khun- san U Khrang kim sngewbha satia ia ka, ka ruh da ka jingsngewsih ka phetnoh shiteng miet ban leit phai sha la ki Kmie ki Kpa ha Burakhia; hynrei ki pat kim pdiang shuh ia ka ban shong ban sah ryngkat bad ki. Bran U Khrang u shim da ka lieng ban leit sha Burakhia hynrei um lap. Ha ka step ba u mut ban wanphai noh sha Sarang, u i'ohi ia kawei ka samla ba ka shong thawiur harud wah bad ka khaweit kti sha u. Ynda ula poi hajan u lap pynban ba ka dei ka tnga jong u. U Kyntiew ia ka hapoh lieng bad bran u wan sha Sarang: da kaba ai kyrteng Khasi artad ia ka - Ka Wanphai. 34 U Jasow tnga Ka Khylloid ki pynkha ia Ka Tdum tnga U Phalup; Ka Piah, U Phar; U Shaw tnga Ka Roin; bad Ka Kyrsot tnga U Jai'ong. Ka Tdum tnga U Phalup ki pynkha ia U Lwai, U Phyrban, Ka Rod, Ka Lait bad ka Saw. Ka Piah U Phar ki pynkha ia u Kor, Ka Tew bad Ka Sai. Ka Kyrsot U Jaiong ki pynkha ia U Shon, U Jop, Ka Bon, Ka Roifi bad U Dap. U Noi tnga ka Nariang na Mawlong ki mon ban shong ban sah hapud Mawlong bad ki pynkha ia U Jar, U Sor, Ka Sai bad Ka Khapiah. U Jar ka Wanlar ki pynkha ia U Ksanjar, U Beit, Ka Jah, bad ka Thad. Na ki khun ki ksiew U Noi Ka Nariang, tang U Ksanjar u poikha ha Mustoh. U Sor bad Ka Sai ki poikha ha Mawlong. Ka Khapiah ka Tap khynraw ba lymban u maw. Ka Lha ka i'apduh bad ia ka jaka ba ka shong la tip pateng kum ka Shken-Ka-Lha. Ka Lynnong ruh hadien ba ka Tap noh; u tnga jong ka uba na Mawphlang ula i'alam noh ia ki khun baroh sawngut sha Mawphlang. Kaba sah pateng ha ngi haduh mynta ka long tang ka Ri Ka Lynnong. Ki khun U Jrem pat na ka Nong Mawlong; hadien ba u Tap tyrut ha Synrang U Jrem; ki leit shong leit sah noh ha Mawlong. U KuVa pat u Tap duh ba siat U Jasow ba u wantuh na lyngkha mynmiet. U Khrang Ka Wanphai ki pynkha ia ka Ngad tnga U Than, Ka Jyrngoi tnga U Laid, bad U Khylleifi. Ka Ngad tnga U Than ki pynkha ia u Thngan tnga ka Dah, Ka Hat bad Ka Shei. Ka Wanphai ka Tap noh ha ka khlam bah ha Sarang bad U Khrang u poi ha ka lanot khop ban sumar khun rit. Lada um don U Khlor tymmen uba isynei ia U Khrang, lehse ki khun jong u baroh laingut kin jin da la Tap jingit. Ka Jymgei U Laid ki pynkha ia U Botkha, Ka Bon, Ka Sap bad U Biro. U Khylleifi tnga Ka Tangmet ki pynkha te U Jan tnga Ka Lamon, kiba pynkha ia U Miet bad U Bor tng\Ka Patat. U Bor bad Ka Patat ki pynkha ia u Shaw; Ka Phet, U\Ja)'ong bad ia Ka Beh. Ka Phet U JaTong ki pynkha ia U Klor, U Lar3p^0nLar, U Pynbat bad U Khyllein. La ai kyrteng U Khlor ia U Khun Rangbah Ka Phet U JaTong ban pynkynmaw burom la uta U Khlor Tymmen uba la isynei ban Tarap lem ia U Khrang namar ba Tap noh Ka Wanphai ha ka khlam mynba ki khun ki dang rit bad ba ki khun san ki don jngai na u. Dei U Khlor tymmen uba la pynim ia u bad ia ki laingut ki khun rit jong u. Hadien ba U Khrang ula kut jingmut ban nym shong kurim shuh, ula khroh 1 a ki khun san ban wanphai biang sha Sarang. U Jasow kum u khun rangbah u sngewsang ban ieh ia la u jong u kpa bad sa shisien ki leit phai biang sha Sarang. II. Ka Pateng U Bon Ka Shat U Bon tnga ka Shat ki pynkha ia ka Pat, U Behar tnga ka Hat; U Khlor tnga Ka Lamei, U Kui'a tnga Ka Phen, U Roi, U Phan, Ka Hai tnga U Kor; Ka Piet tnga U Shonglaid bad U Bor tnga Ka Siarkom. U Behar Ka Hat ki pynkha ia ka Shong, U Shlan, Ka Ngoi, Ka Jen bad ka Satai U Khlor Ka Lamai ki pynkha ia U Kham, U Bukai, U Sna bad Ka Lar. U Kui'a Ka Phen ki pynkha ia U JaTong, U Jin tnga ka Sdiah, bad U Anai. U Jin Ka Sdiah ki pynkha ia U Kynbna, Ka Saei, Ka Wanswett, U Laid bad U Kmen. Ka Hei tnga U Kor ki pynkha ia U Shah bad U Rkat. Ka Phet tnga U Shonglaid ki pynkha ia Ka No, Ka Sohmen, Ka Shlaitbid. Shaphang Ka Pet, U Roi bad U Phan ngim don jingtip ei ei shaphang ka pateng jong ki. 36 III. Ka Pateng U Khang Ka Shati U Khang Ka Shati ki pynkha ia U Jerkha tnga Ka Beh; Ka Mad tnga U Botkha; Ka Bukma tnga U Shong. U Jerkha ka Beh pat ki pynkha ia Ka Rap, Ka Shympai, Ka Top, U Khang bad U Konrai Ka Beh tnga U Jerkha, dei ka khun U Saei ka Pein. Ba kumta da kane ka jingi'apoi kha poiman ka don ka jingiadei kaba jan bha hapdeng U Khang bad U Saei. Ka Mad tnga U Botkha pat ki pynkha la Ka Lai, Ka Hei bad U Bir U Botkha u dei na Shala bad u shong duh ha Mustoh bad la ki khun haduh kajingi'ap. Ka Bukma U Shong ki pynkha la ka Khain (i'apduh) bad la ka Tohbat tnga U Bnoi. Namar ba u Shong u dei na Mawlong ka leitshong noh ha Mawlong; hynrei ka lapbat pat ka ioh ia U Shong bad ka ioh sawngut ki khun - Ka Khain, Ka Lyngngiar, Ka Buki, Ka Pyllah. U Sonrai u shongkurim ia ka Pyllah bad ki shong ki sah ha Mustoh. IV. Ka Pateng U Saei Ka Pein U Saei u don artnga, Ka Pein bad Ka Mud. Ynda la Tap Ka Pein u shong kurim sa ia Ka Mud. Na Ka Pein u ioh ia U Jin tnga Ka Riah, U Jwat, ka Larmon; Ka Beh tnga U Jerkha bad ka Syad tnga U Du. Na ka Mud pat u ioh ia U Plat tnga Ka Sngin; bad Ka Shong tnga U Boit. U Jin Ka Riah ki pynkha ia U Jer tnga Ka Wantem bad ia ka Wanphet tnga U Rngin. U Jer Ka Wantem ki pynkha ia ka Shong tnga U Kromsoifi bad ia U Jer tnga Ka Roin (U Jer u Tap noh tang shu kha ia u khun uba ar). Ka Wanphet U Rngin pat ki pynkha ia U Shaw tnga Ka Wanphet bad ka Warthma tnga U Ngin. U Jwat tnga Ka Larmon pat ki pynkha ia Ka Wat bad Ka Shong. Ka Syad U Du pat ki 37 pynkha ia U Sit, U Syrma, U Shongwir, Ka Jylliang bad Ka Tangthma U Kynshe Ka Sohmen ki pynkha ia ka Byllin, Ka Pawai, Ka Rtei bad U Bonai. Ka Mud tnga baar U Saei pat ka pynkha ia U Phlet tnga Ka Sngin bad ia Ka Shong tnga U Bait. U Phet Ka Sngin pat ki pynkha ia Ka Bi bad Ka Bishni. Ka Shong U Bait ki pynkha ia U Bonai bad Ka Bakai. V. Ka Pateng U Kait Ka Lynnai U Kait ka Lynnai ki pynkha ia Ka Beit tnga U Syrpai, Ka Ksiam tnga U Rkat bad Ka Ksanshong. Ka Beit U Syrpai ki pynkha ia U Wandat bad Ka Pdah. Ka Ksiam U Rkat pat ki pynkha ia U Don, Ka Pateng, Ka Phai'ong, Ka Konei bad U Noh. Ka pateng U Kait bad Ka Riah (shipara) ka roi bha ha Nongwar, katba ia ka pateng jong ka Ksanshong pat ngim tip namar ba ka shongkha shabar shnong Nongwar. VI Ka Pateng U Skot Ka Snaiwir (Nongbah) U Skot Ka Snaiwir ki pynkha ia U Sit tnga Ka Stem; U Lai tnga Ka Phet bad Ka Wani'ow (i'apduh). U Sit Ka Stem ki pynkha ia U Kyrshir, bad Ka Riah; katba U Lai Ka Phet ki pynkha ia U Jon bad Ka Riangmon. Ka khana pateng ka iathuh ba ka Wani'ow ka shah nguid ha u maw bad ia kane ka jaka la sien haduh mynta mynne Ka Mawngoid. VII. Ka Pateng U Anai Ka Lngam U Anai Ka Lngam ki pynkha ia U Than, Ka Samad bad Ka Wanshong tnga U Kat. U Than u kurim artnga Ka Phin bad Ka Synhiang. Na Ka Phin ki kha U Bonei, Ka Lorkhma bad ka Lngam. Na Ka Synhiang pat kha Ka Lorjong bad Ka Synfiia (namar ba ka kmie jong ka ka Tap noh tang shu kha). Ka 38 Wanshong U Kat ki pynkha ia U Sah, Ka Lasam bad Ka Stepwan. la ka pateng Ka Samad bad U Tangmon ym don jingthoh jingtar satia. VIII. Ka Pateng U Syrna Ka Noh U Syrna Ka Noh ki pynkha ia U Tanghat tnga Ka Wanswetl; U Mon tnga Ka Juna bad Ka Sngap tnga U Snge. U langstep Ka Wanswett ki pynkha ia ka Laitstep, Ka Steplait, U Phai bad U Wankhmah. U Mon Ka Juna ki pynkha ia U Ram, U Pang bad U langmet. Ka Sngap U Snge ki pynkha ia U Shan tnga Ka Laitstep. C5fS)C # 39 Lynnong — 3 Ka Phetmungor bad Ka Sawthyndaw Hadien ba ki Shala kila shong la sah ha Kalatek, Dilong bad Sarang kumba arpateng ne, ka la don ka jingkylla kaba khraw ha ka liang ka synshar khadar ha Bengal. Ki Masulman kila pyntroih thiaw la ka jingsynshar Hindu ha Ri India baroh kawei. U Padsha Aurangzeb, u syiem Mughal; ula kwah ban jop lut ia ka Bengal bad Assam.
