Bad la ki jaka ba tarn na ki com- pound hapoh kut-shnong, ynda thung da ki maw 9. la ki dieng na katei ka kut-shnong ba dang pynsah thymmai, uno uno uba leit thaw Ting; un da siew dor; namar ba ki long ki dieng kiba ieh bad sumar sorkari da u Sande. 10. la ki i'ing, ki lynti, ki dieng bad ei ei katba don kam hapoh kut-shnong; yn khmih ne pynbeit shisien shisnem. 1 1 . la katei ka kular (barim) bad ia kane ka jingpynbeit lah ban pynbeit ne pyndap ktien pat hadien ha kano kano ka por, da kaba ia mon lang kum U Sande. la kane ka jingpynbeit ne jingpyndap la pdiang tylli da ka durbar bad ba la sign da baroh ki Headmen ha ka 6 tarik, March, 1926. 92 v) Kl DEWANI BYM LAH RAI Kawei pa kawei ka Hima Khasi ka pdiang ia ka bishar blei kum kawei na ki atiar bishar haba ka bishar briew kam kot ryni'eng shuh. Hynrei tang ka Hima Sheila ka bym pdiang ia ka bishar blei, laitnoh tang ka smai ka kiria. namar ki shem ba hadien ba ki briew kila buh la ki phan ki kyrpat; ka dor jong ka bishar blei ka lip ba ki phan ki kyrpat ki bah: namar ba ki nongri nongdup jong ki phan ki kyrpat ki dawa ba kila i'oh hukum na u blei ban leh kumta. Ka jingbishar kam hok shuh namar ba ki ‘lei shnong ‘lei thaw kim lah shuh ban tukla namar ba ma ki hi ki don ka jingiadei bad kitei ki phan ki kyrpat. Ba kumta la ka hok la tep la buhrieh noh ba ki kyrsan kyrbah kita ki phan ki kyrpat. Ha ka hamsaia ka hima Sohra la i'athuh ba ka Ngam-um bad ka khalai wait ki long ki ar ki jingbishar blei ba kyntang. Hynrei kine ruh ki duhnoh namar ki shem 1a kajuh ka jingshem kaba ki Sheila ki shem. Ha ki sngi kiba khatduh ka hima Sohra ka pdiang tang ka bam - smai ha kano kano ka jingmudui kaba ym don sakhi satar. Ki suit ki shor ha U ‘Lei muluk u Lei jaka ba uno uno uba smai bymhok un kit hi la ka pap bad uba smai ia ka hok un foh hi la ka hok. Ka kyntien smai kiria ka long ka kyntien kaba shyrkhei hapdeng ki War Shelia namar ki tip ba lada ki smai bymhok kan bam kylla la ka ryni'eng ka ryni'ot ka Ting ka sem. U shnong u thaw u suit u shor ryngkat u klong u skaw, u khnam ka ryntieh, ka i'adum ka i'adrod ha u ‘lei pyndem u 'lei duwan: ba uno uno uba len uba kiat ia ka jingshisha un kyllon kumba dung sniang. La i'athuh khana da ki tymmen ba la don shisien kawei ka briew ha Nongwar kaba smai ha pyndem duwan ba lada ka 93 kren ia ka lamler kan Tap da Teng ha syndah rishot. La ong ba shisha kata ka briew, namar ba ka smai lamler; ka Tap da Teng shisha ha syndah u rishot. Kila don shibun ki Ting ha Ri War kiba la smai bymhok tang ban da rapjot la ka burom, bad baroh kila mad la ka apot bipot bymhok. Ha ka Hima Sheila ka don sa kawei ka rukom bishar ia ki mokotduma dewani bym lah pynkut bad kata ka long da kaba ki arliang mamla ki ia pynmih kyrtong ban i'akhun. Namar ba ki aift jong ka Hima Sheila ki long kiba pyrkhing; la shah ia ki arliang mamla ban pynmih kyrtong da ki dkhar ym da ki khun ka Sheila Conferederacy. la kane ki ju leh ha madan Porkan bad kano kano ka liang kaba jop ka kam bad dokhol ia kato ka jaka ba i'aleh mokotduma khlem don jingdawa manhani ei ei. Dei namar kata ka daw ki riewspah na Shala bad Mustoh ki ri ia ki dkhar bad ai jaka rep jaka riang ia ki bad kiba kloi ban pynmih kyrtong ha kano kano ka por. vi) KA JINGLONG TRAI SHNONG Ha ka hima Sheila ki don arjait ki nongshong shnong. Ki Trai shnong bad Ki Shong Thap. Ki Shong Thap ki dei tang ki dkhar ki kliang kiba shu wan shong pur shong bylla bad ki bym don hok don iktiar ei ei ha ka kam shnong ka kam thaw ne kam hima sima; kiba ia ki lah ban beh noh ha kano kano ka por ne, haba ki trai jaka kim ai jaka shuh ia ki ban shong ban sah. Hynrei ki Trai Shnong, ki long ki trai muluk ki trai jaka, kiba Toh ia ki hok ki bynta baroh hapoh ka Hima. Ban long U Trai Shnong, la pynskhem ia u da kine ki jingshisha - (a) Ba la kha ia u na ki kmie ki kpa ba hiarpateng na ki saw-hynhun Saw-Kuro - U Ben U Khrang, U Kait Ka Riah, U Khang U Saei bad U Skot, U Anai U Syrna, U Ei U Noi. (b) U Nongwei ne ka 94 Nongwei lada ki poikha poiman bad u ne ka briew jong kane ka Hima, haba kila don khun don kti: na ki khun ki kylla long ki trai shnong jong kane ka Hima. Kaba pynskhem bad bat pynrkhing bha ia ka jinglong trai shnong dei ki bri ki khyndew bad ka jinghiar pateng na ki Seng. Ki khun ki ksiew jong ka Hima Sheila, kampher la ki shong shnong hangno hangno ruh ki long hi ki trai shnong jong ka Hima Sheila bad ki don ki juh ki hok ha ka imlang ka sahlang, ka synshar ka khadar. Kum ka jingpynbeit ryntih ha ka synshar shnong synshar thaw; ki shnong ki thaw ki ju pynkhuid ne seng lynti shisien ne arsien shisnem: u trai shnong la u don hangno hangno ruh, ka shnong ka bat bad phah pynkhuid ia ki bri ki khyndew jong u (ki lynti) ne u hap ban siew kuna ne shah shop baisngi ha ka durbar shnong. la kane u dei ban siew ha ka miat ba la buh haba ka durbar kala pyntip lym kumta ka kuna kan long arshah. Lada jia urn shah shkor pat ia kane, ka durbar ka lah ban lilam ia kato ka bri ka khyndew. Hynrei kum u trai shnong pat u i'aleh hi ban pynbiang ia ka jingdawa ka durbar. Hynrei lada jia pat ba uno uno uba shong nongwei bad uba kwah ban pyllait noh ia la ka jinglong trai shnong; u dei ban da ai da ka jingthoh kaba shai bad siew ia ka bai pyllait shnong katba ka durbar ka oh dor. Na ka bynta ki bri ki khyndew bad ki kam seng kam dang u dei ban buh da u briew uba thikna uba ka shnong ka lah ban kern lada u pynkhein ia ki hukum shnong. Kum kane koit kam ju kham jia namar ki kheifl sang ban duh la ka hok jinglong trai shnong. la ki Nongwei bar llaka ba wan shong bylla ha ki shnong hapoh ka Hima Shelia, ki lah ban long trai shnong lada ki leh thikna ha ki kam shnong kam thaw bad kitkhia ha ki kam adong shnong baroh. 95 Lada jia ba ki Tapoi kha poiman bad u ne ka briew jong kine ki shnong bad haba kila don khun: na ki khun ki kti ki kylla long trai shnong jong kata ka shnong ba ki shong ki sah. Kaba khampher na ki rukom fiiew trai shnong, dei ka jingi'adei seng ha Laiseng: namar tang ki nonghiar pateng jong u Kynta, U Nabein bad U Tangrai ki long kiba i'oh hok ioh bynta ha Laiseng. Naduh ba la khang apot ia ki Mawlong na ki daw pynkheifi riti jong ki, tang ki khun ki ksiew jong kitei ki lai kiba shong basah ha Nongwar, Mustoh, Nongkroh bad Tyrna ki long kiba i'oh hok i'oh bynta ha Laiseng. vh) KA HIMA SHELLA BAD KA HIMA KHATSAWPHRA U Dr. Homiwell Lyngdoh ha ka kot jong u “Ka History Ki Syiem Khasi bad Synteng’’ ula kynthoh ba ka Hima Shell shisien ka la long ka bynta jong ka Hima Nongkhlaw. la kane ka jingthoh la kye mynjur bad pynbud mawsawa da u Dr. Hamlet Bareh Ngapkynta bad kiwei ki nongthoh ba hadien, khlem da wad ia ka thymmei jingshisha; la ka long ne em kumta. Ki batai hana, ba ha ka kyntien Khatsaw-phra ka kynthup ia ka Hima Sheila. Ka Hima Shelia ka don 23 shnong haduh ka snem 1 724. Nangta ka kylla long noh ka Hima 1 2 shnong haduh ka snem 1 870 bad ka Hima ki 9 shnong hadien ka 1870. Katkum ka history Khatsawphra ka mut ka Hima ki Khatsaw Kur bad 8 Lyngdoh: ki bym don jingi'adei ei ei ruh em bad ka Hima ki 23 shnong ne Hima Sheila. Ki record kiba don ha ka Hima 23 shnong ki i'athuh ba dei ha ka por ka jingsynshar ki 4 duwakdar - U Bor, U Steifi, U Kynshe bad U Jerkha ba la don ka thma hapdeng U Basan Swer bad u Basan Nongkseh. U Basan Swer bad U Buhsing Lyngdoh kila shah jop bad kila pheti’ap sha ki thaift Laitsohpdiah bad Mawshbuit. U Laitlyngka syiem Nongkhlaw, ula shim kabu 96 ia kane ka jingshem lanot jong ki bad ula hiarthma ia ka Kyntursniang bad ka Raij Khatar-blang Khatar-shnong. Nangta u behthong ia U Basan Swer bad U Buhsing Lyngdoh na Laitsohpdiah bad Mawshbuit. Ha ka kyrduh lad khak, U Basan Swer bad U Buhsing Lyngdoh kila pheti'ap sha Pyrkew Dewsaw, kawei na ki Sande ka Hima 23 shnong. U Sande ka Pyrkew Dewsaw ula pan jingmut na ki Duwakdar halor kane ka kam bad la pynsngewthuh ia U ba ka Hima ki 23 shnong ka dei ban i'eng pdeng bad bym dei ban lushia ne tuklar ia ka kam jong kiwei pat ki Hima kumba la long pateng la pateng ka nojir jong ka Hima. Ki Rangbah U Sande Dewsaw ki wan Vathuh ia kane ka khubor da kaba sngewsih ha U Basan Swer bad U Buhsing Lyngdoh. Hynrei hapdeng jong kane ka sohsat, U Sande Nongsteng u tyrwa mon sngewbha ban iada ia ki na ka kti jong u Laitlyngka. Kane ka jingleh kala pynbitar lep ia U Laitlyngka bad shisyndon u pynbna thma pyrshah ia ki Nongsteng bad u ai hukum ia ki laingut ki rangbah shipai jong u - U Ramdat, U langjoit bad U Syrtet ban tur laidong bad khyllep ia ka shnong Nongsteng, na shatei, na mihngi bad shatei lam sepngi bad u Ramdat bad ka kynhun kin risa kum ka dak laisien laiwat shuwa ban fiiom ia ka shnong Nongsteng. U Ramdat bad U Jathiat kin tur ia ka Nongsteng na shaphang shatei lam sepngi; katba U langjoit bad U Syrtet kin tur na shaphang shatei bad mihngi. Ha kane ka jingi'aid lynti, ka kynhun U Ramdat ka wanpoi haduh neng shnong Tynger; bad ki da ngeit ruh ba ka dei ka shnong Nongsteng. Te, namar ba la sdang dum kila rieh noh ia lade hapoh artylli ki mawbah da kaba ki thmu ban hiarthma mynstep. Ki Tynger mardor ki leit 1'ashem ia ki Duwakdar bad phah briew haman la ki shnong. 97 Jrain ki rang kiengwait kiengstieh ki hiar sha Dewsaw bad Tynger shimiet shimiet ban i'ada na u Nongthom bor. Ka khanapateng ka i'athuh ba dei ha kata ka miet ba ki Tynger ki suit ki shor ha u Klor bad pynbam nia pyrshah ia kane ka jingthmu dusmon jong U Laitlyngka. La ong ba ha kata ka miet kala don ka jingslap bad jingkhih eri'ong kaba jur. Baroh ki kynthei khynnah ki phetrieh sha Dewsaw bad sha ki krem ki kroh ha ki bri ki bsah kylleng; lait tang ki Rangbah kiengwait kiengstieh kiba ap pahara ia ka shnong. La ong ba U Klor, ha kata ka miet u la pynkhih ia uwei na kita ki mawbah ha kiba ka kynhun U Ramdat ka sah bad ula ban ia baroh kiba don hangta. Kane ka jingjia kala pynkyndit thret ia u Ramdat bad ynda ula khan ha ka shanam, u lap shisha ba kata ka shnong kaba u thmu ban hiarthma kam dei satia ka Nongsteng. Kumta, shimiet shimiet ryngkat ka kynhun kaba dang lait im, ki wanphet haduh kawei ka madan kaba ngi tip pateng haduh mynta kum ka madan Jathiat ne ka Pyndem Jathiat. Tang shu shai phngoit mynstep bran ki her sha Nongsteng lyngba ki riat ki ram. la u Maw uba la lymban ia ki paid u Ramdat la tip pateng haduh mynta kum u Mawban Nongphlang ne U Mawngat Nongphlang: bad ia u maw pat ha uba U Ramdat u sahmiet la tip pateng kum U Maw Ramdat: ban sakhi ia kane ka jingjia ba shisha kaba la jia ha ki khnong ki khriang ka history.U langjoit bad U Syrtet ruh ki ngat ka juh ka apot ha Wah Umi'am. Bun na ka kynhun ki Tap jyllop ha kawei ka jaka kaba la tip pateng kum ka Workhyllek. Kiba dangsah na kine ki kynhun ki tur beit beit pyrshah ka shnong Nongsteng. Ynda la poi ha ki khyrdop jong ka shnong Nongsteng U Ramdat bad ka kynhun jong u kila risa kynhoi laisien laiwat kumba la iakut. Uwei u briew na 98 Nongsteng ula pyrkhat ba kata ka jingkynhoi ka dei jong ki kur jong u na Mawtap kiba wan ban Tarap ia ki Nongsteng. Bran ula plie ia ka khyrdop bad mar kumta u shah mait ha shen. Ka jingi'aleh kala long kaba jur bad ki Nongsteng kila duh hynriew khlieh. U Syrtet bad U Tangjoit ruh ki tur lang bad ki Nongsteng kim lah kyrda shuh bad bran ki phet rieh shapoh khlaw. Ki Khatsawphra ki rung hapoh shnong bad ki lute katba don. Te, namar ba ki Nongsteng ki siat tuh ia ki na ki jaka rleh, kim nud satia ban sah hapoh shnong. U Ramdat u hukum ban thangsaifi ia ka shnong baroh kawei. Ynda la dep thangsaifi, jar jar ki khreh ban mih noh na shnong bad leit sahmiet sha kawei ka jaka phlang haneng shnong. Ki Rangiapom Nongsteng kiba ap syntiat shilynter ka khlaw ryngkat ki jingshai tit ha ki stieh jong ki sia ki bud nadien. Ka kynhun Khatsawphra ka bym phohsniew ei ei ba ki Nongsteng ki bud syntiat, ki jied ia kawei ka madan ban sahmiet. Ynda la palat shiteng syni'a ki Nongsteng ki par sor sha ka ktem buh tiar thma jong ki bad knieh lut ia ki bad ki da mait naphang katba i'oh. hja ka jingdum ki khatsawphra ki phet Tap phet sakma, hynrei ki Nongsteng ki buddien thop. Tang shu shai plait ki kynrup bad mait kat ia uba ki ia kynduh. Ka Pam-Ramdat, ka Pam-Syrtet bad ka Pam- Tangjoit ryngkat ki mawlong ha kiba ki shan bad kyllong Tap; kin Tai sakhi pateng la pateng ba hangne ki Radbah U Laitlyngka ki kyllon ha ka syrti waitlam ki Nongsteng. la kiba lait ki beh thong bad ki khang kdong ha kawei ka riat bad ki pyni'ap lut khoit ia ki hangta; laitnoh tang ia U Pdah; kata ruh hadien ba kila siah ia ka khmut, ot ia ki shkor bad rymmiang shyntur bad shaifi ia ki shympriah kti shympriah kjat jong u: ba un leit Tathuh ha la ki kur ki kha bad u syiem u 99 Kmie ia ka bor bad jingkhlaift ki Nongsteng. Ki da ai artad ka khubor jingmaham ba lada ki kwah ban hiarthma ia ki Nongsteng kin khreh u paid shipyrha u krai; lym kumta baroh kin mad ia kajuh ka sohsat. la ki metiap jong kito baroh kiba shah khrai la bret ha ‘Noh-khynriam’: ban puramit pateng la pateng ba ki Khatsawphra kim shym Toh jaka ban i'uh kjat ha ka hima ki 23 shnong. Ym slem hadien kane ka thma, U Laitlyngka: katba u dangi'aid pyniar hima sha ki thain Laitsohpdiah, ula snah pynTap ha la ki jong ki kynum namar ba u leh beih ia ka para jong ki. Haduh mynta ki sin ia ki Ngapkynta "ki Ngapkynta pynTap kynum ne ki Ngapkynta pom kynum" bad kane ka jingjia kala long ha ka snem 1 731 , bad ka jingpymar hima ki Khatsawphra ka kut hangne. U Basan Swer bad U Buhsing Lyngdoh, da ka jmgi'arap ki Nongsteng kila Toh biang ia ka Kyntursniang bad raij 12 blang khatar shnong; hynrei kim shlan shuh pat ban buhai ha Kyntursniang ba ki tieng ia U Basan Nongkseh bad U Basan Nong-Umlong. Da ka jingi'asngewthuh jingmut bad ki Nongsteng ki tei ia la ka Nongbah ha Weiser. Ba kumta, nadun ka snem 1731 ym shym don sakhi satar ban pynsabut ba ki Khatsawphra ki dang kyntur jaka pyrshah ia ka Hima Sohra ne ka Hima 23 shnong. la ka Mawmluh bad Sohrarim ruh ki da thied da ka dor ban pynshong pynsah ia ki nongbylla kit nar: kiba kit nar na Synrang Jyrteh sha Padua ne na Synrang Jyrteng sha Kamrup. Don ruh katto katne ki Nongthoh kib3 pyni'sng n>a ba hana, ia ka hima Shelia la synshar da ki Syiem Sohthyndaw kaba long kawei na ki kpoh syiem jong ka Hima Nongkhlaw 100 bad ki ong ba kane ka kpoh kala duh jait la slem. Kane ka dei tang ka pynkut ma syndet kaba ym lah ban pynTeng nongrim la, na ka history ne ki khana pateng ne ka hiarpateng. Ka history ka Tathuh ba ka Sawthyndaw ka dei ka Soskular (quadriple alliance) hapdeng ki Mawlong, Ki Sawseng, ki Syiemlieh Mawmluh bad ki Syiem long Nongspung ha ka snem 1662-63 ha ka thma Phetmungor. la kane ka soskular la pynlong ha U Lum Baniang bad ka duwan Sawthyndaw ka dang sakhi haduh mynta: ban i'aleh pyrshah ia ki Mughal hapoh ka jingialam U Mir Jumla, uba thmu ban hiarthma ia ka ri Khasi bad uba la sher dara ha Lum Pukri bad Ichamuti. Ki Sheila, naduh ba ki wanphet na Pomshala; mynta kumba arphew pateng ei ei, kim shym la ju shah jop ne shah synshar hapoh uno uno u syiem. Ki Khanapateng bad ki jingthoh jingtar ki sakhi ruh ba ka hima 23 shnong ia kaba la seng ha Shyrten ha ka snem 1662-63 kam shym la ju shah jop thma hano hano ruh: lait noh haduh ka jingwan ki phareng 1828-1839. ossoos 101 Lynnong: 5 Ki Seng Ki Dang Hadien ka thma pyrshah ki Syiemiong, ki Saw kynhun ki pynlong ka durbar pyllun ha Mawhat Pynter: kata, shuwa ba kin shim la la ki jong ki jong ki bynta ban buhai bad ban shong ban sah. Ki Rangbah nongi'alam ki smai madan ba ha kane ka ri kaba thymmai - kajingsuk, jingiaryngkat bad jinglaitluid kan synshar bad suhsieng lynter. Baroh kin i'oh la ki jaka ki phuta bad kin trei kin ktah da ka jingkylluid mynsiem bad jingkmen. Ki kular ban kynther dewmpt ia baroh ki rukom rim kiba teh ba khum bad pynlong mraw shilynter 1a ki; da ki rukom ba thymmai: kiba pher bak Ibak na kiba ju long. Da kawei ka jingmut ki iakut lang ba ha kane ka ri kaba kin buhai ka Iyer jong ka jingiaryngkat, ka jinglaitluid bad jingbym ia fiiew shiliang khmat ha ka imlang sahlang, ka synshar ka bishar bad ka trei ka ktah kan beh pynngad shilynter. Bunsien ia kane ka kyntien ‘Seng’ la sngewthuh bakla da kiba bun, namar ba kim pei la ka jingmut ba tynrai jong ka. Katkum ka jingmut jong ki War Sheila, ka kyntien Seng ka mut ka jingi'asyrdoh lang jong baroh shikpoh kiba hiar pateng na u juh u sohpet u shynnai U Kparad ka Kmierad tymmen: kiba don ka juh ka hok i'oh pateng ia ki khyndew ki shyiap bad ki kamai kajieh jong kitei ki tymmen: kampher la ki hiarpateng na ka liang kynthei ne liang shynrang. la kawei pa kawei ka kpoh kaba hiarpateng la tip ia ka kum 'Ka tnad’ bad baroh ki tnad ki pynlong ia ka Seng. Dei kane kaba la pynpher bak Ibak ia ki na kiwei pat ki para khun Khasi Khara ha ka liang ka i'oh 102 pateng hiarpateng katkum ki du$tur ki riti jong ki War Sheila baroh ki khun ki waris (kynthei bad shynrang) ki i'oh ka juh ka hok i'oh pateng. Namar kata, haba ki tnad kila i'ar bad roi pait la donkam ban don ka Seng ka ban pyrkhat ban bishar ha kano ka rukom yn phiah yn bynta ia ka hok jong kitei ki tymmen ha la ki tnad ki tnad. Katba ym pat pynlong seng: kitei ki khyndew ki shyiap ki dang sah Ri Seng, bad haba kitei ki tnad baroh ki ia shong durbar la khot ia kata ka durbar - Ka ‘Durbar Seng’, la ki nongmihkhmat kiba ka Tnad ka da jied ban leit mihkhmat sha ka Durbar Seng ki khot ‘Ki Tymmen Seng’: Katba ia ka ling jong ka hynmen-san kaba shong ha Ting - tymmen ki khot ‘Ka ilngseng’ bad ia u hymmen rangbah ki khot 'U Nongsaid’. la ki kynthei ki khot ‘Ki Kur’ katba ki shynrang ki dei ‘Ki Kni’. Ka hynmensan bad u hynmen rangbah ki long kiba donbor ban korbar ia ka Ting ka kpoh ne ka Seng ka dang. i) Ka Jaipateng ha ki Seng ki dang Ban long ki khun seng jong kano kano ka seng dei ban tip ia la ka pateng bad ka kpoh nangno ki hiar bad ki hap ban jai ne pynhiar pateng ia lade na kata kata ka tnad. Hapdeng jong ki War Sheila, ki don ar rukom ki jingiadei na ka jait, kaba mut na ka jingiadei Seng lang ne ba 1a i'oh hok i'oh bynta lem na kajuh ka Seng “Rai Shyieng bad Rangliang” na ka ‘Kur’ pat ka mut - na kajuh ka kpoh Rai Shyieng jong ka kmie. Dei hangne ba ki nongthoh kiba mynshuwa ki sngewthuh bakla ba ki War Sheila kirn don jait (kaba ha ka jingmut jong ki ki mut ba kim don Kur); kane ka long kaba bakla. Shipara khun seng ki ia kam jait. Katba ka kur pat ka hiar pateng tang na ka liang jong ka kynthei. Ka jinghiar pateng na ka liang jong ka kur ka long tang na ka liang ka kynthei (Rai Shyieng) kumba long lem 103 ki para Khasi khara; katba ka jinghiar pateng ha ka jait rte ka Seng pat ka long na baroh arliang: Rai Shyieng bad Rangliang kata, na ka kynthei bad na u shynrang kumjuh. Baroh ki nonghiar pateng na ki khun kynthei bad shynrang jong kitei ki tymmen ki long ki trai seng bad ki I'oh ia kajuh ka hok ka bynta ha ka Seng. Ka jingi'apher bad kiwei pat ki para Khasi ka long ba ki shynrang jong ki kim ju i'oh hok i'oh thana ei ei ha la iing; katba ki War Sheila ki i'oh kajuh ka hok ka bynta ha ki khyndew ki shyiap la, ha la ka iing kmie Ting kpa ne ha ka Seng ka dang. Kane ka jinglong ka pyni'apher bak Ibak ia ki na ki Khasi Khynriam, Khasi Pnar ne Khasi Bhoi: kiba long tang ki shongthap shongshipor ha iingkur ne tang u ‘sikpa ha Ting tnga. Hapdeng ki War Sheila U Shynrang u long u trai ha iingkur ne ha iing la jong; bad u i'oh ka kyrdan kaba kham halor la ha iingkur ne ha iing la jong. Kane ka long namar ba u don ka hok kaba mar ia ryngkat ia ha iingkur ne ha iing la jong. U shynrang u long u Tymmen Seng na la ka kpoh ha la ka Seng ka dang; kaba ka kynthei kam lah: namar ka synshar ka bishar ka kynih ka phawar ka dei tang ka jong u rangbah. Ha iingkur pat u long u nongsaid u nongbah khala ia la ka iing ka sem bad na ka bynta kane u i'oh ia ka hok ka bynta kum u nongsaid. Namar kata, wat ki bri ki khyndew bad ki iing ki sem kiba u i'oh u kamai bad la ka tnga ki long ki jong ki khun. U, lymne ka tnga jong u kim lah ban leh trai khlieh halor kine ki kamai kajieh khlem ka jingi'a mynjur lang: namar baroh arngut ki trei namar la ki khun. Haba kumta, kumno ki War Sheila ki jaipateng ha la ki Seng ki Dang ? Shuwa ba ki kpa tymmen kin i'uh kjat ha War Shelia ki pynlong kane ka jingi'akut ba kyntang ha Mawhat, ba 104 ka ri ha kaba kin shong kin sah kan long ka ri ha kaba laitphar na ka jingbanbein bad ka jinglongmraw; ka ri ha kaba ka jingiaryngkat para briew bad jinglaitluid kan synshar. Bad shynrang bad kynthei ki i'oh hok i'oh bynta lang mar kumjuh ha ki khyndew ki shyiap. Halor kane ka nongrim ki rai ba ki khyndew ki shyiap baroh kin long ki jong u paitbah ym jong u shimet armet ne jong ka kpoh ka kynja. Dei halor kane ka nongrim ba sa mih ki seng ki dang; kiba ka rukom pyni'aid ka i'apher bak Ibak na baroh ki rukom pyni'aid khyndew pyni'aid shyiap hapdeng ki Khasi kiba shong ha Bhoi, ha Pnar ne ha ri Lum. Kane ka long ka nomuna kumno ki War Sheila ki jai bad ki hiar pateng ha la ki Seng ki Dang; bad kino kino ki bym lah ban jai ia la ka jong ka pateng ha kano kano ka Seng ki duh hok duh bynta. Bad kino kino pat kiba kam seng bymhok khlem tip ia ka jinghiar pateng ka jor ka snam; ki duh jait duh kynja, duh i'ing duh kur - haba ki tymmen seng ki pynkren hok da ka smai ka kiria. Namar kata, ki briew ha War Sheila ki buh ia la ki pateng pakit ba ki khun ki waris jong ki pateng la pateng kin nym kma nym kwit na la ka jymbuin u sohpet. Kane ka long ka jaipateng seng kumno ba ki don ka jingi'adei iasnoh bad kitei ki kpa tymmen kmie tymmen kiba wanhiar na Pomshala ban buhai ha ri War - a) Ka Pateng U Khang Ka Shati na Mustoh U Khang shitnga Ka Shati ki pynkha ia U Jerkha, Ka Mat, bad Ka Bukna. U Jerkha shitnga Ka Beh (Khun U Saei Ka Peifi) ki pynkha ia ka Rap, Ka Shymphai, Ka Jap, ka pynkha ia ka Wanphet bad u Sanrai. U Sanrai shitnga Ka Pyllah ki pynkha ia U Suna, U Jerkha, U Don bad Ka Lar. U Suna shitnga Ka Bishni ki pynkha ia Ka Bamon, Ka langrai bad Ka Tapbat. 105 Ka Bamon shitnga U Joh (na Nongbah) ki pynkha ia U Dwan, U Monsing, U Jitrai bad Ka Mihsnge. Ka Mihsnge shitnga U Hon ki pynkha ia Ka langrai, Ka langthma, Ka Kseh bad U Jitrai (bym kit apot). Ka langrai shitnga U Ksanieng ki pynkha ia U Botsing, U Kuhai bad Ka Don. U Kuhai shitnga Ka Siarmon ki pynkha ia Ka Lang, U Kham, U Ronsing bad U Subasing. U Subasing shitnga Ka Swet ki pynkha ia U Borjodhon. (U Subasing U Kurim artnga Ka Swet bad Ka Keneris). Na ka Keneris kha ia U Tiengred. U Borjodhon kurim artnga i) Ka Kini kaba pynkha ia Ka Twil bad Ka Swil (Tula) ii) Na Ka Shri kha U Rasmohon, U Oltoma, U Har (iapduh), Ka lensiar bad U Habasing. Ka lensiar shitnga U Wendli Wriah ki pynkha la U Besjo, U Shosing, Ka Bethel, Ka Limeri bad U Phistar (Wanswett). b) Ka Pateng U Jin Ka Riah (Na Nongwar) U Saei shitnga Ka Peih ki pynkha ia U Jin, U Jwat, U Kynshe, Ka Beh bad Ka Syat. U Jin shitnga Ka Riah ki pynkha ia U Ker bad Ka Wanphet. Ka Wanphet shitnga U Rngin (na Sawthyndaw) ki pynkha ia U Shaw bad ka Wanthma. Ka Wanthma shitnga U Ngun (na Ramdait) ki pynkha ia U langhat bad U Rymboh. U langhat shitnga ka Shandikhen (Na Nongtrai) ki pynkha ia U Khut, U Amor bad Ka Koniang. Ka Koniang shitnga U Bosan ki pynkha ia U Ron, U Sing, U Nojor bad Ka Weng. U Nojor shitnga ka langsngi ki pynkha ia U Syntew, U langhat, Ka Lan, Ka Tibon bad ka Stem. Ka Tibon shitnga U Ram ki pynkha ia U Kron, U Khang, Ka Shap, U Jor bad U Sing (iapduh) U Khang shitnga Ka Siarbon ki pynkha ia Ka Shan, U Rai bad Ka Swet. Ka Swet shitnga U Subasing ki 106 pynkha ia U Borjodhon. U Borjodhon shitnga Ka Shri ki pynkha ia U Rasmohon, U Oltoma, U Har (iapduh), Ka lensiar, bad U Habasing. Ka lensiar shitnga U Wendli Wriah ki pynkha ia U Besjo, U Shosing, Ka Bethel, Ka Limeri bad U Phistar. k) Ka Pateng U Anai Ka Lngam (Nongbah) U Anai shitnga Ka Lngam ki pynkha ia U Than, U Shanwon, bad U Wanshong. U Than kurim artnga i) Ka Phin kaba pynkha ia U Bamei, U Lorthma bad Ka Lyngam. (ii) Ka Shanieng kaba pynkha ia U Larjang bad Ka Shaniong. Ka Lyngam kurim artnga i) U pang uba pynkha ia U Than bad U Pang ii) U Ron uba pynkha ia U Snge. U Than shitnga Ka Wanswett ki pynkha ia U Jor, Ka Joh, U Jitrai bad Ka Wanswett. (la ka bynta U Jitrai kit apot ka Wanswett bad ia ka bynta Ka Joh kit apot U Jon). U Jon shitnga Ka Bamon ki pynkha ia U Duwan, U Mansing, U Jitrai bad Ka Mihsnge. Ka Mihsnge shitnga U Mon ki pynkha ia ka langrai, Ka larigthma bad Ka kseh. Ka langrai shitnga U Ksanieng ki pynkha ia U Botsing, U Kuhai bad Ka Don. U Kuhai shitnga Ka Siarmon ki pynkha ia U Kham, U Raimanik bad U Ronsing. U Kham shitnga KaTewdiar ki pynkha ia U Subasing. U Subasing shitnga Ka Swet ki pynkha ia U Borjodhon. U Borjodhon shitnga Ka Shri ki pynkha ia U Rasmohon, U Oltoma, U Har (iapduh), Ka lensiar bad U Habasing. Ka lensiar shitnga U Wendli Wriah ki pynkha ia u* Besjo, U Shosing, Ka Bethel, Ka Limeri bad U Phistar. d) Ka pateng U Skot Ka Ryiah (Na Nongbah) U Skot shitnga Ka Ryiah ki pynkha ia U Sit, U Lei bad ka WanVow. U Sit shitnga Ka Stem ki pynkha ia Ka Riah bad U Kynshing. Ka Riah shitnga U Hon (uba na ka kpoh Ka Phar 107 U Kynsheng na Nongwar) Ki pynkha ia Ka Shongthma, U Pyrde bad U Man. Ka Shongthma shitnga bad U Ksanjar ki pynkha ia U Ksan, U Borkha bad U Hon. U Hon shitnga Ka Mihsnge ki pynkha ia ka langrai, Ka langthma bad ka Kseh, Ka langrai shitnga U KsanVong ki pynkha ia U Kuhai, U Botsing bad ka Don. U Kuhai shitnga Ka Siarmon ki pynkha ia U Kham, U Raimanik, U Ronsing bad Ka Lang. U Kham shitnga Ka Tewdiar ki pynkha ia U Subasing. U Subasing shitnga Ka Swet ki pynkha ia U Borjodhon. U Borjodhon shitnga Ka Shri ki pynkha ia U Rasmohon, U Oltoma, U Har (iapduh), Ka lensiar, bad U Habasing. Ka lensiar U Wendli Wriah ki pynkha ia U Besjo, U Shosing, Ka Bethel, Ka Limeri bad U Phistar. e) Ka Pateng U Nabeift Ka Tylliang na Laiseng. U Nabeifl shitnga Ka Tylliang ki pynkha ia U Pykad U Pykad shitnga Ka Shan ki pynkha ia Ka Spah. Ka Spah shitnga U Sit ki pynkha ia Ka Stem, Ka Jikon bad U langlait. U langlait shitnga Ka langjoh ki pynkha la U Ramsai, U Khang bad Ka Phin. U Ramsai shitnga Ka Shan ki pynkha ia Ka Bi, U langlait bad U Don. U langlait shitnga Ka Wanphet Ki pynkha ia ka Shan, Ka Laitmet, Ka Siarmon bad U Borkha. Ka Shan shitnga U Rynjih ki pynkha ia Ka Beit, Ka Saw, Ka Phoin, Ka Shongji bad U langlait. Ka Beit shitnga U Wanstep ki pynkha ia Ka Shaier, Ka Mohon, Ka Tewdiar, Ka Joba bad Ka Donnam. Ka Tewdiar kurim artnga i) U Kham uba pynkha ia U Subasing bad ii) U Painmanik uba pynkha ia U Mudui, U Lasing, U Saei, bad Ka Jarmai. U Subasing shitnga Ka Swet ki pynkha ia U Borjodhon. Na ka Keneris ka tnga baar jong u pat u pynkha ia U Tiengred Diengdoh. 108 g) Ka Pateng U Wanshaw Ka Klor na Sawthyndaw U Wanshaw shitnga Ka Khlor ki pynkha ia ka Shatai, Ka Phim, Ka low bad ka Wanhat. Ka Wanhat shitnga U Wanbot ki pynkha ia U Shong, U Shain, U Laitmet bad U Wansai U Shong shitnga Ka Riang (khun Ka Pydah U Buhkhut) ki pynkha ia U Thor, U Shongthma, U Wanbot bad Ka langshai. Ka langshai shitnga U Krom ka pynkha ia U Beinnoh. U Beinnoh shitnga Ka Noit ki pynkha ia U Ram, U Bormanik, Ka Donrit bad Ka Donwan. Ka Donwan shitnga U Mihsnge ki pynkha ia Ka Steplait, Ka Tewroi bad U Rynjih, U Rynjih shitnga Ka Shan ki pynkha 1a Ka Beit, Ka Saw, Ka Phoin Ka Shongji, U langlar bad U Sar (iapduh). Ka Beit shitnga U Wanstep ki pynkha ia Ka Tewdiar, Ka San, Ka Shaier, Ka Joba bad ka Donnam. Ka Tewdiar shitnga U Kham ki pynkha la U Subasing. U Subasing shitnga Ka Swet ki pynkha ia U Borjodhon. Khyndiat shaphang ka pateng U Nongthoh pat ka long kumne:- ng) Ka Pateng na U Saei Ka Peih na Mustoh. U Saei kurim artnga i) Ka Met kaba pynkha ia U Piet bad Ka Sheng ii) Ka Peih kaba pynkha ia U Jin, U Jwat, U Kynshe, Ka Beh bad Ka Syat. Ka Beh shitnga U Jerkha (khun U Khang) ki pynkha ia Ka Rap, Ka Shymphai, Ka Jap, U Khang bad U Kynrai. Ka Rap shitnga U Ste ki pynkha ia Ka Riang, Ka Lah, Ka Met bad Ka langsnge. Ka Riang shitnga U Sierlar ki pynkha ia U Laitshnong. U Laitshnong shitnga ka Wanphet ki pynkha ia U Ste bad U Saei. U Ste shitnga Ka Shyrwoifi ki pynkha ia U Snakon bad U Bosan. U Snakon shitnga Ka Jinamphet ki pynkha ia Ka Sdiah bad Ka Ngoi. Ka Sdiah shitnga U Laitshnong ki pynkha ia U Snakon, U Borjit, Ka Roifl bad Ka 109 Rit. Ka Roifi shitnga U Santhma ki pynkha ia U Porbot bad U Ata. U Porbot shitnga Ka Mihsnge ki pynkha ia Ka Laitstep, U Mut, U Saei bad Ka Lar. Ka Laitstep shitnga U Konsan ki pynkha ia Ka Shyrwoin bad U Thuron. Ka Shyrwoifi (u tnga ngim tip) ka pynkha ia Ka Sorbon, Ka Watnam, U Rai bad Ka Shiang. Ka Shiang shitnga U Ador ki pynkha ia Ka Bari bad Ka Basi (iapduh). Ka Bari shitnga U Borjokisor ki pynkha ia U Endren, U Piren (iapduh) U Endli (iapduh) bad U Wendli (Wriah). U Endren Wriah shitnga Ka Loris Dkhar (khun Ka Simai Dkhar U Meste Wanshan) ki pynkha ia Ka Dlistimai, U E. Weston, Ka Wissimai, U Brington bad Ka Lilydora Dkhar. U E. Weston Dkhar shitnga ka E. Saiwett Wanswett ki pynkha ia Ka Lapherlin, U Enbanshanbor Roy, U Biangpaia bad Ka Badalarisha Wanswett. h) Ka Pateng U Kynta Ka Laitmet na Laiseng U Kynta shitnga Ka Laitmet ki pynkha ia U Dilong bad U langlong. U langlong shitnga Ka Phar ki pynkha ia U Bakai. U Bakai shitnga Ka Kon ki pynkha ia U Jai'ong. U Jai'ong shitnga Ka Tynniang ki pynkha ia Ka Mihsnge bad Ka Wanshan. Ka Mihsnge shitnga U Jirai ki pynkha ia Ka Lasam, Ka langsnge bad U Norshing. Ka Lasam shitnga U Ron ki pynkha ia Ka Wanshan, Ka Sandykhem, Ka Mihsnge bad U Donsan. Ka Sandykhem shitnga U Jor ki pynkha ia U Ron, U Jai'ong, U Kyrban bad Ka Tala. U Jai'ong shitnga Ka Thot ki pynkha ia Ka Shatai, Ka Kseh, Ka Hoi bad Ka Laitmet. Ka Kseh shitnga U Sataid ki pynkha ia U Borjokisor bad U Mojokisor (iapduh). U Borjokisor shitnga Ka Bari Wriah ki pynkha ia U Endren, U Piren, U Endli (iapduh) bad U Wendli. U Endren shitnga Ka Loris Dkhar ki pynkha ia Ka Dlistimai, U Weston, Ka Wissimai, 110 U Brington bad Ka Lilydora. U Weston Dkhar shitnga Ka Saiwet Wanswett ki pynkha ia Ka Lapherlin, U Enbanshanbor Roy, U Biangpaia bad Ka Badalarisha. Naduh na Laiseng haduh U Nongthoh ka don mynta khatar pateng thik, kaba pynshisha ba ki Shelia ki wan buhai ia ka Ri War ha kaba sdang jong ka khatsan spah snem: kata shuwa ba ka Hima Shyllong kan paw pyrthei; bad naduh kata ka por ki kpa tymmen jongngi ki buh la ki jaipateng khnang ba ki khun ki ksiew pateng la pateng kin tip la ka tynrai bad pynshong nongrim ia lade ha la ki Seng ki Seng. Kine ki jaipateng ki long kiba la pdiang bad pynshisha ym tang da ki trai seng hynrei da ki bor synshar bishar kumjuh. ii) Ka Seng U Anai Ka Lngam Katkum ka jingi'athuh ki tymmen ki san, kane ka long ka Seng ka banyngkong eh jong ka Ri War Sheila: ba la pynlong ia ka hadien 6 pateng bad kata ka long kumne:- U Anai Ka Lngam ki pynkha ia U Than, Ka Samad, Ka Wanshong bad U langmon. U Than tnga Ka Phin ki pynkha ia U Nomei, Ka Lorkhma, Ka Lngam. Ka Lngam tnga U Ron ki pynkha ia U Snge tnga Ka Korsai, bad kine ki pynkha ia Ka Laidiang, Ka Shongwan, Ka langstep bad U Snge. Ka Laitstep U Stepwan ki pynkha ia ka Pyrdei tnga U Botrai, kiba pynkha ia ka Rynji, U Snarai, U Stepwan bad U Stepwar. Te, namarba ia ki bri ki khyndew ym shym la Vasam Tapiah naduh U Anai Ka Lngam haduh ka Pyrdei tnga U Botrai: la pynlong ia ka Seng jong kitei ki tymmen. Ki khun Seng jong U Anai Ka Lngam ki la khot sngewbha ruh ia ki 4 duwakdar ban ia don lang; bad don napdeng jong ki ruh kiba ia dei Seng lang. La pynbeit ha itngseng Ka Rynji ban jied arngut ki Tymmen Seng na ka Ill shitnad bad baroh ki long 8 ngut. Kine ki Tymmen Seng ki dei ban long tang ki trai ym ki poikha; kampher wat la u dei tang u khunlung ruh tang ba u dei u trai. Ka kynthei kam lah ban long tymmen seng. Lada u dei tang u khunlung; ka seng hi baroh kawei ka bah khlieh ban i'asaid na ka bynta ka kpoh jong u baroh kawei. Nalor kitei ki Tymmen seng, ki jied ruh sa ia ki bud tymmen seng, namar ki ia donkam. Ki Tymmen Seng shisien ba la jied ki long shilynter; katba ki bud Tymmen Seng pat ki long tang shisien bad ia kine lah ban jied wat na ki poikha ruh. Ka kam ba ki Tymmen seng kin leh ka long - (i) Mano ba dei hok ban long trai-ilng-Seng; bad ka bynta i'ingseng ha ka jingi'asam doh kyndang ka long ia ryngkat bad U Tymmen Seng. Nalor kata, ka i'ingseng ka i'oh tarn kawei ka bri ha ka jingi'asam ba ka Seng ka dei ban ai: bad ha ka por ba kan kam kynti ia kata ka bri ka dei ban khawai uwei u sniang ia ka Seng, (ii) Ki pynthikna mano ban long nongsaid na ka liang ki khun shynrang ka Pyrdei U Botrai da kaba pynsngewthuh shai ba u Nongsaid urn don hok ban dawa Ting dawa sem na ka Seng; lait tang ka Ri Nongsaid, bad u ruh, kum ka trai i'ingseng u dei ban ai uwei u sniang ia ka Seng ha kajuh ka sngi ka trai Tingseng ka khawai ia ki khun seng; lym kumta un nymlah kam longtrai halor kato ka jaka ba ai ri Nongsaid ka Seng, (iii) Ban kheifi ia ki bri ki khyndew baroh kiba dei ki ri Seng jong ka Pyrdei U Botrai bad la sabut ba ki don 23 tylli ha ka jymma jong ki: bad kawei kawei ka tnad ka Toh mar 5 bri: bad artylli la ai ia U Nongsaid bad ka Rai-Tingseng mar kawei. Naduh kane ka Seng sa i'eng ryntih ka tip-kur tip-jait, ka tip-seng tip-dang hapdeng ki briew jong ka Ri War Sheila, la kane ka Tingkur (Tingseng) ki duwakdar ki kyrkhu ki kyrdoh bad 112 kurnjuh ruh ia U Nongsaid; u ban bah khala kit khala ia ka khia ka shon jong ka kur ka jait baroh kawei. Haba ki sam bynta ia kitei ki artylli ki sniang ba ai Ka Kur bad U Nongsaid, ka long ha kane ka rukom - ia ka doh na baroh artylli ki sniang la sam 3 bynta marbiang: shibynta ki buh kyrpang ban sam seng bad sa ia ki arbyta pat la khleh lang ban sam na ka bynta ki Tymmen Seng, Ka Rai-Ting, U Nongsaid, ki bud tymmen bad ka bynta khmat briew ia baroh kiba don ha Tingseng ha ka sngi seng. Ka bynta khmat briew ba don ha ilngseng ha ka sngi seng ka long kumne - shibriew 3 dkhot (ka doh, ka shyieng bad ka khlein). Ka bynta ki Tymmen Seng, ka Rai - ling bad U Nongsaid ki long ia ryngkat; hynrei ka bynta jong ki Bud- tymmen ka kham duna khyndiat. Lada ki don ki Duwakdar ba la khot kyrpang, ki ruh ki ioh kat ka bhah U Tymmen seng. Ki Saw Duwakdar, ynda ki poi ha ka durbar hima; kila iaroh shikatdei eh ia ka jingryntih jong ka jingpyniaid seng U Anai Ka Lngam ha Rai-ling Ka Pyrdei U Botrai; ia kaba ki Tymmen seng kila buh ryntih ban pynskhem ia ka jingiasam Tapiah baroh hakhmat jong ki Duwakdar. Ki iaroh ruh kumno Ka Rai - Ting ka jai ia la ka pateng naduh U Anai Ka Lngam haduh ha ka bad kurnjuh ruh U Snarai kum u Nongsaid bad nongkorbariing-kur: bad kurnjuh ruh U Stepwan bad U Stepwar shuwa ba kin rah la ki bhah ki bynta kiba ka Seng kala ai bynta ha ki. Hadien kane ka seng; kiwei ki seng ki kham ih bad kham wandur; kiba sah rukom pateng la pateng haduh kine ki sngi. Ki tymmen ki ju maham ba kano kano ka kpoh kaba set ia ki kot-Seng kot-dang bad bat ia ki khyndew ki shyiap ha lade: ki kylla duh kur duh ling. 113 iii) Ka Seng U Syrna Ka Noh Katkum ka jingi'athuh jong ki tymmen ki san bad katkum ba paw shynna na ki kot Seng kot dang; ki seng ki dang baroh ha War Sheila ki paw shynna tad haduh kane ka Seng; kata ruh haduh U Shan Ka Laitstep. Ka pateng jong U Syrna Ka Noh ka long kumne - U Syrna Ka Noh ki pynkha ia U langhat tnga Ka Wanswett; U Mon tnga Ka Juna bad Ka Sngar tnga U Snge. U langhat tnga Ka Wanswet ki pynkha ia Ka Laitstep, Ka Steplait, U Phai bad U Wankhmah. U Mon tnga Ka Juna pat ki pynkha ia U Ram, U Pang bad ka langmet. Ka Sngar tnga U Snge pat ki pynkha ia U Shan tnga Ka Laitstep. U Shan tnga Ka Laitstep pat ki pynkha ia Ka Laitksan, Ka Laitthma, Ka Tep, Ka Riang, U Don bad U Ji. Tad haduh ki khun U Shan Ka Laitstep ba ki khun ki ksiew U Syrna ka Noh ki sdang ban ia lum seng ha Ting Ka Laitksan. Baroh hynriew tnad ki pynmih mar saw - sawngut ki ‘bud tymmen seng’ na kawei kawei ka tnad bad baroh ki long 48 ngut, ia kiba la aibor ban synshar bad bishar ia baroh ki kam Seng jong U Shan Ka Laitstep. la kito ki tymmen seng jied bynrap la tip ruh ia ki kum 'Ki Tymmen Seng Sorkari’ ki bym da donbor haduh katta ban rai kam kum kitei ki 24 ngut ki Tymmen Seng ba la jied da ki tnad. Nalor ki tei ki tymmen seng ki jied ruh sa arngut ki Tymmen Seng Rai-Ting bad arngut ki Tymmen Seng Nongsaid, kiba ka bor jong ki ka long mar ia ryngkat bad ki Tymmen Seng Sorkari. la u nongkhot jong ka Durbar Seng ruh la fiiew ba u long hi uwei na ki Tymmen Seng tang ba um don bor ban rai kam. Haba Tasam ia ki bri ki khyndew, kiba long ka hok nongkynti jong U Shan Ka Laitstep la buh kyrpang ia ka 114 jingTabynta da kumne - (i) Ka Bynta Rai - ling ne ka bynta jong ka Kur kaba bat ia ka llng-seng. (ii) Ka Bynta Ri Nongsaid Gong u Kfli rangbah u ban long u nongsaid u nongthew jong ka ling ka kur. la ka bynta Rai - ling la ai ha ka liang jong ka Laitksan kum ka hymmen nyngkong kaba bat ia ka ling -kur llng-seng: tang ba ka dei ban khawai ia ka seng uwei u sniang uba shongdor shiteng ia ka dor jong katei ka bri Rai - ling, la ka Ri Nongsaid pat la ai ha ka tnad jong U Dan kum u hynmen shynrang rangbah duh jong ka ling ka kur; bad na ka bynta kane U Dan um donkam ban ai ne khawai sniang ia ka Seng. Hadien ba la pyndep ia kine ki bynta, ia ki bynta kiba dang sah la iasam marbiang hapdeng ki 6 tnad, da kaba ki buh kawei ka ri-tdong ia kaba kin dang ia bam khawai seng uwei u sniang ha kawei pat ka por. Ka jingi'asam bynta jong ka seng U Shan Ka Laitstep ka long katkum kane ka kular seng iv) Ka Kular Seng "Ngi thoh skhem kane ka kular Seng shaphang ki khyndew U Shan Ka Laitstep, kiba na Nongbah; kiba ngi la lah ia bynta hapdeng hynriew ngut hynriew bynta. Ki kyrteng ki jaka long kine - (i) Lyngkien (ii) Umnia (iii) Mushiang (iv) Nordilong (v) Kroh (vi) Tiahrong (vii) Lyngkien. la kine ki bynta la iasam hynriew bynta. Baroh ki ktem la shim bynta lang kumne Shaphang Khasi ba khot kadiang, la shim bynta I) Ka Laitksan, U Don ba shim bynta ha pud Ka Laitksan, U Ji, ba shim bynta ha pud U Don, Ka Laitthma, ba shim bynta ha pud U Ji, Ka Tep ba shim bynta ha pud ka Laitthma, Ka Riang, kaba ngi iehnoh ka bynta ha pud Ka Tep (ba oh apot) shaphang dkhar. 115 Ka khyndew kaba ha Jri Ri Nongbah, ka bym pat ia bynta, kaba long: 1 .Pud Sepngi, U Jiwan Mustoh; 2. Pud Mihngi, U Maw Sandi Mustoh; 3. Pud Phang dkhar, U Saei; 4. Pud Phang Khasi, U Hon. la kane ka khyndew ngi ia bynta laingut lai bynta - 1. Ka Laitthma, 2. U Don. 3. Ka Riang. la ka bri haba ha ri Rewmeifi ri Nongbah de ka bym pat la bynta kaba long 1. Pud Sepngi Ka Wanji, 2. U Pud Phang Khasi U Liarkha, ia kane ka khyndw ngi ia bynta 4 ngut 4 bynta. 1. U Ji, 2. Ka Laitksan, 3. Ka Tep, 4. Ka Riang. Ngi iehnoh ka khyndew ha Briwah ri Nongbah ka bym pat ia bynta, kaba long shipud phang sepngi U Jon, 2. Pud Mihngi Ka Wah, bad Ka Wanshong, 3. Pud phang dkhar u Jon, 4. Pud phang Khasi ka Bon. la kane ka khyndew ngi la bynta 2 bynta, 1 . U Ji, 2. Ka Laitksan. Ka kyrteng jongngi ki Seng - 1 . U Khang. 2. U Ramrai 3. U Behwar. 4. U Ksansnge. 5. U Borjit. 6. U Pdam. 7. U Haising. 8. U Than 9. U Kiri 10. U Muluksing. 11. U Shah. 12. U Konrai. 13. U Mudin. 14. U Tanghat. 15. U Kat. 16. U Bormanik. 17. U Amor. 18. U Wansai. 19. U Sanlong. 20. U Sansnge. 21. U Botkha. The 29 th October, 1875 U Botsing, Sirdar Nongbah. Nongthoh Katei ka kular Seng kala man long ka dur ka nuksa ia baroh ki seng ki dang hadien habud. Kumba paw; baroh ki Seng kiba hadien ki long ia kiba la thoh shai bad bniah bha. Ki Seng kiba ngi tip haduh kine ki sngi ha Mustoh, Shala, Nongwar, Nongbah ki long kine:- Ha Shala: i) Ka Seng U Thngan Ka Dah ii) Ka Seng U 116 Bonai Ka Top iii) Ka Seng U Hirai Ka Du bad kiwei. Ha Mustoh: i) Ka Seng ka Rap U Ste ii) Ka Seng U Pynsen Ka langji iii) Ka Seng U Smon Ka Wanji iv) Ka Seng Ka Konjri U Bonai bad kiwei. Ha Nongbah: i) Ka Seng U Shan Ka Laitstep ii) Ka Seng Ka Bi Ka langshai iii) Ka Seng U Juhai U Ranjit iv) Ka Seng U Jon Ka Bamon bad kiwei. Ha Nongwar: i) Ka Seng U Bosan U Shakon ii) Ka Seng Ka Lait Ka Phai iii) Ka Seng Ka Wanphet U Tanglait iv) Ka Seng U Ramrai Ka Mad bad kiwei. Kito ki Seng kiba ai kyrteng U Shynrang ne Kynthei na khmat ki long shitnga bad na kajuh ka shnong. Kito ki para shynrang ka mut ki dej shipara kiba tang arngut hi: kaba mut ba ki khun ki waris jong baroh arngut ki ia don bynta lang namar ba ym shym la i'asam Tapiah ia ki bri ki bsah mynba kitei ki tymmen ki dang im. Ka jingmyntoi jong ki Seng ki dang ym tang ba ki ia tip ia ithuh para ba ia hiar pateng na ka juh ka doh ka snam ka thymmei: hynrei ka Seng katkum ka kular ba nyngkong ka ai hok ai bynta mar ia ryngkat kynthei bad shynrang khlem don kano kano ka jingfiiew shiliang khmat. Ki khun ki waris jong katei ka kpoh tymmen ki long ki trai halor ki bri ki khyndew, ki kamai ki kajieh la, na ka liang kmie ne liang kpa kumjuh. Tang ia ka Rai - ling ne ka trai Ting seng; kaba long ka hymmen san la ai kyrpang ia ka khyndew Rai-Ting. Kumjuh ruh ia ka Ri Nongsaid dei ban Toh na ka liang jong U Hymmen shynrang rangbah. La ngeit ba ia ka Rai-Ting bad ia U Nongsaid la pynkyntang lypa naduh ka kpoh ka kmie, bad ki fliewsang ban kyntait ne lyndet ia kane ka rukom ba la buh pateng la pateng. 117 la ka Rai-iing ki shaid ai ka bynta kaba bha khnang ba ka lah ban kdup ban kyrshan ia ki hymmen ki para kiba hap ha ka apot ka bipot. Kumjuh ruh ia u Nongsaid ki ai ka jaka kaba kham bit khnang ba u lah ban i’asaid ban Tada ia la ka kur ka kpoh haba poi ha ka eh ha ka kher. la kine la ai khnang ki jaka kiba bha bad ba ioh jingmyntoi khnang ba ki poikha poiman kin nym don daw ban kdew kti haba ki bah ki kit ia la ka ring ka kpoh ba ki pynlut phut ia ka kamai kajieh lang jong ki ban da ia la ka ilng ka kur. Lada jia ba ka kpoh ka pynkha tang para shynrang khlem kur kynthei: ia ka rai-iing ki ai ha u hymmen san (hymmen rangbah) bad ka ri nongsaid ka duh noh. Lada jia pat ba kha tang para kynthei, ka hymmen san kan ioh ia ka rai-iing bad ka ri Nongsaid ka duh noh. Tang haba kha khleh kynthei shynrang ka hymmen san kan ioh ia ka rai-iing bad u shynrang nyngkong un ioh ia ka ri Nongsaid. la kane ka rukom thymmai la seng Nongrim tang naduh ka por ba ki Saw Kynhun ki wan buhai shnong ha ri War. Hadien bala dep buh ryntih la ki dustur khyndew ki shyiap: ba ka synshar ka bishar ruh ka sdang ban wandur. Wat la ka jingbuh ha ki jingthoh jingtar shaphang ki dustur ki riti bad ki kular seng ki paw shynna tad haduh ka snem 1 875: ki seng ki dang kila ih kila wandur naduh shuwa ka snem 1850; tang ba kirn paw shynna ha ki jingthoh jingtar. V) Ka Durbar Seng Shaphang ka durbar Seng bad ka bor jong ka la mynjur ha ki jingbishar baroh jong ka Hima Sheila naduh ki Duwakdar haduh ka Durbar Hima. Ka Durbar Seng kaba nyngkong eh ba la pynlong da ki Rangbah na Mustoh, Nongwar, Shala bad Nongbah dei ka Durbar Seng U Anai Ka Lngam: hynrei ka dur 118 ka dar jong ka kam pat da long kaba janai. Dei tad haduh ka Durbar Seng U Syrna Ka Noh ba ka Seng kala sdang ban wandur da kaba buh ia kine ki kyndon kiba kham shai — i) Kaba thung Tymmen Seng : Shaphang kaba jied bad thung tymmen Seng: la jied na man la ka tnad: kata, naman la ki nonghiar pateng jong utei u tymmen bad kine ki Tymmen Seng kin pyrkhat bad rai ia ki kam Seng baroh jong utei U Tymmen. Ha kane ka por, ia ki rai baroh la buh jingkynmaw da ki ksah thri bad ksah Iwar. Dei tad ynda ha ka Seng U Shan Ka Laitstep la buh thikna ha ki jingthoh jingtar ia ki jingpynbeit pynbiang baroh. Te, namar ba U Shan Ka Laitstep ki pynkha hynriew ngut ki khun - Ka Laitksan, U Don, U Ji, Ka Laitthma, Ka tep bad Ka Riang: ki kylla long hynriew tnad. Kumta la rai ban jied 12 ngut ki Tymmen Seng. Arngut na kawei ka tnad. la ka Laitksan, khun nyngkong ki pynlong ‘trai Seng’ bad ka ling jong ka ka kylla long ‘Ka trai Tingseng’ bad U Dan, kum u hymmen san rangbah u kylla long U Nongsaid ne nongkorbar kam jong ka ling ka kur. La pynlong riti ba ka ‘rai-ilng’ nalor arngut ki tymmen Seng ka dei ban pynmih tarn sa uwei bad baroh ki long 13 ngut ki tymmen Seng. Lada lap ba kano kano ka tnad ka sah riewkynthei ba ym don nongsaid nongkorbar; u Nongsaid jong ka Kur un shimti ban khmih bad ban i'eng kum u nongsaid; namar kata ka kpoh kam lah ban wan ha Durbar Seng khlem tymmen Seng. La ju pynlong tymmen wat ia kiba dang anabalit ruh bad u Nongsaid jong ka Kur un ia said na ka bynta kata ka tnad. U poikha um lah ban long tymmen seng ne mih bujli namar ka tnga bad ki khun, bad ym ju sngewtynnad ia u bar seng ban wan sngap ne 119 tuklar ha ka kam Seng kiwei. Haba jia ba don ka khawai dawai Seng ka ju long ka dustur ban jied ‘bud tymmen seng' nalor ki tymmen seng na man la ka tnad. Kat ka jinghiar pateng na u Syma ha U Shan kala long 9 pateng; bad ia ka Kular Seng jong ka Seng U Shan ka Laitstep la thoh shai kumba la kdew mynshuwa. Kane ka jingTasam ia ki khyndew Ri Seng da ka Durbar Seng, ryngkat kaba da buh ryntih da ki jingthoh jingtar ka long dang tang ha kaba kut jong ka Khyndai spah snem: katba ka thoh ka tar ha ka liang ka synshar ka bishar ka la long kham mynshuwa; kata naduh kaba sdang ka Khadphra spah snem. Shuwa jong kata, ia baroh ki rai ne jingi'akut la buh jingkynmaw da ki ksah thri bad ksah Iwar. Kumno ki bor synshar ki burom ia ki rai jong U Seng, lah ban i'ohi na kane ka nomuna jong ka Rai U Sirdar Nongbah ha ka jingbishar - Ka Rai na Ka Jingbishar U Sirdar, Nongbah (Lyngkien) Nga U Sirdar bad ki tymmen, namar kane ha ka jingbishar jongngi, la paw ka jingmudui U Niaphosing, U Borwan bad U Rai (ba la iap) bad ba sei ka kot ksan, kaba i'oh na ki Wahadadar rim, bad kawei pat ka kot ba la ai ki tymmen, kiba dei Seng jong U Tanghat Ka Wanswett bad ba i'athuh kiba dei Seng jong U Tanghat Ka Wanswett ba la sabut biang. Hynrei ba ai jubab ki shah mudui, ba ki ong, ba la ia bynta ia ki khyndew U Tanghat Ka Wanswett, te kumno ki ia bynta, ia kata ruh ym sabud bad ba U Wankhmah uba dei u kthaw pateng jong ki nongmudui, ki ong, “ym shym kha na U Tanghat Ka Wanswett, hynrei la kha na uno uno u briew, ne kano kano ka briew”, 120 Namarkata, la hukum ia ki Nongmudui, kumba la sabut biang kiba dei Seng jong U langhat Ka Wanswett, na ka bynta U Wankhmah, ba ki long ki khun ki ksiew jong u, namar ba dei ki khun ki ksiew pateng U langhat Ka Wanswett na ka bynta U Wankhmah. Kumta ki nongmudui ia ki bri ki khyndew jong U langhat Ka Wanswett, kin Toh shi bynta kine ki Nongmudui na ki shah mudui bad kiwei ki briew kiba dei Seng jong U langhat Ka Wanswett, kumba la munjur hi U Khang, U Borsan bad ki lok jong ki bad kila kyrpad ruh ba ngin shim ia ki dolil jongki, kawei pat ka Koiphot dt. 30.1 1 .1872. Ki pyni ia ki kyrteng ki bri kiba ha Ri Nongbah bad ki pud jong ki; ki kyrteng ki bri baroh long kine:- I. Umnia: 1) Pud Sepngi 2) Pud Mihngi 3) Pud Shatei 4) Pud Shathie II. Mawsheng: 1) Pud Sepngi 2) Pud Mihngi 3) Pud Shatei 4) Pud Shathie III. Sohtympew: 1 ) Pud Sepngi 2) Pud Mihngi 3) Pud Shathie 4) Pud Shatei Khang ka Wah Bakra U Donkha. U Kyrshin U Shah bad ka Lang. U Don bad Ka Bein Ka Laitstep sdang U Kynshin U Shan. U Skot. Khang Ka Wah Bakra U Khyllin, Ka Pyrdei Ka Pyrdei Ka Pyrdei 121 IV. Mawlein: 1) Pud Sepngi 2) Pud Mihngi 3) Pud Shatei 4) Pud Shathie ... V. Ri Ka Sya: 1) Pud Sepngi 2) Pud Mihngi 3) Pud Shathie 4) Pud Shatei VI. Kuther ba khot Kem - 1) Pud Sepngi ,.. 2) Pud Mihngi 3) Pud Shathie 4) Pud Shatei VII.
