Shong Nongbah: 1)PudSepngi U Dusan 2) Pud Mihngi UKot 3) Pud Shathie Ka Kseh 4) Pud Shatei U Dusan Ha kane ka mokotduma, U Khang, U Borsan bad kiwei na Nongbah, kiba tong ki shah mudui; kila ai jubab pat ia ka Koiphot U Niaphorsing, U Borwan, U Ramjan; ki ong ba ka jingmudui jong ki kam long kaba shisha ia ka banVoh khyndew U Tanghat Ka Wanswett kiba ha ri Nongbah, ki ong ngi la dep ia bynta 3 ngut - i) U Phai. ii) Ka Steplait. iii) Ka Laistep ki khun U langhat Ka Wanswett. 123 Te, kumta ma nga U Sirdar bad ki tymmen, ngi shim ia ki dolil na ki nongmudui, ngi la khmih ngi i'ohi, kawei long kaba la pynksan shisha ki Wahadar rim ia U Niaphorsing bad ia ki lok jong u, kiba hiarpateng na U Tanghat Ka Wanswett. Bad ngi ai hukum ban i'asam bynta kum ki khun ki ksiew U Tanghat Ka Wanswett, shi bynta kin i'oh na U Phai, shi bynta kin i'oh na Ka Steplait, shi bynta kin Voh na Ka Laitstep, shi bynta kin i'oh na U Wankhmah. Bad ia ka Khorsha ba lut ki Nongmudui, yn siew ki shah Mudui, kumba ngi la pynkut ia kane ka Mokotduma. Hynrei ia ka bri kaba na Sohphan Ka Bor, bad kaba na Shnong Nongbah, ba pynpaw ki nongmudui, te long kita ba ujor kiba rem-seng bym dei ki jong U Tanghat Ka Wanswett, ia kita ki bri, ngi la pyllait noh ba dei ki jong ki briew. Dated Nongbah, U Botsing, Sirdar Nongbah. The 19^ Deer. 1872 U Robrai, Tymmen Katkum ka rai U Sirdar Nongbah, ka paw ba ka jingbishar ka peit bad bniah bha haba bishar wat haba ki jong Ka Laitstep, Ka Steplait bad U Phai ki mut ban kyntait ne pynduh seng ia U Wankhmah: khamtam haba ka jingbishar U Sirdar ka shem na ka rai ki Saw Wahadar tymmen ka Sheila, ba U langhat Ka Wanswett ki don 4 ngut ki khun, ym laingut kumba kitei ki ong, kata, i) Ka Steplait, ii) Ka Laitstep. iii) U Phai bad iv) U Wankhmah. Halor kane ka nongrim U Sirdar Nongbah U pynksan ia ka jingmudui U Niaphorsing pynshah ia U Khang bad kiwei kiba thmu ban pynduh hok ia U Wankhmah. Wat ha ka appeal ba ki shah Mudui ki appeal sha U Deputy Commis- sioner, U Deputy Commissioner urn shym kynriah na ka rai U 124 Sirdar Nongbah u ong, “With reference to the appeal, it appears clear that the suit to which it refers was adjudicated upon by the Sirdar of Nongbah contrary to rule 26. note (a) Khasi Hills rules lays down that Sirdar cannot try suits in which a native of another Sirdarship not resident in that jurisdiction is a party and the Elaka of Sheila, the Sirdar of the British village of Nongbah had no power to try the suit between U Niaphorsing of Nongwar and U Khang of Nongbah . It is true as engaged by U Botsing Sirdar of Nongbah that he took up this suit by orders of the Court of Deputy Commissioner, but this order which was passed on the 7 lh November, 1872 by the Extra Assistant Commissioner was a mistake. For the reasons given the decision passed by the Sirdar of Nongbah must be set aside, and the respondent is warned that if he wishes to proceed on his suit that he must institute proceeding before the court of the Deputy Commissioner in the usual way. Shillong, H. S. Bivar, The 5"‘ Sept. 1873 Deputy Commissioner. Ha ki jingialang Seng mynshuwa, kata, san ne hynriew pateng naduh ba kila shong la sah ha kane ka thain, bad haba ym pat don jingthoh jingtar; la mih bun ki jingartatien la kane ka rukom pyni'aid seng la kan trei kam ne em! Pynban katba nangiaid ki por ka nangi'aid donbor na kawei ka pateng sha kawei pat ka pateng tang da ka jingnep jingkynmaw lyngba ki ksah haduh ban da wandur bha da ki jingthoh jingtar. 125 Ka riti ban Toh bynta lang kynthei bad shynrang na ki hok ki kamai jong ki kmie ki kpa ka nangskhem bad nang wandur katba ki por ki nangTaid. Kumjuh ruh ka rukom ban buh jingkynmaw ia ki pateng pakit ban tip kano ka jait kano ka kur ka pynduh pyndam phiaw ia kino kino ki jingkulmar ha ka poikha poiman ban ri kyntang kano ka kur bad kano ka jait. la u sohpet u shynnai na ka liang ka kynthei, ki War Sheila, ki niew ba ki dei ki kur, hynrei kiba hiar pateng na ka liang U Shynrang ki dei ki ‘Jait’ katba kito pat kiba hiar pateng na ka liang kpa, ki dei ki kha ki man. Na ka liang shynrang phang kpa, kata, lada U shynrang u long na ka liang kynthei na ka hymmen, u khun shynrang u lah ban shongkurim ia ka khun kynthei u kni, bad 1a kata ki ong, “uba bud kni.” Hynrei lada u dei pat u khun u kni, um lah ban shong kurim ia ka khun ka syngken ne kmie kha namar ba sang ba long kliang (shong kliang). Lada jia pat ba uno uno u briew u wan poikha ha ka kmienah kmiesan ha iing, u khun shynrang jong ki um lah ban leit poikha haka khun kynthei ka kmie kha ne ka syngken namar ka long ‘aikhaw kylliang', kaba seng ba ma. Kumta, katba paw na ki riti synshar bishar, ia ka rukom pyni'aid seng pyni'aid dang la burom da baroh ki Kashari hapoh ka hima; wat haduh ka jingsynshar phareng ia ki jingpyni'aid seng la burom kyrpang. VI) Ka Ri Laiseng Ka Ri Laiseng ka long ka Ri Seng jong U Kynta, U Nabeifi bad U Tangrai: bad hadien ka Sawthyndaw jong ka Phetmungor, ka khlam kala sar ia ka Laitmawria, ka jaka shong jong ki: bad ki khun ki ksiew jong ki ki wan phet sha Nongwar, Mustoh, 126 Nongkroh bad Tyrna: bad haduh mynta, kine ki shnong ki long ki trai jong ka ri Laiseng. la kane ka jaka la ai sngewbha da U Khang U Saei na Mustoh ha kitei ki laingut ban shong ban sah bad ban rep ban riang namar ba ka Thylliang, ka khun ksiew jong ki ka ia poi kha bad U Nabeifi. U Nabeifi pat u khot bad ai jaka ia U Kynta bad U Tangrai ban wan shong shngaifi bad u ha Laitmawria, bad hangne ki roi parum pareh tacj haduh ba ka khlam ka sar ia ka shnong jong ki ba kiba sah ki sa phet ha kitei ki saw-shnong. Hadien ka jingphet shnong phet thaw jong ki khun ki ksiew kitei ki laitngut; kala don ka jingkyntur hima jong ki Mawlong ban dokhol ia ka ri Laiseng bad ki katto katne ki bynta Ri Nongkroh ha ki thain Mawthadwang. Kane kala wanrah ia ka thma Umsanglet. Ki Laiseng kila jop bad la pynskhem ia u pud u sam na Umsanglet. Dei kane ka thma kaba la wanrah ia ka Sanglet wat haduh ka poikha poiman hapdeng ki Mawlong bad ki Laiseng. Ynda ha ka por jong ka jingsynshar ki Phareng, ki Mawlong sa shisien pat kila pynkhih Mokotduma na u pud Mawsanglet beit haduh Pasbiria. U Deputy Commissioner ula rai bad pynbeit ia kane ka Mokotduma da kaba thung pud da ki Morok bad ki thum baroh shilynter hapdeng ki Laiseng, Ki Mustoh bad ki Mawlong. Ha ka jingshisha ia ka Ri Laiseng la pyni'aid da ki member Seng jong kine ki Sawshnong, hynrei namar ki Mokotduma la donkam ban don U President bad ki Tymmen Seng kin long ki dkhot trei kam jong ka Durbar Laiseng. La jied nyngkong eh ia U Alongsing, Headman Mustoh, ban long U President Ka Laiseng; da kaba ia kut durbar ba ka jinglong President kan Vaid kylliang kylliang hapdeng kine ki 127 Saw- shnong: bad une U President un shong ha ka kam baroh shirta. Hadien ka jingi'ap jong U Alongsing, la thung ia U Mahari, Sirdar Nongkroh ban long U President uba ar da ka jingTajied paitbah bad un neh ha ka kam 5 snem. Mynta ka dei sa ka pali na Tyrna, bad ha kane ka election jop U Dumbura. Nangta ka wan sa ka pali ki Nongwar bad ha ka election jop U Sorbodhon Roy uncontested. Hadien U Sorbodhon Roy wan long Presi- dent U Shinta M. Roy na Mustoh bad hadien jong u wan long President U Wendly M. Roy na Nongkroh. Uno uno napdeng ki khun seng u lah ban leit ban rep ban riang, ban thung ban tep hapoh ka hima Laiseng tang ba ki dei ban da pan jingbit na ka durbar seng bad siew katto katne u khorsha katba pynshong ka durbar Seng. Uno Uno uba ieh khali khlem trei lai-snem, ka durbar seng ka lah ban shim noh ia kato ka jaka bad ai ha kiwei pat ki para khun seng. Ka Durbar Laiseng ka long ka durbar kaba ha khlieh duh jong ka Ri Laiseng; kaba lah ban rai kut ia ki jingi'a kajia pud kajia sam baroh hapdeng para khun seng hapoh u pud u sam jong ka. Hynrei ka Durbar laiseng kam don bor pat ban bishar ia ki phoidari ne ki case ia shoh ia dat hapoh Hima Laiseng, khamtam eh haba ki mamla ki long na ki Sande bapher bapher. la kum kine ki case la ju phah sha U Deputy Commissioner, ha ka por ka jingsynshar ki phareng, bad sha ka District Council hadien ka jingleit noh ki phareng. Ka durbar Laiseng ka lah ban beh seng ne khang apot ia uno uno u para khun seng uba pynkheifi ia ki kular seng ne u bym mynjur bad ki rai jong ka durbar seng. Ka durbar Laiseng kam lah ban aiwai ia u mawshun da kaba ia teh kular; ne shop khajna na ki dieng kiba uno uno u khun seng u pynngad bad die ia ki. 128 Hynrei kam ju shim khajna ne musul na u para khun seng uba pyngngad ia ki dieng na ka bynta ban pyndonkam ia lade la, ha kaba thawi'ing thawsem ne ha kiwei pat ki jingdonkam. Shisien shisnem ka durbar seng ka ai jingkheifi ha u paitbah bad ia ka peisa tyngka baroh kaba tam na ka jingpyndonkam jong uwei u snem la nikar paitbah hapdeng ki para khun seng kiba wan durbar seng; nangta ki sa sdang ka jingkheifi jingdiah ba thymmai. la ki khyndew Laiseng ym ju i'asam i'apiah kumba leh ia ki Ri Seng ha la ki jong ki jong ki tnad haduh ba ki kylla Ri kynti. Ki lah ban dokhol katba ki dang trei, bad lada kim trei shuh; kiwei pat ki para khun seng ki lah ban trei bad dokhol ia kato ka jaka da ka jingaibor jong ka durbar seng. Namar kata, U Seng u long u trai bad baroh kiba trei ba ktah bad ba rep ba riang ki long tang ki nongbuhai: kiba ka hok jong ki ka lah ban duh noh ha kano kano ka por ba kim lah ban pynbiang ia ki jingdawa jong ka Durbar Seng. «<?* 129 Lynnong: 6 Kl SnGI BA KHATDUH Kl 4 DuWAKDAR Ki Saw Duwakdar kila synshar bishar ia ka Hima ki 23 shnong palat la ka 60 snem ha ka jingsuk jingsaifi bad jingman bha. Ka Hima 23 shnong ka kylla long ka Hima kaba riewspah bad ba shai khmat tarn na ki Hima baroh ha ri Khasi. Ka jingstad jong ki ban buh ryntih ia ka synshar ka bishar naduh ki Sande haduh ka durbar hima; ki pyni'oh ha lade la ka burom bad ka jingi'aroh na baroh. La ong ba ha ka por ka jingsynshar jong ki ym ju don mokotduma; namar ia ki mokotduma baroh ki pynsuk. Ki Sande ki suk ki sain namar ba ka don ka jingfa trei lang bad ka jingi'a burom markylliang. Ka thong jong ki barabor ka long kumno ban pynroi ia ka Hima bad ban kyntiew ia ka i'oh ka kot jong u paitbah. Ki trei shitom ban wanrah ia ka jingsuk bad ki i'aid kylleng ia ka dkhar ka lyngkien ban wad buit wad lynti kumno ban pyni'ar ia ka trei ka ktah bad ka khai'i ka pateng. Ki long ki kmie ki kpa ia la ki khun ki hajar bad ki pyrkhat synia sngi kumno ba ki kin bit kin biang bad ba kin suk kin saifl. Dei hangne ba ngi shem shisha ia ka jinglong rangbah ba nylla bad ka jingkhraw kaba ngi dei hok ban pyrto. Kum ki nongsynshar bishar kila leh ia la ka jong ka kamram bad kila aiti ia lade ha ka jingshakri. Kila buh ki nuksa kiba ki pateng ki ban dang wan kin bud bad kiba ka history kan pyrto ia ki kam radbah kiba kila leh. Ha ka jingshakri kirn kheifi ia ka jingduh lymne kin riej ia ki jingeh. Dei kane kaba la pynlong ia ki lynter ban Toh ia ka jingieit bad jingshaniah jong baroh. Ha ki sngi jong ka jinglong tymmen ki phuhmat ban i'ohi ba ka hima ka don ha ka jingsuk jingsaifl bad ba ki khun ki 130 hajar ki sham bha ki manbha. Hynrei kumba ka don ka jingsdang ka don ruh ka jingkut. Ha ka snem 1 722 U Jin u kem pang bad shen u khlad noh. Ka jingkhlad jong u kala tap dum ia ka Hima ki 23 shnong baroh kawei namar uwei u khlur ula jah noh na ka sahit jong ki 23 shnong. La pynlong ka jingthang donburom da ka hima ryngkat ka khawai dawai bad ka phur ka siang san sngi lynter. Shen hadien kane sa kawei pat ka jingkah dum ka wan tap ia ka hima 23 shnong: la bna ba U Steifi Duwakdar u i'ap halor lieng na ka jingpang i'ap them katba u dang wanphai na Shilot. Arbnai hadien la bna pat ba U Bor, uba la thiah pang la katto katne bnai ruh um don shuh. Ka Hima ka poi ha ka shai'ong. Ryngkat ka jingi'am briew bad ka jingsngewsih la thang siarkait ia ki baroh arngut da ka hima ryngkat ka phur ka siang 5 miet 5 sngi lynter. Mynta ka Hima 23 shnong ka don sa tang arngut ki duwakdar - U Jerkha bad U Kynshe bad kine ruh kila tymmen eh bad kila kwah ban lait noh na ka kam; hynrei ka Hima kam shah. La don ka jingi'akren jong ki Rangbah ba dei ban pynmih bujli noh ha ka jaka jong kitei ki arngut ba la i'ap; hynrei kiba bun ba lang kirn mon ban thung duwakdar pyndap katba dang don kine arngut. Ha ka durbar hima kaba la long ha Shala ha ka snem 1724 la ia pyrkhat kumno yn leh halor kane ka kam. Ha ka jingi'a ai jingmut ka durbar kala kad arliang. Shiliang kirn mon ban bynrap Duwakdar katba dang don kitei arngut bad shiliang pat ki ong ba namar ba kitei ar kila tymmen eh; dei ban buh nongi'arap. Ha ka jingi'arah kti kito ki sande kiba mon ban buh nongVarap ki ioh 12 sande bad ki thung arngut ki Dewanji ban i'arap ia ka Hima 23 shnong. Ki 1 1 Sande ki khlad noh na ka Hima bad ki sah kyrpang. Kane ka jingjia kala 131 pynsngewsih eh ia U Jerkha bad U Kynshe. Ha ka history jong ka Hima 23 shnong ka snem 1724 ka long ka snem kaba sngewsih tam kaba sah kum ka dak i'ong ha ka kitab jong ka por. Hadien shisnem tam u Jerkha ruh u khlad noh ynda ula im kumba 115 snem. Mynta u sah satang U Kynshe bad urn lah shuh ban wan durbar, la ki kam hima sima baroh la pyniaid da ki Dewanji kiba ki paitbah kirn i'oh satia ka jinghun bad jingshaniah. U Kynshe ynda ula dap kumba 125 snem u iap noh bad ka Hima 12 shnong kam don Duwakdar shuh Tang shu iap U Kynshe ki dewanji ruh ki sahngeh noh ka hei kam Ha ka snem 1730 ki Rangbah bad Ki Kaida ka hima ki pynlong ia ka Durbar paitbah ha Phali ban iu pyrkhat kmnno yn leh haba baroh ki duwakdar mynta kirn don shuh La don ki rangbah kiba ai jingmut ba dei ban bud ia ka nuksa U Jin ba U Paitbah u dei ban jied bad ba lada don mano mono ha I >niait ia ka jingjied dei ban kuna bad masorkha no ka hima. i lynrei kiba bun ba lang kim sngewiahap jingmut da kaba pynuiaw bn kane ka shim noh ia ka jinglait-luid jong u briew Ki pynidaw ruh ba bun na ki riewdonburom kim mon ban trei m kane ka kam namar ki hap ban im na ka dan ka khrong bad ka jingai sngewbha ki sande. Namar kata, ki ong ba kar, khcmbhu ba lea Hima ki 12 shnong kan leit thied noh da u syiem u ban synshai bisharhalorjong ki. la kane kajingaijingmulbun ki newiangbali kila sdang ban pyrshah namar ki ong ba U Jin ula maham lypa ia ki jingeh ki ban wan na ka jinglong syiem. Hynrei ki rangbah Mustoh bad Shala ki batai hana, ba u Syiem uba ki thmu urn long kum kiwei pat ki syiem kiba ki i'ohi sawdong jong ki. U Syiem jong ki 12 shnong un long u syiem uba ki da thied da u sbai bad u ban leh tang ia kaei kaba ki bthah. Lym kumta ka 132 Hima kan sah khlem nong bishar synshar namar ba ym don ba treh ban shimti ia kane ka kam. Hadien ka jingiatainia kaba jur, ka durbar ka mynjur kum ka jingpyrshang ban leit thied syiem na dkhar bad ka aiti ia kata ka kam ha U JaTong bad U Bonai ban wad ia u briew na ka jait syiem uba treh ban wan bishar synshar ha ka dor 23 pen u sbai. U JaTong bad U Bonai kila leit beit beit sha Surong Durgapur bad kila Toh ia uwei u samla syiem uba mon sngewbha ban wan long syiem ha ka dor 23 pen u sbai. Une u long u khun syiem khatduh jong ka Ting syiem Durgapur bad ia ka kyrteng jong u la tip kum U Ganga Singh. Kine ki rangbah Shala kila i'athuh ruh ba ka Hima, nalor ka 23 pen u sbai kan ai ruh ha u ia ka Hat-bam-Syiem bad pynbiang ia ka jaka shong jaka sah jong u baroh. Ha ka step kaba bud bran ki wan da ka lieng bad ki poi ha ka sngi Hat Kait-thang ha ka por janmiet. Te, namar ba ym pat dep shna Ting shna sem; ki Rangbah bad ka durbar kila kyrpad ia u JaTong bad U Bonai ban nang ai jaka ia u shipor ha Ting jong ki. Khnang ba une U Syiem un nym tip shibun shaphang ka Hima, la i'akut ban shna ia ka Ting syiem jong u ha Tynger kawei na ki shnong kiba rit jong ka Hima. Tang shu dep tei ka Ting, ki Talam ia U sha Tynger bad da shisha u pynpaw ia ka mynsiem kit hima bad u trei shitom namar jong ka. Kumba ju long ka nojir arsngi hapoh phra sngi u hap ban hiar shong bishar ha Shala bad kumjuh ruh shisien saw sngi u hap ban leit sha Hat Pdia ban peit ia ka dan ka khrong bad ka few ka Hat. Ha ka por tlang pat u hap ban leit sha Phali man ba don durbar ban ia pynbeit ia ki kam hima sima. 133 i) Ka Durbar U Ganga Singh Katkum ka jingkheifi jong U Shloi Duwakdar bad U Ksan Mastor: U Ganga Singh u shimti ia ka kam kum u syiem ka Hima ki 12 shnong (ia kaba la tip paitbah kum ka Hima Sheila) ha ka Tlang jong ka snem 1731. Ha kane ka Durbar kaba nyngkong U Ganga Singh ula ai jingmut ia ka durbar ba ia ka Hat Kaitthang yn khot noh ka Hat Pdia khnang ba ki dkhar ki lah ban sngewthuh lang. U ai jingmut ruh ba ia ka Hat Phali ne Pahari Bazar dei ban pynheh ia ka. U kular ban leit ia kynduh da lade ia ki mahajon dkhar bad pynshlur ia ki ba kin wan sha kine ki hat. Kane kajingai jingmut jong u kala pynsngewbha ia ki rangbah bad ki paitbah ka hima. Sa kawei pat ka jingai jingmut jong u ka long ba ia ki rai durbar baroh dei ban da thoh ha ka bui. Lehse kane ka long ka sien kaba nyngkong ha ka history ka Hima Sheila ba ia ki rai baroh la thoh da u khulom sner bala wieh ha ka umsoh Ortoki ha ka ktien Bangla. la kane ruh ka durbar kala mynjur. Nangta ula ai jingmut ba namar ba ka Hima Shelia kam don riti Phoidari satia u sngew ba kane ka hukum ka dei ban don ha ka hima: ba ia kino kino kiba leh ki kam runar kam dakaid pyrshah ia la u para nongshong shnong dei ban buh da ka aifl kaba pyrkhing. Ki rangbah kila kylli jingmut na u ha kano ka rukom yn buh pyrkhing haba ki Sande kila don ia la ki riti synshar bishar bad ki aift ki kanun kiba biang halor kane. U Ganga Singh u ai jingmut ba kino kino ki Phoidari kiba ki Sande kim kot bor ban bishar kin wan sha u bad lada lap ka sabut kaba biang ia kum kine ki riewrunar dei shisyndon ban tylliat da u maw. la kane ruh ki rangbah bad ka durbar ki mynjur. Haduh mynta dang don sah u Maw-tylliat u Ganga Singh ha 134 Tynpor, bad da shisha kane ka rai ka pynsma khlieng her ia baroh ki riewrunar ha ka hima. U ai jmgmut ruh ba ka Hima ka dei ban shop khewa ia ki lieng baroh kiba wan kiew na dkhar ha Phali bad kane ka peisa kan leit sha ka hima. Kane lei lei ka jingai jingmut kala nangpynsngewbha shuh shuh ia ki Rangbah bad la ong ba ka nam bad ka burom jong u Ganga Singh ka la her sha kawei pa kawei ka thliewilng hapoh ka hima Sheila. Baroh ki pyrto ia ka jingstad pyrkhat ki Mustoh bad ki Shala ban pyni'oh ha ki 12 shnong ia u Syiem uba stad kum U Ganga Singh. Hynrei tang ka por ka ap husiar bad ka peitthuh dngong. ii) Ka Bishar Synshar U Ganga Singh Ha ka liang ka ktien ka thylliet bad ka aibuit aibor u Ganga Singh u long uba shai bad man ki khep u pynpaw ia la ka jingtbit. Ki jingai jingmut jong u barabor ki long kiba kordor bad ba dei ban iaroh; hynrei ha ka liang ka nia ka jutang bad ka bishar mokotduma u kham duna; namar ba dang don ki riewsaid ba rangbah kum ki jong U Bosan, U Snakon na Nongwar; U Giri na Mustoh bad U Bonai, U Jaiong na Shala: bad man ka por ki rai mokotduma jong u ki rem ha ka Durbar Hima. Kane ka la pynmong shikatdei eh ia U Ganga Singh namar ba urn lah ban leh san ha ki kam hima sima. Ha la mynsiem u atnud khuipyrshah ia kine ki rangbah bad um ju sngewtynnad satia ia ki, wat la habar um ju pynpaw. La katta ruh suki suki u pyrshang ban bat ia la ka bor bad ban bishar katba u sngewmon ne katba ki lok jong u ki aibuit ia u. Kane ka jingleh kala pynmong ia kiba bun ki rangbah ka hima bad ki ruh ki ap thik ia ka por. La ong hadien sansnem 135 ba ula synshar ula pyrshang ban lyndet bad Tuhroit ia ki dustur riti bishar synshar ka Hima bad um bud ia ki riti kiba ki saw Duwakdar kila buh bad u thap shim ia ka bor bishar synshar baroh ha lade. Ha kawei ka por U Nising na Sinai u Tapher jingmut bad ki lok ki jong U Ganga Singh na Tynger bad kine ki leit pharep ha u Ganga Singh ba U Nising hana u long uba aiksuid U Ganga Singh u summon ia u Nising ban wan hajir ha Kashari ha hat Pdia. Ha kata ka durbar ki don bun ki Rangbah kiba wan sngap khnang kaei ka rai ba U Ganga Singh un ai halor U Nising. Tang shu sdang ka Durbar, U Ganga Singh U sei ka kot bad u pule ia ka rai ba u ai halor U Nising. U Nising u bym bna ei ei, u tang shu i'ohsngew ia kane ka rai ula lynftiar kliang ha Durbar. Ki Rangbah da ka bor kila pynsahngeh bad pyntngen ia U Nising. Hadien kata, U Bonai ula i'eng bad ula buh kane ka jingkylli, “Mano Syiem ba la kern bad nishan ia U Nising ba phi hap ban ai kane ka rai kaba kyrkieh halor jong u ?” “Balei ngan i'athuh ia ki nongkem nongnishan, haba nga kum u Syiem nga da tip skhem ba kine kiba nishan bad ba kern ki long ki briew kiba donburom bad ba lah ban shaniah," jubab syndet U Ganga Singh. “Kiei kita ki rangbah kiba donburom bad ba lah ban shaniah, hato ki don ma hangne ?” kylli pyrshah U Bonai. “Hoid, ki don hangne,” la jubab U Ganga Singh. “Lada ka long kumta,” kern ktien U Bonai, “Ka rai kaba phi ai ka dang duna namar ia ka kyrteng jong ki ym shym la kynthoh satia ha kane ka rai.” Saw kyrang laifi U Ganga Singh bad khynfiiuh rem kita ki amgut na Tynger. “Sa kawei pat,” ban ktien U Bonai, “Hato don jingbishar hok ma khlem da ailad ia u shahmudui ban saitda ia lade ?” Ir khih ka durbar baroh kawei. Nangta, kern ktien U 136 Giri, “Kane ka rai kaba khlem pan jubab ne ai sakhi ne pynshisha i'ano U Nising U aiksuid, Ka long ka rai kaba buh ia ngi ka durbar baroh kawei ha kajinglyngngoh bad jingartatien. Te, lada ka burom jong u syiem kan Tai bteng bad pynmih kum kine ki jait rai: ka hima kan jot bad ka banbor kan synshar.” Shaw risa u paitbah ka durbar. “Nga kyrpad ia u syiem ba shisyndon u dei ban pynduh ia kane ka rai lymda u sei ia ki sakhi bad pynsabut ba U Nising u aiksuid ia uta uta: lym kumta ngi ka durbar baroh kawei ngi pyrshah ia kane ka rai banbor. Ym dei ba u mawtylliat un hap tang halor U Nising hynrei ha ngi uwei pa uwei uba u syiem bad ki lok jong u ki shan khmat. Mynta ngi sngewthuh ba ka bishni ka dhon kala i'oh jaka ban shong khet ha ka Hima Shelia.” Kita ki Rangbah na Tynger ki shu dem la ki khlieh katba U Bonai u batai jai ia kaei kaba U Giri bad U Bosan ki pynshait nia bad u pynbor ia U Syiem ba u dei shisyndon ban weng noh ia kane ka rai bymman kaba long pyrshah ia ka dustur ka riti jong ka Hima Sheila. Namar, lada kine ki briew na Tynger ki don ei ei ban nishan pyrshah ia U Nising, ki dei ban buh shuwa hakhmat U Sande Sinai. Nalor nangta, U Syiem um don hok ban tuklar ia ka bishar jong U Sande lymne pdiang ia kano kano ka Mokotduma lymda la wanrah da U Sande. Nangta, ka durbar ka dawa ba dei ban pynshitom ia kine ki amgut kiba shu pharep sniew ia U Nising khlem daw bad kiba u syiem u ong ba ki long kiba donburom bad kiba lah ban shaniah. U Ganga Singh um nud ang wat tang shikyntien ruh, namar mynta u sngewthuh ba ula hap ha ka rem. U Giri, U Bonai bad U Snakon ynda kila Vohi ia kane, kila kren sha ki Rangbah ka Durbar ki ong, “Hato ka durbar ka 137 mynjur mo ba kane ka rai U Syiem kan sah bad ba yn tylliat ia U Nising khlem daw ?” “Em, em,” wan ka jubab na ka Durbar. Ka durbar shisyndon ka pynduh ia kane ka rai bad ka shaifl kuna shipen u sbai ia kine ki rangbah kiba pharep lamler pyrshah ia U Nising. U Ganga Singh bad ki lok ki atkhui bad ka durbar ka wai. iii) Ka Palki U Ganga Singh Hadien ba U Ganga Singh ula synshar kumba 15 snem ia ka Hima Sheila, ka nam bad ka burom jong u kala par kylleng ka ri Khasi bad ri dkhar. Ka jingstad jong u ban khroh ia ki mahajon dkhar ban wan sha Hat Pdia bad Hat Phali kala wanrah ia ka spah bad ka jingmanbha ha ka hima baroh kawei. Ki briew ki im suk pahuh pahai namar ba ka synshar ka khadar ka beit ka ryntih ba don ki kaida bad ki riewrangbah kiba peit miet bad sngi ia ka bha ka miat jong ka hima. Hynrei ha ki bor kiba habar ki tip tang ia ka nam jong U Ganga Singh bad ka burom jong ka Hima Sheila. Suki suki ka jingsarong ka rung ha U Ganga Singh bad u klet noh ba u long tang u Syiem uba ki paitbah kila thied ia u da u sbai. Kane ka pynlong kumta namar ba u don katto katne ki lokna Lyngkien (Nongbah), Tyngrong, Tynger bad Nongtrai kiba pynkiew skong ia u. U Ganga Singh ruh u ieit u sngewtynnad ia ki bad u theh lut la ka jingshaniah ha ki. Ha kawei ka step kine ki lok jong u kila wanpoi jraifi dangstep. U Ganga Singh da kaba kmen u pdiang burom ia ki bad u khawai ka bam ka dih kyrhai. Hapdeng jong kane ka jingiakmen ia sngewbha u Ganga Singh u pyni la ki jingeh ban Taid kjat naduh Tynger haduh Hat Pdia namar ba ula kham noh ka met. 138 “Lada ngan jin da la synshar ha ri dkhar, ki khun ki hajar jongnga kin bah ia nga ha ka Palki. Hangne nga synshar ia ka ri kaba riewspah bad ba tuid da ka dud bad ka ngap, pynban nga hap ban raid da ka kjat thop shi thop. Te kumno keifi ki para syiem para bakhraw kin burom ia nga !" U Snge na Lyngkien, uba ju shang ia ka ri dkhar u sngewthuh ia kane ka jingkren U Ganga Singh bad u batai ha la ki jong ki lok kumno ki briew ha ri dkhar ki burom syiem. “Ka dei ka mon jongphi keifi syiem," pynbud sa ki lok jong u na Tynrong, Nongtrai bad Tynger; “ba lada phi sngewthuh ia la ka bor syiem: shisyndon pynmih da ka hukum ban bah palki ia phi kylliang kylliang man ka hat da ki shnong.” Kane ka jingai jingmut kala ngam jlang ha ka jabieng U Ganga Singh bad kumta kumta hi u pynmih ka rai ba man ka Hat Pdia ar shnong kin phah nongbah maramgut na kawei kawei ban bah palki ia u; bad ia kane yn sdang da ka shnong Shala bad shnong Mustoh naduh ka Hat Pdia ka ban wan. U phah ruh ia kine ki lok ban pyntip ia kane ka khubor ha ki shnong baroh. Ha ka sngi Hat Pdia kaba bud U Ganga Singh u lap ba ym don ba mih briew na Mustoh bad Shala ban bah palki ia u. Da ka jingbitar u hiar sha Hat Pdia ryngkat ki lok jong u. Ki Rangbah rangsan ruh na kiwei ki shnong jraifi ki hiar ban leit durbar ha kata ka sngi hat. Tang shu sdang ka durbar, jraifi U Ganga Singh u kyrhuh ia ki Mustoh bad Shala balei ba ki nud ban pynkheifi ia ka rai Syiem khlem da phah briew ban bah Palki ia u. Ki riew rangbah bad ki Kaida kila ong ia u Giri ban jubab haior kane bad U Giri u i'eng da kaba khublei ia u syiem bad ka durbar u ong, “Syiem badon burom, ngi la ioh ia kane ka hukum lyngba U Snge na Nongbah: hynrei ynda ki rangbah 139 jong u Sande Mustoh kila shong pyrkhat halor kane; ki dap da ka jinglyngngoh nangno kaba kum kane ka hukum ka mih. Ngi don hangne baroh ki rangbah jong ki shnong ki shnong hynrei ym don ba bna satia ba ka durbar ka ia pynmih kum kane ka hukum. U Sande Mustoh um lah ban pdiang ia ka hukum u syiem lymda ka wan lyngba ka Durbar hima. Hato phi sngewdei mo ba ma ngi ki Kaida bad ki kynrad kin bah Palki ia phi u syiem uba ngi la shu thied da ka dor jong u sbai ? Nga ieng hangne ban kylli na ki para rangbah baroh jong ka Durbar hato kane ka hukum u syiem ka long ma kaba shong flia ? Bad lada ka durbar ka ong ba kam long kaba shongnia, shisyndon u syiem u dei ban pynduh ia kane ka hukum bad nga khot ia ka durdbar ban i'eng kum ka sakhi ba ka kwah ba u syiem u dei shisyndon ban weng noh ia kane ka rai.” Baroh u paitbah u i'eng bad u Ganga Singh u sah marwei tang bad ki katto katne ngut ki fiiangkohnguh jong u. U Bonai, U Snakon, U Bosan, U Jaiong bad U Rngin ki kyntu ba u syiem shisyndon u dei ban pynbna ba ula weng noh ia kane ka hukum; lym kumta ka durbar kan nirad syiem ia u. U Ganga Singh u poi ha ka lehraifi bad jahburom bad um banse ban pynbna ba ula weng noh ia ka hukum bah Palki ia u. U paitbah ka durbar ula risa laisien laiwat bad ka burbar ka wai noh. U Ganga Sing u sat ha la ka dohnud pyrshah ia u Giri bad ki lok jong u: hynrei um tip satia ba kito baroh ki dei ki Kaida bad ki rishot jong ka Hima kiba ka kyntien jong ki ka long ka aifi. Sniew bok ba ha kata ka sngi hat U Giri u bun kam shane shatai hapoh hat bad u mih khatduh briew ban wan sha shnong. U Ganga Singh bad ki lok jong u ki Tohi ia kane bad ki 140 ap thap ha lynti. Tang shu poi ha ka jaka ba biang ki tied ia u haduh ban da jem bad ki thang ia ki tmaifi ki tmoh jong u baroh. Da kaba shitom u poi sha shnong bad u i'athuh ia kaba la jia baroh ha u shnong u thaw ryngkat kaba bthah artad kumne, "Ngim dei ma ngi ki ban ktah kti ia u mraw uba ngi la thied, hynrei ngin aiti ha kiwei pat ban leh ia kane ka kam. leh ia kane ka kam ha nga, bad ha ka por kaba biang ngan sa pyni la ka bor. Hynrei leit bak bak mynta sha Nongwar bad i'athuh ha U Bosan bad U Snakon ia kaba la jia baroh bad ong ia ki ban ap ia ka jubab na nga ynda nga wanphai na Nonglwai Kumjuh ruh u phah briew katto katne ngut ban i'athuh ia U Jaiong, U Bonai bad U Rngin ia kaba la jia baroh bad ong ia ki ban ap ia ka jubab na u tad ynda u wanphai na Nonglwai. Ha kata hi ka miet U Giri u mih bak na la shnong ban leit sha Nonglwai bad shikynhun ki nong bud nongrap. iv) Ka Thma pyrshah U Ganga Singh Ka khubor ba U Giri ula shah leh beijot ha U Ganga Singh bad ki lok jong u kala par stet ha ka Hima baroh kawei. Ki riew rangbah kila sat sia, hynrei kim mon ban leh ei ei namar ba U Giri u khang ba ki kynrad kim dei ban pyniPp ne pynhlar kput ma ki ia u mraw: ka dei ka kamram jong kiba lait ban leh ia kata ka kam. Ynda ki tip ba U Giri bad ka kynhun jong u kila leit sha Nonglwai; ki rangbah na ki shnong ki shnong ki pynkhreh bad ap triang ia ka por. Ki Nonglwai, kiba la long teng ki lok jong ki Shala tang shu Tohsngew ba u Giri u wanpoi, khrui ki ia lum ha llng-kur Jyrwa. Ynda kila Tohsngew ia kiei kiei baroh kila kular ban Yarap ia u ban weng ia kane ka lehraifi: tang ba ki Khaifi bad ki Jyrwa kin Tateh lok. U Giri bad ki nongbud jong u ki kular da 141 kaba kmen hakhmat U Ksan bad U Snabeift ki rangbah kur ki Nonglwai. U Giri u pynpaw ba ia ka jingleh niam tiengkur u kwah ban leh iaka hakhmat la ki kur ha Mustoh. Hadien ba la dep ka kfiia ka khriam kaba pynpaw ia ka jingjop; jraifi ki mih na Nonglwai ryngkat ka kyrkhu kyrdoh jong ki kur ki kmie bad bran ki wan sha Mustoh. Ynda ki poi hajan Mustoh ki lap ba kine ki kur Khaifi kila ap lypa ha Lad Ka Dker bad hangta hangta hi ki pynlong ia ka jingiasuit ia tang teh lok hapdeng ki Jyrwa bad ki Khaifi ryngkat ka khawai ka dawai bad ka leh kmen leh sngewbha. Ha kata hi ka miet ki phah briew sha Nongwar ban iathuh ia U Bosan bad U Snakon bad kumjuh ruh ia ki jong U Jai'ong, U Rngin bad U Bonai ba kirn lum ia ki riewthma bad ia kynduh lang ha Pyn-a bad dangstep kin tur pyrshah ia U Ganga Singh bad ka kynhun jong u kiba pahara ia ka Ting syiem jong u ha Tynger. Kumno re kumno uwei u briew na Nongbah (Lyngkien) uba don ha Mustoh ha kata ka miet ula leit bran sha shnong ban iathuh ia ki lok U Ganga Singh ba ki Nonglwai bad U Giri kin thorn ia ka Ting syiem ha ka step kaba bud. Ki lok U Ganga Singh shimiet shimiet ki rah ia kane ka khubor sha Tynger bad pynsngew ha ki skhor U Ganga Singh. Ki da iathuh ruh ba ki Nongwar hapoh ka jingi'alam U Bosan bad U Snakon ryngkat ki Shala hapoh ka jingialam U Rngin, U Jai'ong bad U Bonai kila ap lypa ha Pyn-a. U Ganga Singh um don por satia ban lum ia ki lok jong u na Tynrong, na Nongtrai bad Nongbah. Ki lok jong u ruh na Tynger tang shu i'ohsngew ia kane ka khubor ki ran rud bad kirn nud khih. Shimiet shimiet U Ganga Singh ryngkat katto katne ki nongbud nongrap jong u bran ki phet na Tynger lyngba 142 ka Nongtrai sha Nonglait da kaba ki thmu oan her Tap sha ri dkhar. Ka kynhun U Giri ynda kila tip na ki Dewsaw ba U Ganga Singh bad ki lok kila phetiap sha ki thain Nongtrai, wut ki bud dien. Ynda ki poi ha Nongtrai la i'athuh ia ki ba ki phai shaphang Nonglait. Shikynhun ki rangkieng wait kiengstieh bakhlaifi bad ba stet ki beh thong nadien bad ha ka por nohphai sngi ki lap ngung ia ki ha pynnoh Nonglait. Ki Nonglwai ki sei la ki ryntieh bad ki khnam bad ki siat ia ki khlem da lait wat tang uwei ruh ban ryngkang sha ri dkar. Ki mait ia ka khlieh U Ganga Singh bad ki sieh ha u siej ryngkat ka duhoi ka risa jop thma. Tang shu poi ha Shala ki pynlong ka khawai ka dawai kaba heh bad ki i'ashad i'akmen baroh shimiet. Tang shu riew u Syiaf nyngkong jrairi ki i'eng ban kiew sha Mustoh bad ki sieh ia ka khlieh U Ganga Singh ha Pyndem Sande. Laisngi laimiet ki pynlong ka phur ka shad ryngkat ka khawai dawai ryngkat ka leh niam leh rukom. Ynda la dep kine baroh ki rangbah bad ki paitbah ryngkat ka ksing ka dhah ka shad ka kmen ki leit on lynti ia ki Nonglwai haduh Mawhat ha Pynter bad ki pynlong ka jingi'a khublei bad jingianguh mar kylliang. Ka khana pateng ka i'athuh ba ki Jyrwa ki long kiwei na ki nongsiat khnam kiba tbit bad bakhlaifi haduh katta katta bad ki rang kieng wait kiengstieh ruh kiba kat ki rang kiengwait kiengstieh kiba stet ban talaifi wait kum ka leilieh. La Tathuh ruh ba U Ksan bad u Snabeifi ki lah ban siat wat ia u soh ne ka pylleng halor ka khlieh jong u briew na jngai khlem da pynmong wat ia uwei u shniuh ruh. Dei naduh kane ka por ki Khaifl bad ki Jyrwa ki ia tieng-lok bad ka kut ruh ka jingsynshar syiem ha ka Hima Shelia. Mynta ki kynmaw ia ka 143 jingkren jong U Jin bad ki sngewthuh ba ka Hima Shelia, lada ka dei ban raid shaphrang: horkit kam dei ban raid lait na ki jingsneng jingpyni jong u: lym kumta ki jingeh kin lynsher lynter tait. KA DURBAR HIMA I V) (Hadien U Ganga Singh) Ka jingi'ap jong U Ganga Singh ka long ka jingjop jong ka synshar paitbah ha ka Hima Shelia: kaba U Jin kum u nongseng jong ka ula maham ba kawei pat ka rukom jingsynshar kan pyntroifi thiaw ia ka Hima Shelia. Kane da shisha ka urlong bad ki tymmen ki san ryngkat ki Kaida bad ki rangbah nongTalam jong ka hima sa shisien pat ki shong ban pyrkhat jylliew halor kane ka phang. Sa shisien pat ki khot kyrkieh ia ka durbar Hima ha Phali ban ia phylliew jingmut halor kane ka phang . Ka mat jong ka jingiakren kaba nyngkong ban pynpaw ia ka jingsngewnguh sngewburom ia ki Jyrwa kiba la wan i’arap ia ki ban jop ia U Ganga Singh: U Syiem mraw ba leh trai khlieh bad thombor ia u paitbah bad ka hima. Ki pynpaw ruh ia ka jingsngewnguh ba sa shisien pat ka Hima Shelia ka lait na ki kynjri ka jinglong mraw hapoh ki syiem ban i'eng rasong pat kum ka Hima kaba laitluid ha kaba ka Synshar paitbah ba pura sa shisien pat kan san kan thylleng. Ka Durbar ruh ka pynpaw ia ka jingsngewnguh da kaba ka phah ia ki jingai sngewbha ba kordor sha ki Kur Jyrwa ha Nonglwai lyngba ki briew kiba sian ba sngewthuh kiba ka Hima ka jied kyrpang na Durbar kum ki nonglam ktien jong ka Hima. Ka Durbar ka pynsngewthuh ruh ba kumba U Giri u i’eng khmat na ka bynta ka Hima bad da ka mon sngewbha u ia-teh lok bad 144 ki Jyrwa; to ai ba u juh u ksai jong ka jingi'aieit ia sngewbha un teh song ia ki bad ka Hima Shelia kumjuh. Ka Durbar ruh ka pynpaw ia la ka jingsngewnguh sngewburom ia U Giri uba la weng bad kyndat ia ka lehbor thombor, ka lehraifi bad ka jahburom ka hima da kaba u peifi ia la ka jingim ban Taleh pyrshah ia U Ganga Singh ba khwan bor. Ha kajuh ruh ka por ka pynpaw la ka jingsngewnguh ia U Bosan, U Shakon, U Lwai, U Jaiong, U Rngin bad ryngkat kito baroh kiba ia don bynta ha kane ka kam Tap kam im jong ka Hima: kiba na ka bynta ka burom ka ijot jong ka Hima ki kloi ban phah ia la ka jingim: bad lymda dei ka jingshlur bad jingdoh satar jong ki ka Hima Sheila kan kylla long ka Hima Tynshop jong ka jingshah rkhie bein hapdeng para khun syiem khun hima. Ka Durbar ka sngewdei ruh ban buh ha ka jingkynmaw ba kano kano ka wei pat ka rukom synshar khadar ka ban mih nalor kaba U Jin ula phriang madan ha Shyrten bad ba la pdiang shityllup da ki paitbah ka Hima 23 shnong: kan lynsher kylla ia ki paitbah bad ka Hima Sheila. Ka durbar ka rai ruh da kawei ka jingmut ban khot ia ka Durbar pyllun hadien ar-hat (Phra sngi) ha kaba yn jied ia ki duwakdar balor ka nongrim bad ka nomuna na mynbarim kaba U Jin ula ruid phang bad ba la pdiang pyllun da ka Durbar ki 23 shnong ha Shyrten ha ka Hang jong ka snem 1662. VI) Ka Durbar Hima II Ha ka Tlang jong ka snem 1 763 bad katkum ka rai jong ka durbar Hima I hadien ka jingTap jong U Ganga Singh Syiem la pynlong ia ka durbar jied Duwakdar pyllun ha Phali. Ha kane 145 ka durbar la wanmih baroh ki khmat rangbah balit na ki 12 shnong katkum ba la pynjari paitbah da ki rangbah ki rangsan bad ki Kaida jong ka Hima. Da kawei ka jingmut kila ia rai ban khyllie biang ia ka jinglong Duwakdar ha ka hima da kaba pynskhem ia baroh ki kular kiba la i'ateh ha Shyrten. Ki pynskhem ruh ba ia ki duwakdar dei ban jied paitbah ha khmat durbar bad ia kino kino kiba shah jied lada ki kyntait yn masorkha na ka hima ryngkat ka kuna 23 pen u sbai; bad kine ki duwakdar kin neh shirta ha ka kam. La i'akut ruh ba yn jied ia kitei ki saw ngut ki duwakdar tang na ka kpoh kitei ki duwakdar tymmen: kata, na ka kpoh U Bor, U Steifi, U Kynshe bad U Jerkha; ia kiba la tip pateng kum ki Saw Seng na Shala, bad ym shym la ailad satia ia ki Nongjrong ban i'oh bynta ha kane ka kam namar haduh kata ka por baroh ki khun ki ksiew jong kitei ki Saw duwakdar tymmen ki dang shong dang sah tang ha Shala. Halor katei ka nongrim la jied ia kine harum ban long ki bteng duwakdar - 1 . U Amor I uba hiar pateng na U Bor. 2. U Jitrai I uba hiar pateng na U Kynshe. 3. U Taprai I uba hiar pateng na U Steifi. 4. U Khana uba hiar pateng na U Jerkha. Ka durbar kala kylli markhmat la kin pdiang ne em ia kane ka jingjied jong ka durbar bad baroh saw ngut ki mynjur ban shimti ia kane ka kam kaba ka durbar kala tynrong halor jong ki. Ka durbar kala risa bad la pynskhem ia ki kum ki duwakdar ka Hima Sheila baroh shi umor. Naduh kane ka snem ka jingsynshar ha ka Hima Sheila ka neh thik ha ki Saw Duwakdar bad ka hima ka raid shaphrang 146 ha ka spah bad ka burom ryngkat ka jingsuk bad jingshngairt. Ki tei ki Saw Duwakdar ki synshar haduh ka thma Mawkhyrdop ha Mawmluh 1812-14 mynba u Konrai Syiem u synshar ha Khatsawphra bad U Haifi Sing u synshar kum U Syiem khynnah ha Mawmluh. Hadien ka jingiap jong kitei ki Duwakdar ka Hima Sheila kala jied sa ia kine napdeng ki Saw Seng ban long ki Duwakdar bad kine ki synshar haduh ki sngi ka jingwan ki phareng bad kita ki long - 1 . U Mihsnge uba hiar pateng na U Jerkha. 2. U Sohmen uba hiar pateng na U Kynshe. 3. U Donkha uba hiar pateng na U Steift. 4. U Ksan uba hiar pateng na U Bor. Katkum ka jingkheifi jong U Shloin Duwakdar bad U Timo- thy Evangelist: kitei ki duwakdar ki shimti ia ka kam hadien jong ka 'Ma Mawkhyrdop. Ka ‘Ma Mawkhyrdop ka bthei ha ka snem 1812 bad ka kut ha ka snem 1814. Katkum ka jingpashat jingmut U Rangbah B. Wollington bad U Rangbah S. M. Ropmay kitei ki sawngut ki Duwakdar ki sdang synshar naduh ka snem 1816. Ki nati ki pynsabut ba dei kitei ki duwakdar kiba la ia soi sorkular nyngkong eh bad ki phareng ha ka snem 1826 shuwa ba kino kino ki syiem Khasi kin ia teh soskular bad ki phareng. Ki nati ruh ki I'athuh ba kitei ki duwakdar ki long kiba khatduh eh ban bat ia ka kam duwakdar shirta. Hadien ka jingwan ki phareng ka kam Duwakdar ka neh tang 3 snem, 8 snem bad 5 snem. Bad khatduh ia wai ka term Duwakdar ka neh tang 5 snem bad kane ka dang Yaid haduh mynta. 147 vii) Ki Sngi Khatduh U Jerkha Ka Ai'om jingsynshar Duwakdar, ka da long shisha ka ai'om ksiar ha ka history ka Hima Sheila: namar ka long ka aVom ha kaba kajingsuk jingsaifi, ryngkat ka jingshngaifl bad jingpahun pahai ki tap bad synshar ia ka Hima baroh kawei. La paw ha ki khanatang ba ka Hima Shelia ka long kaba riewspah tarn, ba shai bad ba pawkhmat eh ha ka Ri Khasi Jaintia. Namar ba ki nongsynshar bishar ki long kiba jynsur jingmut jingpyrkhat bad Tohi jngai, la shem ba ym don mokotduma ne jingi'aleh jingiakynad, namar ba ki nang ban tern bad khem urn jem umjah. Katkum ki nojir ba la sabut bun ki mokotduma ki kut ha ki rai rajinoma. Hynrei ki sngi jong ka jinglong tymmen bad jingsah tang marwei ha ka kam; namar lai-ngut na ki duwakdar kila i'ap, kirn long satia ki sngi kiba suk. Katkum ka rai na Shyrten, la i'akut durbar ba ki Duwakdar kin synshar - bishar shirta bad ba yn nym pyndap duwakdar katba dang don duwakdar. La ia mynjur durbar lang ruh ban shu thung noh da ki Dewanji ha kano kano ka jaka ba khali, kata, ha kano kano ka jaka jong uno uno u Duwakdar uba i'ap: hynrei ym shym la pynshai pat la kine ki Dewanji kin long napdeng jong ki hi ne lah ban thung da kiwei pat. Ka por ka i'aid bad ki duwakdar ki Tap uwei hadien uwei pat bad mynta sah sa tang U Jerkha; bad u ruh ula tymmen. Kumta ka Durbar ka rai ban thung Dewanji noh ha kine ki jaka ba khali da ki briew kiba sian bad ba nangthoh nangtar. la kane ruh baroh 23 shnong ki ia mynjur; hynrei ym don Khasi pat uba nangthoh nangtar uba treh ban long Dewanji ban i'arap ia U Jerkha Duwakdar tymmen. Ki Khatar shnong - Nongwar, Shala, Mustoh, Nongtrai, Dewsaw, Nongbah, Lyngkhom, 148 Tynger, Umtlang, Mawrap, Rymnong bad Nonglyngkien: namar ba ki nang ban kren Bengali tiak tiak: ki mynjur ban thung Dewanji da ki dkhar bad ban siew ia ki da ka tulop. Hynrei ki 1 1 shnong pat ki Nongkroh, Tyrna, Nongriat, Mynteng, Ramdait, Synnei, Nongshluit, Nongsteng - Umeit, Mawphu, Thieddieng bad Sinai-Mawshynrut, kim mynjur satia ia kane ka jingai jingmut, namar bun na ki kim nang dkhar bad ki sngewrem ban shah synshar bishar ha u dkhar u lyngkien. Ki 12 shnong pat kiba nang Bangla ki sngewthuh ba kine ki Dewanji ki long tang kum ki shakri jong ki, kiba ka hima ka da siew tulop. Ki 1 1 shnong ki i'ohi ba lada ki ailad ia kane ki muktiar kin leh donbor eh bad kin khem ia ki. Namar kata, la mih ka jingi'a turko kaba jur ha ka durbar bad U Jerkha Duwakdar u rai da ka majority. Ba kumta, ki 1 1 ki rem bad ki khlad noh na ka Hima Sheila. Ka snem 1 724 ka long ka snem kaba sah dak Tong ha ka history ka hima Sheila; namar dei ha kane ka snem ba ka Hima ka kad arliang. Ki 1 1 shnong wat la kila mihnoh na ka Hima Sheila, pynban ki bat ia ka hok Trai hat ha Phali. Ki 1 1 shnong ynda kila khlad noh na ka Hima Sheila ki shu shong pdeng kumto khlem ia snoh satia bad kano kano ka Hima. Ha ka snem 1728-29 ki khatsawphra hapoh ka jingi'alam bakhlain bad ba donbor jong U Syiem Laitlyngka; ki la sdang ban kyntur jaka bad pyni'ar hima ia lade. Ki la jop ia ka Kyntur sniang bad beh krad ia U Basan Swerbad U Buhsing Lyngdoh. U Buhsing Lyngdoh bad U Basan Swer ryngkat ki pait ki pyrton ki phetrieh sha Pyrkowdewsaw; hynrei u Sande Pyrkowdewsaw u kyntait ban T'arap. Hapdeng kane ka sohsat, ki Nongsteng ki tyrwa ban Tarap bad ha ka thma pyrshah ia U Laitlyngka, Ki Nongsteng ryngkat U Basan Swerbad U Buhsing ki jop thiaw. 149 Hyruei ka shimpor ia U Buhsing Lyngdoh bad U Basan Swer ban seng ia ka Hima Sohra haduh ka snem 1795. Ynda la seng ia ka Hima Sohra ki Mawphu, Ki Thieddieng, Ki Nongsteng bad ki Umeit-Umblai ki ia snoh noh bad ka da kaba kyrshan ia U Buhsing bad U Basan Swer ban tei ia ka Nongbah jong u ha Sohra khnang ban khanglad ia ki lai-shnong - Ki Ryngud, Ki Laitiam bad ki Sohbar ban kyntur jaka. Ka Thma Siat-u-dei ha ka snem 1 787-88 ka long ka thma kaba rai kut ia u pud u sam ka Hima Sohra ha ka jingiadei bad kitei ki laishnong. Katba ki 8 shnong pat - Ki Tyrna, Ki Nongkroh, Ki Ramdait, Ki Nongriat, Ki Mynteng, Ki Nongshluit ki Sinai- Mawshynrut bad ki Synnei' ki shong pdeng bad kirn mon ban Yasnoh bad no bad no ruh. Kine ki shnong ki kylla long llaka Sorkar noh hapoh ka jingpyniaid ki Sirdar ynda ki phareng ki wan bad jop ia kane ka Ri Khasi. Ba Kumta, naduh ka snem 1724 ka Hima Shelia ka kynthup tang ia ki 12 shnong - Nongwar, Shala, Mustoh, Nongbah, Nongtrai, Dewsaw, Tyngnger. Lyngkhom, Rymnong, Mawrap, Nonglyngkien, Umtlang: bad naduh ka snem 1765 ka Hima Sheila ka kynthup sa tang 9 shnong namar ka Mawrap, Nongbah bad Nonglyngkien ki khlad noh na ka ban long ki shnong Sorkar hapoh ka jingsynshar Sirdarship. vii) Ki Hat Ki lew: Ka Khali Pateng la ka Hima 23 shnong ba la tip kum ka Hima Shelia: la byhshet haior artylli ki hongrirh kiba skhem - Ka jingYatylll bor Idng (coflecfive Security) bad Kf Hat ki Tew ka Khali ka pateng. KI lap ba don tang kawei ka lyhti bah kaba pynlasnoh ia ka ri Thor bad ka them Ri War ki 23 shnOng bad kata ka long ka Wah fiakra he ka wafi UmYarh. Ha'dien ba ki 23 shnong ki la rai 150 ban pynlong kawei ka Hima na Shyrten: ban ia tylli lang kawei pyrshah ia kano kano ka bor kaba thmu ban thorn: la ka bor na ri Lum ne na Ri Thor: ka mat kaba bud ka long ki Hat ki lew ka Khail pateng. Da ka jingstad ki Duwakdar ki la pynlong ia ka Hat Pdia. Suki suki kane ka Hat kala roi bad bun ki nongkhail dkhar na kylleng ka Bengal ki wan ban ia khail pateng bad ki Khasi. Haba ka khail ka pateng ka roi ki briew ki manbha bad ki riewspah bad pynlah ia ki ban pyni'ar la ka rep ka riang ka thung ka tep. Ki duwakdar ruh ki trei shitom ban gibuit ailynti kumno ban trei ban ktah bad kumno ban nang pynjur ia kg jingi'a dei Tajan bad ki dkhar. Barabor ki leit sha ri dkhar ban wad ki lad thymmai ban trei kam. Hapoh ka jingi'alam jong ki, ki briew jong ka Hima 23 shnong mynta kirn im shuh tang da ka rep shisnem, hynrei ki pyrshang ban thung da ki jingthung kiba neh rta bad kiba ai jingmyntoi lynter. Namar ba ka ri ka long kaba sboh ki hikai ia ki briew ban thung soh thung kwai bad la lap ba kine ki jingthung ki ia dei bha. Hapoh 50 snem ka jingsynshar jong ki, ki khlaw ba rben ki kylla long ki brisoh brikwai kiba wanrah ka spah ka hajar. Ka them 23 shnong ka kylla long ka ri jong ka dgd bad ka ngap. Ynda ka jingpynmih soh pynmih kwai kala jur, ki paitbah 23 shnong ki lap ba ka hat Pdia ka jngai eh bad kg shitom ruh ban leit ban wan ha ka por Lyiur namar ba hap ryngkang ia ka Bakra. Da ka jingstad ki duwakdar ki wanrah noh ia ka ha Sohlap, bad la ailad ruh ban dang don hi ka jingTadie ia thied ha Hat Pdia khamtam ha ka por soh. Suki suki ka Hat Sohlap ka kylla long ka pdeng jong ka khail pgteng jong ka them Ri War bad u budlum jong ka Hima 23 shnong. Hynrei ynda ki 151 brisoh brikwai jong ki Nongjrong kila sdang ban pynmih jingmyntoi; la i donkam ba dei ban don sa kawei pat ka hat Tlang ha Phali khnang ba ki Nongjrong ki lah ban pynpoi la ki mar jong ki ha kane ka Hat. Suki suki ka jingpynmih soh pynmih kwai pynmih sla tyrpat jong ki Nongjrong ka palat bun phew shah ia ka jingpynmih soh ki Shala bad Mustoh na ri thor ri madan. Kane kala pynlong ia ka durbar hima bad ki duwakdar ban shim kabu bad pynlong ia ka Phali, ka pdeng jingkhaii tlang jong ka them Ri War baroh kawei. Da ki hajar ki lieng kit soh ki kievy sha hat Phali man ka sngi ryngkat ki tiar bam tiar dih bad ki jingdonkam baroh jong ki briew ka 23 shnong. La ong ba ym shym don hat don i'ew ka ban iphuh iphieng kat ka Hat Phali ha kito ki juk; bad ym don kawei ruh ka mar kaba ym lah ban shem ha Hat Phali kaba la die ha ki iew ha Bengal. Katkum ba paw na ki riti, ka Hat Pdia ka kylla long ka Hat-barn Duwakdar katba ka Hat Phali ka sah ha ki 23 shnong: wat la ki 1 1 shnong kila khlad noh na ka Hima Sheila. Shaphang ka jingai ia ka Hat Pdia (Kaba kylla long ka Hat Sheila) ym lap sabut satia ba la don kano kano ka jingiateh kular ba la thoh, lait tang ba ki tymmen ki pynkynmaw na ka por sha ka por: ba ia kg.ne la kular ban ai ha ki long duwakdar kiba ka Hima ka thung naduh na Durbar Shyrten 1 662. Katkum ka dorkhas 30 tarik January, 1864, ba la ai da ki khatar shnong ha U Major H. S. Bivar, Deputy Commissioner; bad bala mynjur da ki Duwakdar bad ka Durbar; ka ong kumne, “la kata ka Hat Pdia bad ka Dan soh, ngi baroh 12 shnong, ngi ia mynjur ryngkat bgn ai ha kino kino kiba ngin pynlong Duwakdar ba kin bam namar ba ki korbar na ka bynta jongngi.” Lehse kum ia kata ka Kplgr lah ban shu buh jingkynmaw ha ki Ksah thri namar ka thoh ka tar kam put wan. 152 Shaphang ki hat ki lew jong ka Hima, ka don kane ka kular naduh mynba rim bad kaba dang trei kam haduh kine ki sngi. la kane la thoh hadien ba ki lai-shnong - Ka Mawrap, Ka Nongbah bad Ka Nonglyngkien kila khlad noh na ka Hima Shelia: bad kata ka long kumne:- “Ngi ki 9 shnong bad ki Sawseng Sheila kiba ngin soi kyrteng hapoh ngi la ia seng durbar ha Phali. Ngi Yathoh da kane ka kular shaphang ki hat ba Tew long na mynbarim hapoh llaka Sheila tang 2 (ar) tylli - Ka Hat Pdia bad ka Hat Phali. Mynta dang khyndiat snem la long sa kawei ka hat - Ka Hat Lyba ba dang thaw thymmai. Na ka bynta kane ka Hat Lyba kitei ki hat barim la rit imat kum ban duh noh bad ki briew baroh hapoh llaka Sheila kirn sngewsuk namar ka long ka jinglutksan. Namar kata, dei ban pynduh noh ia katei ka Hat Lyba." “Kumta kino kino ki Wadar ba la long ne ban dang long ym dei ban leit thaw hat ha katei ka Hat Lyba thymmai lane shawei shawei hapoh llaka Sheila. Lada leit te, ia kita ki Wadar yn duh noh na ka kam Wadar khlem don ktien satia; bad napdeng jongngi ki Shelia bad ki 9 shnong ruh kino kino ki ban leit thaw hat ha kata ka Hat Lyba ne shawei shawei hapoh llaka Shelia te yn long kuna Rs. 20/- uwei u briew. la kane, haba dei ia ki Shelia, yn daifl ki Wadar; haba dei ia ki 9 shnong yn daifl hi ha la ki shnong ki shnong. Haba kim lah daifl ha la ka shnong, yn daifl ki Wadar bad ki 9 shnong ha Phali, bad ia ki kular barim kin sah hi kumjuh." la kane ka kular la ia soi ha ka 1 7th ta'rik, July, 1 879 bad ba la ia soi da baroh ki 9 shnong bad 3 ngut ki Wahddaf: bad ia kane kajuh ka kular la pynskhem da U Deputy Commis- sioner ha ka 19 tarik, July, 1912. 153 Shaphang ka Hat Phali ngi i'oh bun ki syrtap jingtip na ki nati mukotduma kiba la long pyrshah U Sirdar Nongbah, uba kam hana, ba ka Hat Phali ka dei ka jong U Skot, U Anal bad U Syrna ba ki 12 shnong ne 23 shnong ki wan buhai hadien. Hynrei kane ka nongrim kam i'eng namar ba ka Nongbah shisien kala long ka bynta jong ki 23 shnong bad kumjuh ruh jong ka 12 shnong: bad ia kane ka hat la seng shuwa ba ki Nongbah kin mih na ka Hima Sheila. Kala don ruh ka jingi'a takhuh bad ki Nongtrai kiba kwah ban thaw kato soh ha Mawsaw bad Sohmanir. Ki 1 2 shnong ki i'eng pyrshah bad u Deputy Com- missioner u rai pynrem ia ki Nongtrai bad khang ia baroh bym bit ban ishna Hat ne Kato soh ha shilynter ka Bakra Sheila; lait noh tang ki Hat jong ka Hima Sheila. Hadien ba ki Tyrna, Nongkroh, Mynteng, Nongriat, Ramdait, Synnei, Sinai bad Nongshluit kirn treh shuh ban la don kti lang ha ka jingpyni'aid ia ka Hat Phali: ki 1 5 shnong ki pynlong kane ka Agreement hapdeng jong ki - “Ngi ki Rangbah bad ki Paitbah na ki 15 shnong Shelia, Mustoh, Nongwar, Nongbah, Nongtrai, Dewsaw, Tynger, Lyngkhom, Umtlang, Rymnong, Nonglyngkien, Nongsteng. Thieddieng, Mawphu, Umeit-Umblai kiba ngin soi kyrteng harum na ka bynta ia lade bad ki paitbah jong ki shnong jong ngi, rhyftfa ngi ia lum Durbar ha Phali bad ngi ia thoh skhem ia kane ka kular da kumne harum:- 1. Naduh mynbarim, ma ngi ki 12 shnong - Shelia, Nongwar, Mustoh, Nongbah, Nongtrai, Dewsaw, Tynger, Lyngkhom, Umtlang, Rymnong, Mawrap bad Nonglyngkien; ngi long ki trai ka Hat Phali, kaba kynthup de ia ka Mawsaw bad Sohrfianir bad etc bad ma ngi ki Thieddieng, Ki Nongsteng, Ki 154 Mawphu, Ki Umeit-Umblai ngi long kiba jiw wan ban Yalang ha hat Phali ban pynkhraw ia ka Hat. 2. Ba ma ngi ki shnong ka Sheila Confederacy kum ki trai ka hat naduh mynbarim ngi la jiw pynVaid pynYeng ia ka Hat Phali tang ma ngi hi ha ka jingiadei bad kaba lum ia ka Musapha bad synftiang bad ha kaba pynlut ruh ha ki khriang, ki jingkieng naduh Shyrten haduh Hat Shelia bad ha kaba pynkhuid ia ki lynti um haduh pud ri dkhar de. Ngi la jiw siew ruh ia ki Wahadadar kum ka buskit bad ia ki nongpyni'aid bad nongtrei jong ka Hat Phali lem bad kiwei kiwei ki jingsiew. 3. Ba mynta, ma ngi ki shnong ka Sheila Confederacy ngi tyrwa mon sngewbha ia phi ki Thiedding, Ki Nongsteng, Ki Mawphu, Ki Umeit-Umblai ba phin ia long trai lang ia kane ka hat Phali ha ki bynta baroh nadong shadong. 4. Ba ma ngi ruh ki Thiedding, ki Nongsteng, Ki Mawphu, Ki Umeit-Umblai, ngi mynjur ia katei ka jingtyrwa mon sngewbha jong ki shnong ka Sheila Confederacy bg ngin ia long trai bad ia trei lem bad phi ia ki kam jingpyni'aid ia ka Hat Phali baroh. 5. Ba ka Durbar pyllun jongngi ki 1 5 shnong ngi ia Yakut (a) Ba kumba ngi la ia long trai kumne baroh 15 shnong, ia ka jingkieng ha Mawtap hapdeng llaka Thiedding bad Nongsteng yn shna da kaba siew na ka fund Phali da kaba aiwai ha Phali. (b) Ba ka jingshna ia ki jingkieng bad lynti um bad khriang jong ki shnong ka Sheila Confederacy yn neh kumjuh kumba jiw long, (k) Ba ka jingsiew burom ia ki Wahadadar kan neh haba da don tyngka na ka Fund Phali kat ka jingibit ka durbar, lem bad kiwei kiwei ki jingsiew yn neh kumjuh. (d) Ba yn thung 155 Secretary bad Treasurer la nangno nangno katba ibit ka durbar 15 shnong, hynrei ia ki manager yn jied da la ki shnong hi: yn long 15 ngut 15 shnong, bad ki shnong kin wan ai kyrteng ha durbar. Hynrei haba jia ba duna tyngka, ka durbar 15 shnong ka lah ban jied tang uwei ne arngut ki manager kat ka jingibit ka durbar. 6. Ba ma ngi ki Thiedding, ki Nongsteng, Ki Mawphu, ki Umeit-Umblai bad kitei ki shnong jong ka Sheila Confederacy baroh 15 shnong: na la ki shnong ki shnong ngi dei ban wanrah la u soh bad sla tyrpad ha Hat Phali: hynrei ia ka jingleit lam soh bad sla tyrpad ha lew Mawsynram bad Tew Sohra tang shikit shikit la shah ia ki Nongsteng, ki Thiedding, Ki Mawphu bad ki Umeit-Umblai ban leit kumba ki ju leh. Kumjuh ruh ia ki jingpynhiar soh kitei ki shnong ha Sheila Confederacy na ki jaka ba jiw pynhiar soh barabor la shah. 7. Ba haba la kut ka Phali, yn long ka durbar nikas. Lada tarn tyngka ei ei yn Tasam ha la ki shnong ki shnong baroh 15 shnong. 8. la ka shnong kaba ym ia long shitylli, ia kaba wan ha hat Phali, yn ym fiiew kaba lah ban i'oh bynta longtrai lang. 9. Lada ha ka arsien long durbar ym lah ban ia beit, te ki Wahadadar kin rai kut ia ka kam. la kane ka kular la soi da baroh ki 1 5 shnong ha ka 4 tarik, January, 1943. Hadien jong kane ki Mawrap ruh ki mynjur ban iasoh lang ba la pynlong ia ka Hat Phali ka Hat jong ki 16 shnong. 156 Nalor kitei ki kular kala don sa kawei pat ka kular kaba ki Rangbah bad paitbah ka 9 shnong kila wanrah hakhmat jong ki Wahadar ha ka 20 tarik April, 1904 ban register. Ki Wahadadar ruh ki kohnguh bad la register ia ka katkum ka Register No. 15 jong ka snem 1904. la kane ka kular la i'ateh ha ka durbar 9 shnong ha Phali ha ka 18 tarik April, 1904, bad kata ka long kumne - “Ngi ki khyndai Shnong ki ban soi kyrteng harum la Yakut durbar lang ha Phali Bazar ba ngin Yathoh kane ka kular da kumne 1. la ki jingkieng naduh Shyrten haduh Hat Phali tang ia kiba dei hapoh Bakra bah, ngin shna hi ma ngi ki paitbah. 2. la ka Wah Bakra namar ban laid ki lieng soh yn shna ki 9 shnong bad kiwei naduh ka jaka U Soi shatei shaneng. Lada king mawshun Myntlang ki Shelia kin shna da kaba pynlut na ka khajna mawshun naduh kane ka jaka U Soi haduh khap ri dkhar. 3. la ki khyndew kiba dei ki Seng ne ri khorit kiba don ha la ki shnong ki shnong ne ha kiwei ki shnong kiba ia dei lang hapoh khyndai shnong llaka Shelia, katkum ka rukom barim, kata kan long ka jong ki trai seng ne trai khoritdar bad ka jingmth myntoi baroh kin Yoh hi kita ki trai. U bym kit apot urn lah ban Yoh bynta. 4. Kino kino ki ban die ia la ka bynta kirn lah ban die habar llaka Sheila. 5. la ki hok ki paitbah na kano kano ka shnong ki Wadar kirn lah ban die, aiwai ne ai bondobos hano hano khlem da ai ki trai seng ne trai khoritdar hi. 157 6. Ki dkhar die khaw ki dei ban wan lang man ka hat kat kiba kwah. 7. Ki dkhar thied tympew kin wan man ka hat kat kiba kwah bad kin thied ruh na dang shai. la ki paragraph Nos. 6 & 7 ki Wahadadar ki dei ban jari notis shisien shi bnai. 8. la ka lieng Khewa ki Wahadadar ki dei ban da dok bad ban -nym shah ban kiew bun briew ba Toh ngam. U bai khewa dei ban siew shi peisa uwei u briew shisien kiew lieng. 9. la ki pyrha die khaw, ki mawser, ki maloi thew umphniang, ki Kot die jaifi; ki Wahadadar ki dei ban khmih shisien shibnai. la kane ka kular la pyniasoh lang bad ka kular dt. 30.1. 1 865 & dt.25.4. 1874 jong ki khadar bad ki khyndai shnong. Ka kular dt. 30 Jan. 1865 ka kren kumne shaphang ki hat ki i'ew 12 shnong, ka Sheila Confederacy: "Ka Hat Pdia bad ka dan soh ngi baroh 12 shnong ngi ia mynjur ryngkat ban ai ha kino kino kiba ngin pynlong Wadar ba kin bam namar ba ki korbar na ka bynta jongngi. Ka dan soh ruh ka long 12 kai na kawei kawei ka lieng, tang ka dustur ki shim 12 tyngka ha la ka snem ka snem.” Kane ka kular ka mih na ka dorkhas ki Nongwar bad ki Nongtrai kaba ki phah ha U Major H. I. Bivar, Deputy Commissioner: kaba pyni ia ka dustur ki 12 shnong: ia kaba la pynskhem kum ka kular da utei U Deputy Commis- sioner. Katba ka Kular 25 tarik, April, 1874 pat ka kren kyllum tang shaphang ka synshar ka bishar jong ka Hima Sheila kaba ia dei khamtam hapdeng ki Wadar bad ki Sande. Kajingbishar kaba bniah ka pynpaw ba ka durbar Sande ka long ka khlieh synshar bishar ha la ki shnong ki shnong bad ka durbar 158 Duwakdar ka long ka appealate court bad ka durbar Hima ka long ka khlieh duh jong ka synshar bishar. Namar ka Hat Phali ka long ka hat ba khrawtam, ba riewspah tam bad ba pynmih bun eh ka khajna ka musul: ka kylla long ka hat ba bun eh ki mokotduma bad ki jingTa knieh longtrai; bad ki 12 shnong ki bat triang ia la ka hok, Nyngkong eh ki Nongbah ki pyrshang ban kam trai ia ka hynrei kim Toh nongkyrshan ha ka durbar Hima lait noh tang ki Mawrap bad ki Nonglyngkien. Ba kumta baroh laishnong ki ia sylla ban mih noh na ka Hima sheila bad rung kum ki shnong Sorkar hapoh ka jingpynTaid Sirdar ha ka snem 1 865, hynrei kim pyllait pat ia ka jingTalong trai lang halor ka hat Phali bad ka Hat Sheila ryngkat bad ki 9 shnong ka Hima Shelia, ba kim i don lad ban thaw Tew pat la ka jong harud ka Bakra Sheila. Ha ka snem 1871 ki Nongbah ki ai mokotduma pyrshah ia ka Hima Sheila da kaba ki kam trai ia ka hat Phali. Ha ka jingbishar U Deputy Commissioner dt. 4.3. 1 871 U Deputy Commissioner u ai kane ka rai - “It is clear to me that the Nongbah People have no exclusive right to the Phali Bazar. The evidence given by U Bot, the Sirdar of Nongbah itself proved that the inhabitants of Nongbah have not even any exclusive right to the land in which the Bazar stands and to call other witnesses is utterly unecessary. It has been shown by the evidence of the Sirdar Tynrong (Mawrap) and Nonglyngkien that though they seceeded from the confederacy of the 12 villages they were not called upon to pay any tax or as it could appear to give up the right which vest the other villages they held in the Bazar. I cannot think it to be right that the Nongbah people simply because they have come under British rule should make 159 use of the accident of a Bazar being in their immediate neighbourhood to levy a tax on it which has certainly never before been levied since the bazar was established now many generations ago. The Nongbah Sirdar and the People are therfore surely strictly prohibited from levy any such tax or toll as they have endeavoured to impose on the inhabitants of the twelve villages. All parties concerned will be held strictly re- sponsibly for any breach of peace.” Hynrei U Sirdar bad krpaitbah Nongbah kim hun wat ia kane ka rai ruh bad ki pyrshang ban thaw shi thaw mokotduma. Ha ka snem 1881 u Botsing ula pyrshang ban shim khajna jubor ha hat Phali. Ki Wadar bad ki 9 shnong kim shah. Ban nym mih kano kano ka jingiakular U D. C ula phah ia u Police Inspector ban tohkit bad la sabut ba ka Hat Phali ka long ka jong ki 12 shnong ka Hima Sheila bad la adong shisyndon ia U Sirdar Nongbah ban shim khajna. La bishar kut ia ka case dt. 12.3.83 da U Jeebon Roy, Extra-Commissioner ha ka 12:3.1892. Jingbishar “ the documents filed in the case by both parties it appears that the Plaintiffs first attempt was that he with the people of Nongbah jointly petitioned on the 1 st February, 1871 to the Deputy Commissioner for order to keep the place while they were levying tolls from Hat Phali and from levying any toll and an appeal against the Deputy Commissioner order was made to the Agent Governor General which was dismissed. Second’s attempt was in that he made a representation to the Deputy Commissioner on the 24 m December, 1872 de- signing to know what his jurisdiction was in case quarrels and 160 such like matters which occured in Phali Bazar i.e., whether he would decide and dispose of such quarrels. The Deputy Commissioner passed order on it to effect that as village au- thority he should only deal according to rule with ease which take place among the people of Nongbah and in that other cases parties should bring their grievances to the notice of the Deputy Commissioner. The Plaintiffs third attempt was in rep- resenting on the 8 lh November, 1881 by petition to the Deputy Commissioner that he was going to levy Bazar dues only from the native of the plains. He requested the Deputy Commis- sioner to depute a constable to keep the peace. An going was made by Cherra Sub-Inspector, whose report was approved of and the Sirdar was prohibited to levy any tool. After all these unsuccessful attempts he now comes to the Civil Court and produced five withnesses to prove his claim over the land in dispute. The witnesses for plaintiff asserted that the land in dis- pute was allotted to himself since 6 years ago by the members of his family or clans and since then he has grown some oranges there on a portion where there is a good soil and this is a market called Hat Phali which was established by the people and which is still in existence within the land in dispute. Every one has the right to go to the market without paying any dues to any one. The land is divided into two portions separately by a footpath from the good soil and that there is rough ground when no trees can be grown. From the arguments of both parties before me it appears that the defendants have no desire to claim or disturb or has claimed or disturb anyone ‘s right over the upper part of 161 the land where the orange and jack fruit are growing but they hold a general right over the lower part of it. The defendants abducted five withnesses to prove their case; who asserted that the land on which that Phali Bazar is held is a piece of rough ground situated on the bank of Bakra river and that nothing can be grown on it. I therefore consider it to be the best thing to inspect the ground when opportunity allows dur- ing the last winter. I requested Officiating A/r Heath who went down to Sheila in connection with some other matter to in- spect the place. Mr. Heath’s Inspection Memo is filed with the case from which it would appear clearly that the land in dis- pute is divided into two portions (parcels) that the open half way from the river was a jungle in which few source of orange and jackfruit trees grow and lower half bordering on the river was rough ground covered with huge builders. It was on this lower half the bazar was held. There were no trees on this part which could be damaged. Under this circumstances it appear quite clear that no one has disturbed the plaintiff from posses- sion of the upper part. It appears from the evidence produced by both parties that the Phali Bazar had been in existance for generations and no one has any exclusive right over it in any way. Accordingly the court dismisses the case with cost. La katta ruh U Botsing Sirdar bad ki paitbah Nongbah kim hun satia bad ki tei ki rai bad ha ka snem 1898 ki ujor pyrshah ia ki 12 shnong da kaba pynTeng fila ba ka Hat Phali ka dei ka jong U Skot, U Anai, U Syma: kiba long ki kpa tyrnmen jong ki Nongbah, ba kumta ki don hok ban shim khajha na ki nongwan hat namar ba ka Hat Phali ka don hapoh ka Hinria jong ki. 162 Ha ka jingVasaid la sabut ba ki khun ki ksiew jong kitei ki tymmen ki don ym tang ha Nongbah hynrei kila saphret ha baroh ki 12 shnong ka Shelia Confederacy. Ki Nongbah namar kata, kim don hok ban kam trai ba tang ma ki kiba long ki khun ki warisjong kitei ki tymmen bad ba ka Hat Phali ka dei ka jong ki. Nalor kata, ki Nongbah hi kila long shisien ka bynta jong ka hima ki 12 shnong bad naduh hyndai hynthai la pynskhem ia ka Hat Phali kum ka Hat ki 12 shnong. Ki bor synshar ba halor ki maham ia u Sirdar bad ki paitbah Nongbah ba kim bit shuh hadien kane ban thaw jingi'akajia halor ka Hat Phali. Khasi - Jaintia Hills ha ka 8.3.1919; kaba kren kumne - Political Case No. 53 of 1916 Ka Jingbishar Ki Nongmudui bad Nongapil kila buh ka dorkhas ha ka 22.12.1914 ha Kashari ki Wadar Shelia pyrshah ia ki Nongshah mudui bad shah apil kum ki Nongmihkhmat jong ka Durbar Hat Phali, namar kila shim noh Rs. 40/- (Sawphew tyngka) kaba long ka khrong ne ka jingToh kaba mih ha ki por tlang jong ki snem 1913-14 na ki Ghat lieng kiba ha Mawsaw bad 163 Sohmanir kiba dei hapoh ka llaka jong ka shnong Nongtrai bad ha kata ka liang jong ka Wah Sheila kaba dei sha ka liang ka shnong Nongtrai bad ba ki pynleit ruh ia kita ki tyngka ha ki jingi'oh (nejingpynlang tyngka) kiba mih na ka Hat Phali kaba dei hapoh ka llaka Nongbah, bad kaba ki ia phla ba ym don ka jingi'asoh (ne jingiadei) ei ei bad kine ki Ghat lieng ba ki ia mudui. Ki phla ruh ba ia ka jingi'oh ba ki i'oh na kine ki Ghat lieng artylli la ju shim tang da ki Nongtrai hi. Ki shahmudui bad shahapil kila mynjur ba kila lum ia kane ka Rs. 40/- kaba long ka jingi'oh myntoi ba la i'oh na kine ki artylli ki Ghat kaba kila lum da kaba buh u musul 2 anna shispah bhar u sohfiiamtra katkum ba la aibor da ka durbar Hat Phali. Ha kata ka durbar hi ruh ki Nongtrai ki don (naba ka Hat Phali ka long ka spah ba ia dei lang ia ki 23 shnong ryngkat bad ka Nongtrai de), bad ia kane ka musul la pyndonkam ban phuid ne shan ia ka Wah Bakra (Sheila) bad thaw jingkieng de. la kane ka jingi'oh jingmyntoi la pynlong ha ka jingi'oh na ka Hat Phali naba kine ki artylli ki Ghat lieng kila long ka bynta Ka Hat Phali naduh barim bajah. Ki ai fiia ruh ba kine ki artylli ki Ghat lieng kirn shym la don ki bynta ba kyrpang jong ki Nongtrai hi; kiba ym ju don kano kano ka Hat ne Ghat lieng la ka jong ha ki rud jong ka wah Shelia, hynrei tang ka Hat Phali bad ka Ghat lieng jong ka ka lah ban long bad don hok ruh ban pynlong ha kano kano ka liang jong kata ka wah. Ki ong ruh ba kat ki hukum jong ki bun ki Deputy Commissioner ym lah thaw hat ne pynmih Ghat lieng thymmai hajan ki hat ne ki Ghat lieng rim. Da ka jingbishar jong ki (ki Wadar) kaba dt.14.3.1918 ki Wadar kila kyntait ia ka dorkhas ki Nongapil da kaba pynsiew 164 ia ka jingiut bad mynta pyrshah ia kane ka jingbishar la buh ia kane ka apil kaba mynta. Ka jingiakajia ba shisha ka long la kine ki Ghat lieng Mawsaw bad Sohmanir ki long ne kynthup ne em kum ka bynta jong ka Hat Phali kumba la ai nia da ki shahmudui ne ki long kiba kyrpang na ka Hat Phali kumba la batai ne phla da ki nongapil. Mynta ka paw ba ki Nongtrai kila buh ka jingmudui ha ka 1902 pyrshah ia ki katto katne ki nongpawkhmat jong ka durbar Hat Phali namar ba kila shim musul bor na kaba ki Nongtrai ki khot ka “Ghat lieng Phali na kaba ki ia pynmih ia ki sohfiiamtra” la kane ka mokotduma la pyniasuk da ka Rojinoma kaba 2 tarik December, 1904, bad baroh arliang ha kane ka mokotduma ki ia saitnia ba kane ka Rajinoma ka kyrshan mar ia la ka jong ka jong ka liang. Kat ka bynta na ka Rajinoma kaba ki nongapil bad ki shahapil ki ia shaniah ka long kumne- “Ba kumba ka Ghat lieng Phali ka long barabor ha ki baroh arliang jong ka wah naduh hyndai hynthai, kumta ngi naduh kane ka sngi ngin ym lah shuh ban ia kajia, wat lada la pynlong ia ka ha kano kano ka liang ne ha baroh arliang jong ka wah”. Mynta ki nongapil ki phla ne batai ba ki Ghat lieng Mawsaw bad Sohmanir ki long kl bynta jong ka Hat Phali bad kirn shym la pyrshang ban batai kaei ka kyrteng jong ka Ghat lieng Phali jong kiba la kdew ha ka Mokotduma jong ka snem 1 902 lane ka jngai katno na Mawsaw bad Sohmanir. la kine ki bynta kiba ki Nongtrai ki donkam ki shu sngap sian na ki daw kiba shai. La kumno kumno, kila phla ba ki Ghat lieng Mawsaw bad Sohmanir ki don ha ka rud jong ka Wah Sheila kaba marpyrshah ka Kato Shyiapjong ka Mawryngkhong, kaba hapoh ka jingda ka Shelia. 165 Hynrei kane ka jingbatai ka long kaba lamler nadong shadong naba ka khyndew kaba marpyrshah ia ka Kato Shyiap ka long ka Lba kaba hapoh ki khyndew jong ka shnong Sheila bad ka bym dei satia hapoh ka llaka Nongtrai. Kat kine ki nia, ka shai ba ka Ghat lieng Phali jong ki Nongtrai ba la kdew ha ka Mokotdumajong ka snem 1902 ka ia del bad kita ki Ghat lieng Mawsaw bad Sohmanir kumba la sei nia ki shahmudui bad ba la rai da ki Wadar. Khamtam kumba la report ki Wadar ba kine ki artylli ki ghat lieng ki long tang kumba 220 kot sharum ka hat Phali. Nalor kata, ba ha ka mokotduma jong ka snem 1902 ki Nongtrai kila ong ba ka Ghat lieng Phali kaba long ha kata ka liang jong ka Wah Shelia kaba dei sha ka iiang Nongtrai ka dei ka jaka thung soh jong ki. Kumta, lada ki ghat lieng Mawsaw bad Sohmanir kiba long ha syndah ka Hat Phali, kirn kynthup shiteng shiliang ne nadong hadong kata ka Ghat lieng Phali jong ki; ka shai ba ki Nongtrai kila don palat ban ia kawei ka jaka kynshew ia ki soh jong ki. Hynrei ka Nongtrai ka long ka shnong kaba rit bad ka long ka bymthikna ba ki Nongtrai ki lah ban don palat ban ia kawei ka jaka kynshew bad die soh jong ki. Ka long kaba shisha ba ki Nongtrai kila kit la ki sohftiamtra ha Mawsaw bad Sohmanir kiba harud jong ka Wah Shelia naduh hyndai na ka bynta ban die bad shalan sha ri dkhar bad ba ka Hat Phali ruh bad la ki ghat lieng ha ki baroh arliang jong ka juh ka wah kila don naduh hyndai hynthai. Hynrei ha ka jingpyrkhat jongnga ka long ka bymlah pyrkhat ba ki ghat lieng Mawsaw bad Sohmanir, ba ki da long kiba marsyndah bad ka Hat Phali bad ki don ha kajuh ka lynti nur kaba dei ban shna barabor, ba kin long kiba kyrpang na ki ghat lieng jong ka Hat Phali naduh hyndai hynthai khlem da long ruh ha kajuh ka por ka daw jong 166 ki jingTaleh bad ki jingTamudui. Nalor kata, lada kine ki artylli ki ghat lieng kila long shisha kiba kyrpang nadong shadong na ka Hat Phali, ki Nongtrai kin nym long ki nongToh bynta lem ha ka Hat Phali ha ka juh ka liang jong ka Wah namar haba ki ia jan katne katne ia kine ki ghat lieng yn pynduh noh da ka Hat Phali bad ka jingiateh jong ki da ka Raginoma kan mut kumjuh kumba kflia (ne pynduh noh) ia la ki ghat lieng jong la ka shnong na ka bynta ka Hat Phali ha kaba ia dei lang ha kaba ym tang ki briew jong ka Hima Sheila, hynrei ki raiot sorkar bad Sohra de ki ia Toh myntoi lang. Ba ka da long kumne ngam lah khlem da mynjur ia ka jingshem bad rai ki Wadar ba ki ong ba ki Kato Mawsaw bad ki Sohmanir ki long ki bynta ba ia dei lang jong ka Hat Phali bad ha ka Rajinoma kaba 2 tarik December, 1904 ruh ka mut ia ki. Don sa kawei pat ka Agreement jong ka snem 1904 ha kaba la ia kut ba ia ka Wah Sheila naduh Usoi shaneng yn phuid ne shna da ki 1 1 shnong bad kiwei baroh long 23 shnong, haba kheifi lem bad ia ki Nongtrai de kiba wanlam ia ki soh ban die ha ka Hat Phali (kaba la khot ka Hat jong ki 23 shnong) khnang ban lait ka lynti raid lieng ki nongkhall soh. Mynba lada dei ba don maw pat myntlang ia ka Wah naduh Usoi arsut yn phuid ne shna da ki Shelia bad ia ka jinglut la siew na u khajna Mawshun. Haba ki teh ia lade ban shna ia ka Wah naduh Usoi (kaba long jngai na Kato Shyiap) haduh Phali, ki 1 1 shnong ki leh khlem artatien na ka bynta ka jingmyntoi ka Hat Phali. Ka shai namar kata, ba lada ki Nongtrai kila don (kumba ki phla hi) ka jingmyntoi ba kyrpang ha Mawsaw bad Sohmanir, ka bym ia dei bad ki jingmyntoi ka Hat Phali hynrei kaba syriem bad kato ka jong ki Sheila, kila dei ban long ka liang kaba lai ha 167 kane kajingt'ateh agreement kumba ki Shelia kila long ka Hang kabaar. Ha kaba khatduh ka jingkdewjong ki nongapil la ki Kato Shyiap bad Kato Mustoh ban kyrshan ia la ki jingdawa ka long ka bym ia dei (ne bym shai). Ki tei ki long tang ki Kato ban kyntiew bad pynhiar ia ki soh na ki katto katne ki bri soh jong ki Sheila, Mustoh, Nongbah bad kiwei pat ki nongrit ki bym lah leit kit sha Hat Phali bad ia ki Shelia la shah ban lum khyndiat u musul bad ia kine ki Kato la shah ban leh kumta lada ki shna bha bad pynkhuid ia ki lynti ki ban poi sha ki. la ki soh jong ki Nongtrai la kumno kumno lah ban pynkit ha Hat Phali: bad dei na ka bynta ka jingbit jong ki kumjuh kumba na ka bynta ka jingbit jong ki briew na kiwei pat ki shnong kiba shong ha kajuh ka liang jong ka Wah Shelia. La ju pynlong hat teng teng (kata ia ka Hat Phali) ha ka iiang jong ka shnong Nongtrai bad na ka bynta ban pynlong hat kumta la dei ban don ka Kato ne ki Kato ha kata ka liang na ka bynta ki dkhar ban wan pynkit soh ha ki lieng. Hynrei lada ki Nongtrai ki kwah ban dawa (ne kam ia ki Kato Mawsaw bad Sohmanir) kum ki Kato la ki jong bad kiba dei na ka bynta ka jingmyntoi jong ki hi bad kiba kyrpang nadong shadong na ka Hat Phali bad ki Kato jong ka, te ka hukum u Deputy Commissioner kaba 1 7 tarik January , 1 904 (shaphang ka Hat Mawdon) kim ia dei. Kata, la ki Kato Mawsaw bad Sohmanir dei ban pynduh noh. Namar, lada ki long ha kata ka rukom (ba la batai ki Nongtrai) ki long ki Kato thymmai kiba ia tur pyrshah bad pynjot ia ka Hat Phali ba la seng naduh barim bajah. Namar kine ki daw baroh, nga pynskhem ia ka hukum jong ki Wahadadar kaba dt. 14 tarik, March, 1918 bad kyntait 168 noh ia kane ka apil, kata, naba nga kheift ia ki Kato Mawsaw bad Sohmanir ba ki long khlem artatien ki byta jong ka Hat Phali. U G.E. loanes, Deputy Commissioner, ha ka jingbishar jong u dt. 3.1.1922 ula ai kane ka hukum- “Ym don sakhi ban pynshisha ne kyrshan ia ka jingTaleh mokotduma ba ka Phali ka la long naduh ba sdang ka jong ki 23 shnong. Hynrei da khongpong ki kot barim tarn ba la sei- kata ki hukum jong ka snem 1871 bad jong ka 1873 ki kdew shai ba ka Hat Phali ka dei ka jong ki 12 shnong Haba da kumwei ka long kaba shai kdar na ki kot ki sla ba la suh lang bad na ki jingphla sakhi hakhmatjongnga na ki nongmihkhmat jong ki 12 shnong ba naduh u Jumai (1897) ia kiwei pat ki shnong la shah ban ia shim bynta lem ha ka jingpynTaid ia ka Hat. Ka daw jong kane ka jingshah ka long namar ba donkam ban Toh ia ka jingTarap jong ki ban pynkhuid (phuid) ia ki khriang bad shna la ki lynti ki ban poi sha ka Hat. Dang donkam shuh ban pynneh ia kata ka kam bad na ka bynta ban Toh ia ka jingTatrei lang jong kiwei pat ki shnong ba maijan ha ka 1901 la thaw ia ka Agreement ba dei ban buh ka kynja musul (jingsiew) na u soh uba die ha Hat bad ba katto katne na kaba mih dei ban ai ha ki dolar bad katto katne ha ki trai hat. Ym don shuh kiwei ki khrong ne kino kino ki jingmih. la kane ka Agreement jong ka snem 1901 kaba la kynthup ruh ia ki jingpynbeit ia ki por ban die soh bad la don da ki jingthoh ia ki kuna ia ki jingleh palat ia ki hukum jong ka jingpynl'aid. La shem sabut ruh na ki sakhi ba da ki kot ki sla ba ia kaba tarn na ka tyngka jong ka Hat la sam ne ai ha ki nongmihkhmat ym tang na ki jong ki 1 2 shnong, hynrei na kito kiba shabar ruh. la kane la mynjur da ki nongmihkhmat jong ki 1 2 shnong. la kane kaba ki khot ka kot jingkheih jingdiah, ne kot thoh ia ki jingiakut durbar la buh da ka jingi'atyrwa kaba ki nongmihkhmat jong kiwei pat ki shnong ruh kila soi bad man la ka snem ia ki jingtyrwa ba la thoh ha ka bui durbar kiba pyni ia ki tyngka ba tarn jong ka snem bad ia ka jingiasam la ju soi da ki katto katne ki nongmihkhmat jong kine ki shnong kumjuh kumba da ki nongmihkhmatjong ki 12 shnong ruh. Haba ka tyngka kaba tarn ka bun katto katne na kata la aiti ha ka jingsumar jong ki nongmihkhmatjong kiwei pat ki shnong. Kam shai na kine ki kot ki sla na ka bynta aTu ia kane ka tyngka la i'asam kumta; hynrei, la ka long na ka bynta kano kano ka daw, ym lah don jingartatien ba ia ki nongmihkhmat jong kiwei pat ki shnong la ju shah la bun snem ban ia trei tista ha kaba pynYaid ia ka Hat khamtam ha kaba ia dei ha kaba shim bad pynlut ia ka jingmih kaba la khot ‘U Musapha”. Kane ka long kaba ia dei ne i shongnia, naba U Musapha um long u khrong hat ba ju long, 170 hynrei uba la da buh khnang ban pynbiang ia ka jinglut ha kaba shna ia ki lynti syngkieng ki ban poi ha hat bad ba ia kane ka kam dei ban pyndep ne trei da kiwej pat ki shnong kumjuh kumba da ki 12 shnong kiba don ka hok ka jinglongtrai ha ka Hat. Ka jingshah ia kiwei pat ki shnong ban ia shim bynta ha kaba pyni'aid ia kine ki jingthmu ka long kaba hok bad kaba biang. Ka la ju long ruh la bun snem bad kaba dei ban pynneh”.
